## word: apple
- uk: /ˈæpl/
- us: /ˈæpl/
- synonyms: malus domestica || 家苹果（学名） ;; crab apple || 沙果，野苹果 ;; dessert apple || 鲜食苹果 ;; cooking apple || 烹调用苹果 ;;
- antonyms: <无匹配直接反义词> || <无> ;;
- phrases: apple juice || 苹果汁 ;; apple pie || 苹果派 ;; apple cider || 苹果酒，苹果汁 ;; apple tree || 苹果树 ;; apple vinegar || 苹果醋 ;;
- collocations: ripe apple || 成熟的苹果 ;; rotten apple || 烂苹果 ;; crisp apple || 脆甜的苹果 ;; peel an apple || 削苹果 ;; bake an apple || 烤苹果 ;;
- sentencePatterns: An apple a day keeps the doctor away. || 谚语类固定句型，意为“一天一苹果，医生远离我” ;; Would you like an apple? || 用于询问对方是否想要苹果的日常交际句型 ;; The apple tastes + adj. || 用于描述苹果口感的主系表句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: How about an apple? || 来个苹果怎么样？ ;; That apple is so juicy! || 那个苹果汁水真足！ ;; Could you pass me that apple? || 你能把那个苹果递给我吗？ ;;
- idioms: the apple of sb's eye || 某人的掌上明珠，心肝宝贝 ;; upset the apple cart || 打乱计划，搞砸事情 ;; rotten apple (in the barrel) || 害群之马，团队里的不良分子 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 苹果 ;; 苹果树 ;;
- definitionZh: 一种常见的圆形或椭圆形水果，表皮多为红色、绿色或黄色，果肉脆甜多汁，营养丰富 ;; 结出苹果这种果实的落叶乔木，属于蔷薇科苹果属 ;;
- definitionEn: A common round or oval fruit with red, green or yellow skin and crisp sweet juicy flesh, rich in nutrition ;; A deciduous tree of the genus Malus in the rose family that bears this fruit ;;
- example: She bit into a crisp red apple and smiled. || 她咬了一口脆爽的红苹果，笑了起来。
- example: There are several apple trees planted in the backyard of our house. || 我们家后院种了好几棵苹果树。
- example: The recipe says we need two peeled apples to make this dessert. || 食谱上说做这份甜点我们需要两个削了皮的苹果。



## word: unique
- uk: /juˈniːk/
- us: /juˈniːk/
- synonyms: unparalleled || 无比的，无双的 ;; unmatched || 无可匹敌的 ;; one-of-a-kind || 独一无二的 ;; distinctive || 有特色的 ;; exceptional ||  exceptional，杰出的，异常的 ;;
- antonyms: common || 常见的，普通的 ;; ordinary || 普通的，平凡的 ;; generic || 通用的，无特色的 ;;
- phrases: unique feature || 独有特征 ;; unique opportunity || 难得的机会 ;; unique style || 独特风格 ;; unique experience || 独特经历 ;; unique selling point || 独特卖点 ;;
- collocations: absolutely unique || 绝对独特的 ;; rather unique || 相当特别的 ;; unique to... || 为…所特有 ;; uniquely qualified || 完全有资格的 ;; unique identifier || 唯一标识符 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sth is unique to + 特定群体/区域 || 表示某物是某个群体、地区等独有的 ;; It is unique that + 从句 || 用于描述某种情况十分少见 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That's so unique! || 这也太特别了！ ;; Each person is unique in their own way. || 每个人都有自己的独特之处 ;; This is a once-in-a-lifetime unique chance. || 这是个千载难逢的难得机会 ;;
- idioms: one and only || 绝无仅有的，唯一的 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 唯一的 ;; 独一无二的 ;; 独特的 ;; 罕见的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指某事物是仅此一个、没有相同的或可以相比的；也可形容人或事物有与众不同的特点 ;; 非正式语境中可表示十分少见、难得的 ;;
- definitionEn: being the only one of its kind; unlike anything else ;; (informal) very special or unusual ;;
- example: Each person's fingerprints are unique to them. || 每个人的指纹都是独属于自己的。
- example: The region has a unique culture that has been preserved for hundreds of years. || 这个地区有着传承了数百年的独特文化。
- example: This is a unique opportunity for you to meet the top experts in the field. || 这对你来说是个能见到该领域顶尖专家的难得机会。

## word: crab apple
- uk: /ˈkræb æpl/
- us: /ˈkræb æpl/
- synonyms: wild apple || 野苹果 ;; sour apple || 酸苹果 ;; crab || 山楂果，沙果（俗称） ;;
- antonyms: sweet apple || 甜苹果 ;; cultivated apple || 栽培苹果 ;;
- phrases: crab apple jelly || 海棠果果冻 ;; flowering crab apple || 垂丝海棠，花海棠 ;; crab apple tree || 海棠树，沙果树 ;; sour crab apple || 酸海棠果 ;;
- collocations: pick crab apples || 采摘海棠果 ;; make crab apple jam || 制作海棠果酱 ;; ornamental crab apple || 观赏海棠 ;; ripe crab apple || 成熟的海棠果 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Crab apple is often used to make + [food product] || 说明：用于表述海棠果的加工用途，主语为crab apple，后接被动结构说明其制作的食品 ;; The + [adjective] crab apple tree produces + [quantity/type of fruit] every year || 说明：用于描述海棠树的结果情况，可在crab apple tree前加修饰词，后接产量或果实类型的表述 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That crab apple is so sour it makes my face pucker! || 那海棠果酸得我脸都皱起来了！ ;; These crab apple jellies taste way better than I thought! || 这些海棠果冻比我想象的好吃多了！ ;; The crab apple tree in the yard is blooming so pretty this spring! || 院子里的海棠树今年春天开得可好看了！ ;;
- idioms: (as) sour as a crab apple || 像海棠果一样酸，形容人尖酸刻薄 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 海棠果 ;; 沙果 ;; 野山楂（部分地区俗称） ;; 海棠树 ;;
- definitionZh: 蔷薇科苹果属的小型野生或栽培果树的果实，通常味酸，可用于制作果酱、果冻等，也可指该种果树 ;; 比喻性格尖酸刻薄的人 ;;
- definitionEn: A small, sour fruit from a type of small apple tree (genus Malus), often used to make jams, jellies, and preserves; also refers to the tree itself that bears this fruit ;; Informally, a person who has a bitter, bad-tempered personality. ;;
- example: My grandma always makes a jar of crab apple jam every autumn. || 我奶奶每年秋天都会做一罐海棠果酱。
- example: The flowering crab apple along the street has become a popular spot for people to take photos in spring. || 街边的开花海棠树春天成了大家拍照的热门地点。
- example: Don't be such a crab apple — we're just teasing you a little, there's no need to get mad. || 别那么尖酸好不好，我们就是逗逗你，没必要生气。

## word: dessert apple
- uk: /dɪˈzɜːt ˌæpl/
- us: /dɪˈzɜːrt ˌæpl/
- synonyms: eating apple || 鲜食苹果 ;; dessert cultivar apple || 鲜食品种苹果 ;; table apple || 餐用苹果 ;; sweet apple || 甜苹果 ;;
- antonyms: cooking apple || 烹饪苹果 ;; cider apple || 酿酒苹果 ;;
- phrases: crisp dessert apple || 脆甜鲜食苹果 ;; organic dessert apple || 有机鲜食苹果 ;; seasonal dessert apple || 当季鲜食苹果 ;; imported dessert apple || 进口鲜食苹果 ;;
- collocations: grow dessert apples || 种植鲜食苹果 ;; pick dessert apples || 采摘鲜食苹果 ;; sell dessert apples || 售卖鲜食苹果 ;; taste a dessert apple || 品尝鲜食苹果 ;;
- sentencePatterns: ... is a popular variety of dessert apple || 用于说明某品种属于常见的鲜食苹果类型 ;; Would you like a dessert apple as a snack? || 用于询问对方是否想要鲜食苹果作为零食 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Grab a dessert apple if you're hungry. || 饿的话就拿个鲜食苹果吃。 ;; This dessert apple is super juicy! || 这个鲜食苹果超多汁！ ;;
- idioms: the apple of one's eye || 掌上明珠，挚爱 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 鲜食苹果 ;; 餐后甜点苹果 ;;
- definitionZh: 适合直接生吃的甜苹果品种，区别于用于烹饪、酿酒的酸苹果品种 ;; 可作为餐后甜点食用的甜苹果 ;;
- definitionEn: A type of sweet apple that is suitable for eating raw, as opposed to a cooking apple or cider apple which is more sour ;; A sweet apple that can be served as a light dessert after a meal ;;
- example: Honeycrisp is one of the most popular dessert apples on the market. || 蜜脆是市场上最受欢迎的鲜食苹果品种之一。
- example: My grandma planted several dessert apple trees in her backyard. || 我奶奶在她的后院种了几棵鲜食苹果树。
- example: We served each guest a dessert apple with a small piece of cheese after dinner. || 晚餐后我们给每位客人上了一个鲜食苹果，配一小块奶酪。

## word: malus domestica
- uk: /ˈmæləs dəʊˈmestɪkə/
- us: /ˈmæləs doʊˈmestɪkə/
- synonyms: apple tree || 苹果树 ;; cultivated apple || 栽培苹果 ;; domestic apple || 家苹果 ;;
- antonyms: wild crabapple || 野生海棠 ;; Malus sylvestris || 欧洲野苹果 ;;
- phrases: cultivated Malus domestica || 栽培苹果 ;; Malus domestica orchard || 苹果园 ;; nutrient composition of Malus domestica || 苹果营养成分 ;;
- collocations: Malus domestica cultivation || 苹果种植 ;; Malus domestica variety || 苹果品种 ;; Malus domestica fruit extract || 苹果果实提取物 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Malus domestica is + 名词短语 || 用于说明家苹果的类别、属性等 ;; + 动词 + Malus domestica + 状语 || 用于描述对家苹果开展的相关动作 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Malus domestica is just the scientific name for the common apple. || 家苹果就是普通苹果的学名啦。 ;; Oh, Malus domestica? You mean regular eating apples, right? || 哦，家苹果？你是说平时吃的那种苹果对吧？ ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 家苹果 ;; 苹果（学名，蔷薇科苹果属栽培种） ;;
- definitionZh: 蔷薇科苹果属的常见栽培果树物种，其结出的果实即日常食用的苹果，是全球温带地区广泛种植的经济果树。 ;; 植物分类学中对栽培苹果的标准学名称谓，区别于苹果属的野生近缘物种。 ;;
- definitionEn: A widely cultivated fruit tree species of the genus Malus in the Rosaceae family, whose edible fruit is the common apple, extensively grown in temperate regions worldwide as a commercial fruit crop. ;; The standard scientific taxonomic name for cultivated apples, differentiating them from wild related species in the Malus genus. ;;
- example: Malus domestica is one of the most economically important fruit crops grown across temperate zones. || 家苹果是温带地区种植的最具经济价值的果树作物之一。
- example: Researchers are studying the disease resistance genes of Malus domestica to reduce pesticide use in orchards. || 研究人员正在研究家苹果的抗病基因，以减少果园的农药使用量。
- example: Most of the apples sold in supermarkets are cultivars of Malus domestica, bred for flavor, texture and storage life. || 超市里售卖的大多数苹果都是家苹果的栽培品种，是为风味、口感和耐储性而培育的。

## word: able
- uk: /ˈeɪbl/
- us: /ˈeɪbl/
- synonyms: capable || 有能力的 ;; competent || 胜任的 ;; skilled || 熟练的 ;; talented || 有天赋的 ;; qualified || 合格的 ;;
- antonyms: unable || 不能的 ;; incapable || 无能力的 ;; incompetent || 不胜任的 ;;
- phrases: be able to do sth || 能够做某事 ;; be able to handle || 能够处理 ;; be able to afford || 负担得起 ;; be able to help || 能够帮忙 ;; be able to attend || 能够出席 ;;
- collocations: perfectly able || 完全有能力的 ;; financially able || 经济上有能力的 ;; physically able || 身体上有能力的 ;; able student || 优等生 ;; able leader || 有能力的领导者 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be able to + 动词原形 || 表示有能力或客观条件允许做某事 ;; will be able to + 动词原形 || 表示将来有能力或可以做某事 ;; have been able to + 动词原形 || 表示从过去到现在一直有能力完成某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'll be able to make it. || 我能赶到/我能做到。 ;; Are you able to help me out? || 你能帮我个忙吗？ ;; I haven't been able to reach her. || 我一直联系不上她。 ;;
- idioms: able-bodied || 体格健全的，强壮的 ;;

### sense: adj
- translationZh: 能够的；有能力的；能干的；
- definitionZh: 具备做某事所需的技能、知识或条件，可以完成某件事；形容人聪明、能力强，能高效完成任务。;; 描述某人具备完成特定行动的能力或客观条件允许完成某事。
- definitionEn: having the skill, knowledge, or necessary conditions to do something successfully; used to describe someone who is intelligent and very good at doing things. ;; used to say that it is possible for someone to do something, either because they have the ability or because the situation allows it.
- example: She is able to speak three foreign languages fluently. || 她能流利地说三门外语。
- example: We were able to finish the project ahead of schedule thanks to everyone's effort. || 多亏了大家的努力，我们得以提前完成这个项目。
- example: He is one of the most able managers in the whole company. || 他是整个公司里最能干的经理之一。



## word: capable
- uk: /ˈkeɪpəbl/
- us: /ˈkeɪpəbl/
- synonyms: competent || 有能力的，胜任的 ;; able || 能够的，有才干的 ;; proficient || 熟练的，精通的 ;; skilled || 熟练的，有技能的 ;; qualified || 合格的，有资质的 ;;
- antonyms: incapable || 无能力的，不能的 ;; incompetent || 不胜任的，无能的 ;; unqualified || 不合格的，无资格的 ;;
- phrases: capable of || 有能力做，能够做 ;; capable of handling || 有能力处理 ;; highly capable || 能力很强的 ;; technologically capable || 具备技术能力的 ;;
- collocations: capable person || 有能力的人 ;; capable team || 有战斗力的团队 ;; capable of achieving || 有能力实现 ;; capable performer || 表现出色的从业者 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb/sth be capable of (doing) sth || 表示“某人/某物有能力做某事”的基础句型 ;; It is + 形容词 + that sb is capable of sth || 用于表达对某人能力的评价的形式主语句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'm fully capable of it. || 我完全有能力搞定这件事。 ;; She's more capable than you think. || 她比你想的要能干得多。 ;; Is he capable of finishing this on time? || 他能按时完成这件事吗？ ;;
- idioms: capable of anything || 什么事都做得出来（尤指可能做坏事） ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 有能力的，有才干的 ;; 能干的，胜任的 ;;
- definitionZh: 具备完成某项任务、应对某种情况所需的技能、知识或素质的；有足够能力做某事的 ;;
- definitionEn: having the ability, skill, or qualities needed to do something successfully or deal with a situation effectively ;;
- example: A capable manager will always find ways to motivate his team. || 一位能干的经理总会找到激励团队的方法。
- example: This new software is capable of processing thousands of data entries in seconds. || 这款新软件能够在几秒钟内处理数千条数据条目。
- example: We all agree that she is the most capable candidate for the position. || 我们都认为她是这个职位最有能力的候选人。

## word: competent
- uk: /ˈkɒmpɪtənt/
- us: /ˈkɑːmpɪtənt/
- synonyms: capable || 有能力的 ;; qualified || 合格的 ;; proficient || 熟练的 ;; skilled || 有技能的 ;; able || 能干的 ;;
- antonyms: incompetent || 无能的 ;; unqualified || 不合格的 ;; inept || 笨拙的 ;;
- phrases: competent in || 在…方面有能力 ;; competent to do sth || 胜任做某事 ;; competent authority || 主管当局 ;; competent staff || 称职的员工 ;; competent performance || 合格的表现 ;;
- collocations: highly competent || 非常称职的 ;; technically competent || 技术上胜任的 ;; competent enough || 足够有能力的 ;; competent leader || 称职的领导 ;; competent work || 合格的工作 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be competent at sth || 表示“在某方面胜任” ;; be competent to do sth || 表示“有能力做某事” ;; It is competent for sb to do sth || 表示“某人做某事是符合职权的” ;;
- spokenExpressions: He's very competent at his job. || 他工作非常胜任。 ;; I'm not sure if she's competent enough for the role. || 我不确定她是否足够胜任这个职位。 ;; The team is full of competent people. || 这个团队里全是能干的人。 ;;
- idioms: competent to stand trial || （法律术语）有受审能力 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 有能力的 ;; 胜任的 ;; 称职的 ;; 合格的 ;;
- definitionZh: 具备足够的技能、知识或能力，能够胜任某项工作或任务的；符合特定要求或标准的；在法律上指有资格行使权力或承担责任的。 ;;
- definitionEn: having enough skill, knowledge, or ability to do something well or successfully; meeting the necessary standards or requirements; legally qualified or authorized to exercise a power or perform a duty. ;;
- example: She is a competent teacher who always prepares her lessons carefully. || 她是一位称职的老师，总是认真备课。
- example: To get this job, you need to be competent in both written and spoken English. || 要得到这份工作，你需要在英语读写和口语方面都具备胜任能力。
- example: The competent authorities have approved the construction project after a strict inspection. || 主管部门经过严格检查后批准了这个建筑项目。

### sense: adjective (legal)
- translationZh: 有法定资格的 ;; 有权能的 ;;
- definitionZh: 法律上具备行使某项权利、履行某项义务或参与特定法律程序的资格的。 ;;
- definitionEn: legally qualified or authorized to perform a particular act, exercise a right, or participate in a legal proceeding. ;;
- example: Only a competent court has the power to hear this type of case. || 只有具有管辖权的法院才有权力审理这类案件。
- example: The doctor confirmed that the patient was competent to make his own medical decisions. || 医生确认患者有能力自主作出医疗决定。
- example: The contract must be signed by a competent representative of the company to be valid. || 这份合同必须由公司的法定授权代表签署才有效。

## word: incapable
- uk: /ɪnˈkeɪpəbl/
- us: /ɪnˈkeɪpəbl/
- synonyms: unable || 不能的，无法的 ;; incompetent || 无能力的，不胜任的 ;; unfit || 不合适的，不胜任的 ;; powerless || 无权的，无力的 ;; inadequate || 不足的，不胜任的 ;;
- antonyms: capable || 有能力的，能干的 ;; competent || 胜任的，有能力的 ;; able || 能够的，有才干的 ;;
- phrases: incapable of || 不能，无法 ;; morally incapable || 道德上无能的 ;; technically incapable || 技术上不胜任的 ;; emotionally incapable || 情感上无能力的 ;; financially incapable || 无支付能力的 ;;
- collocations: incapable of doing sth || 无法做某事 ;; deem sb incapable || 认为某人无能 ;; prove incapable || 证明是不胜任的 ;; personally incapable || 个人能力不足的 ;; professionally incapable || 职业上不胜任的 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb + be + incapable of + doing sth || 表示某人没有能力做某事 ;; It + be + clear/obvious + that + sb + be + incapable of + sth || 表示某人明显在某方面无能 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'm incapable of keeping secrets. || 我根本守不住秘密。 ;; He's totally incapable of taking responsibility. || 他完全没能力承担责任。 ;; You're incapable of even listening to what I'm saying! || 你连听我说话都做不到！ ;;
- idioms: incapable of harming a fly || 连一只苍蝇都不忍心伤害，心地善良 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 没有能力的 ;; 不能的，无法的 ;; 不胜任的 ;;
- definitionZh: 缺乏做某事所需的技能、力量或素质的；无法完成某件事的；不具备承担某种职责或任务的资格的 ;;
- definitionEn: not having the ability, skill, or qualities needed to do something; not able to do a particular thing; not qualified or suitable for a particular role or task ;;
- example: He was incapable of dealing with the complex problem on his own. || 他没有能力独自处理这个复杂的问题。
- example: The manager was found to be incapable of leading the team to achieve the target. || 人们发现这位经理没有能力带领团队完成目标。
- example: She seems incapable of understanding how much her words hurt other people. || 她似乎没办法理解自己的话对别人造成了多大的伤害。

## word: skilled
- uk: /skɪld/
- us: /skɪld/
- synonyms: proficient || 精通的，熟练的 ;; expert || 专家的，内行的 ;; adept || 娴熟的，擅长的 ;; competent || 能干的，胜任的 ;; skillful || 灵巧的，有技巧的 ;;
- antonyms: unskilled || 不熟练的，无技能的 ;; incompetent || 无能的，不胜任的 ;; amateurish || 业余的，外行的 ;;
- phrases: skilled worker || 技术工人，熟练工 ;; skilled workforce || 技能劳动力 ;; skilled profession || 技术性职业 ;; skilled at / in sth || 擅长某事 ;;
- collocations: highly skilled || 高技能的，技艺精湛的 ;; skilled craftsman || 熟练工匠 ;; skilled labour || 技术劳动 ;; skilled negotiator || 娴熟的谈判者 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be skilled at / in (doing) sth || 表示“擅长（做）某事”，后接名词或动名词 ;; It is important for sb to be skilled in sth || 表示“对某人来说掌握某技能很重要”，用于强调技能的必要性 ;;
- spokenExpressions: You're really skilled at this! || 你这方面真的很厉害！ ;; We need someone skilled to handle this. || 我们需要个懂行的人来处理这个事。 ;; He's skilled enough to fix it. || 他手艺够好，能修好这个。 ;;
- idioms: be skilled in the art of sth || 深谙做某事的门道，精通做某事的技巧 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 有技能的 ;; 熟练的 ;; 技术性的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指经过训练或实践，具备完成某项工作或活动所需的专门知识、能力和经验的；也形容需要特定技能才能从事的工作等 ;; 指做事手法娴熟、技巧高超的 ;;
- definitionEn: having the special knowledge, ability, and experience that is needed to do something well ;; (of work) needing special skills to do ;;
- example: Many countries are facing a shortage of skilled workers in the manufacturing industry. || 许多国家正面临制造业技术工人短缺的问题。
- example: She is skilled at resolving conflicts between team members. || 她擅长化解团队成员之间的矛盾。
- example: Skilled jobs such as software development usually offer higher salaries. || 像软件开发这类技术性工作通常薪资更高。

## word: unable
- uk: /ʌnˈeɪbl/
- us: /ʌnˈeɪbl/
- synonyms: incapable || 不能的，无能力的 ;; unfit || 不合适的，不胜任的 ;; incompetent || 无能的，不称职的 ;; powerless || 无力的，无权的 ;;
- antonyms: able || 能够的，有能力的 ;; capable || 有能力的，胜任的 ;; competent || 能干的，称职的 ;;
- phrases: unable to do sth || 无法做某事 ;; financially unable || 经济上无力的 ;; physically unable || 身体上不能的 ;; mentally unable || 精神上无能力的 ;;

- sentencePatterns: be + unable + to + 动词原形 || 描述主语没有能力做某事的基础句型 ;; Because of + 名词短语, + sb + be + unable + to + 动词原形 || 说明导致无法做某事的原因的句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'm unable to make it. || 我来不了/我做不到。 ;; I'm afraid I'm unable to help. || 恐怕我帮不上忙。 ;; We're unable to offer you the position. || 我们无法给你提供这个职位。 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 不能的；无法的；无能力的 ;;
- definitionZh: 没有足够的能力、权力或机会去做某件事 ;; 因某种限制而无法完成特定动作或达成目标 ;;
- definitionEn: not having the necessary ability, power, or opportunity to do something ;; prevented from doing something by a particular restriction or limitation ;;
- example: Many people are unable to afford the rising cost of housing. || 很多人负担不起不断上涨的住房成本。
- example: He was unable to attend the meeting due to a sudden illness. || 他因为突发疾病无法出席会议。
- example: The little boy was unable to reach the top shelf even with a stool. || 即使踩着凳子，这个小男孩也够不到顶层的架子。

## word: about
- uk: /əˈbaʊt/
- us: /əˈbaʊt/
- synonyms: regarding || 关于 ;; concerning || 涉及，关于 ;; around || 大约，到处 ;; approximately || 大约 ;; roughly || 大致，差不多 ;;
- antonyms: exactly || 精确地 ;; precisely || 准确地 ;;
- phrases: talk about || 谈论，谈及 ;; think about || 考虑，思考 ;; worry about || 担心，担忧 ;; know about || 了解，知道 ;; care about || 关心，在意 ;;
- collocations: about time || 是时候了，早该 ;; about to do sth || 即将做某事 ;; what about || …怎么样 ;; how about || …如何 ;; all about || 全是关于，尽是 ;;
- sentencePatterns: What about + 名词/动名词? || 用于提出建议或询问相关情况 ;; be about to do sth || 表示即将要做某个动作 ;; It's about time + (that) 从句 || 表示某事早该发生了 ;;
- spokenExpressions: How about that? || 那可真不错啊！/ 你说怪不怪？ ;; What about you? || 你呢？ ;; That's about it. || 差不多就是这样了 ;;
- idioms: out and about || （病愈后）外出活动，四处走动 ;;

### sense: 介词
- translationZh: 关于 ;; 对于 ;; 涉及 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于引出谈论的主题或者涉及的对象 ;; 表示动作的对象或相关的范围 ;;
- definitionEn: used to introduce the subject that someone is talking or writing about ;; used to show what something relates to or involves ;;
- example: We are talking about our holiday plans. || 我们正在讨论我们的假期计划。
- example: She knows a lot about ancient history. || 她对古代历史了解很多。
- example: There's nothing new about this method. || 这个方法没有什么新鲜的地方。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 大约 ;; 大概 ;; 周围，四处 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示数量、时间等接近某个数值，不精确 ;; 表示在某个地方的附近到处活动 ;;
- definitionEn: used to say that a number, time etc is not exact ;; used to mean that someone is in or around a place, often moving around ;;
- example: The meeting will start at about three o'clock. || 会议将在三点左右开始。
- example: There were about 50 people at the party last night. || 昨晚的聚会上大约有50个人。
- example: He was walking about in the park when I saw him. || 我看到他的时候他正在公园里四处走动。



## word: around
- uk: /əˈraʊnd/
- us: /əˈraʊnd/
- synonyms: about || 大约，到处 ;; round || 围绕，环绕 ;; approximately || 大概，近似地 ;; throughout || 遍及，到处 ;; roughly || 大致，差不多 ;;
- antonyms: exactly || 精确地 ;; precisely || 准确地 ;;
- phrases: around the corner || 即将来临，在拐角处 ;; all around || 到处，四处 ;; get around || 四处走动，规避 ;; hang around || 闲逛，逗留 ;; travel around || 环游 ;;
- collocations: around 10 o'clock || 大约10点 ;; walk around the park || 在公园周边散步 ;; look around the house || 环视房子四周 ;; around the world || 全世界 ;; hang around with friends || 和朋友闲逛 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + around + 时间/数量 || 表示大约的时间或数量 ;; 动词 + around + 地点 || 表示在某地周围做某个动作 ;; It's + 描述词 + around + 地点 || 描述某地周边的情况 ;;
- spokenExpressions: What's around? || 附近有什么？ ;; Hang around a minute. || 稍等一会儿。 ;; I'll be around. || 我会在附近（随叫随到）。 ;;
- idioms: beat around the bush || 拐弯抹角，旁敲侧击 ;; have been around || 见过世面，经验丰富 ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 大约，大概 ;; 到处，四处 ;; 在周围，在附近 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于表示数量、时间等的粗略估计 ;; 表示到各个地方，没有固定方向 ;; 表示在某人或某物的周边区域 ;;
- definitionEn: used to show that a number, time, etc. is approximate ;; in or to many places, without a clear direction ;; in the area near someone or something ;;
- example: There are around 200 people in the hall. || 大厅里大约有200人。
- example: We walked around for hours looking for the café. || 我们四处走了好几个小时找那家咖啡馆。
- example: If you need help, I'll be around all afternoon. || 如果你需要帮忙，我整个下午都在附近。

### sense: 介词
- translationZh: 围绕，环绕 ;; 在……各处，遍及 ;; 绕过，避开 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示以某物为中心，在其四周 ;; 表示覆盖某个区域的各个部分 ;; 表示绕开某个障碍物或者不愿意面对的事物 ;;
- definitionEn: surrounding someone or something, with the person or thing in the centre ;; existing in all parts of a particular place ;; moving to the other side of something so that you avoid it ;;
- example: She put a scarf around her neck to keep warm. || 她在脖子上围了条围巾保暖。
- example: There are plenty of cafes around the campus. || 校园周边有很多咖啡馆。
- example: We had to drive around the flooded section of the road. || 我们不得不开车绕过被水淹没的那段路。

## word: concerning
- uk: /kənˈsɜːnɪŋ/
- us: /kənˈsɜːrnɪŋ/
- synonyms: regarding || 关于 ;; respecting || 关于，鉴于 ;; about || 关于 ;; touching || 关于，涉及 ;;
- antonyms: unrelated to || 与…无关 ;; unconnected with || 与…无关联 ;;
- phrases: concerning the matter || 关于这件事 ;; questions concerning || 关于…的问题 ;; concerning the future || 关于未来 ;; regulations concerning || 有关…的规定 ;;
- collocations: information concerning || 有关…的信息 ;; discussion concerning || 关于…的讨论 ;; concerns concerning || 关于…的担忧 ;; report concerning || 有关…的报告 ;; policy concerning || 有关…的政策 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There have been debates concerning + 名词/名词短语 || 该句型用于表达某事物引发了相关讨论 ;; We need to collect more data concerning + 名词/名词短语 || 该句型用于表达需要收集某相关事物的信息 ;; The company issued a statement concerning + 名词/名词短语 || 该句型用于表达主体发布了关于某事物的声明 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Concerning your question earlier || 关于你之前问的问题 ;; As far as that's concerning || 至于那件事 ;; Speaking of concerning issues || 说到相关的问题 ;;
- idioms: concerning oneself with || 忙于，关心 ;;

### sense: 介词
- translationZh: 关于 ;; 涉及 ;; 就…而言 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示所述内容与某事物相关、涉及某特定主题或情况 ;; 用于引出讨论、描述、行动等所指向的对象 ;;
- definitionEn: used to indicate the subject that something is related to or discusses ;; used to introduce the topic that a statement, action, etc. refers to ;;
- example: The police are investigating several issues concerning the case. || 警方正在调查与这起案件相关的若干问题。
- example: We received many inquiries concerning the new product launch. || 我们收到了很多关于新产品发布的咨询。
- example: There are strict rules concerning the use of office equipment. || 有涉及办公设备使用的严格规定。

### sense: 动词（concern的现在分词）
- translationZh: 涉及 ;; 让…担忧 ;; 关乎 ;;
- definitionZh: 作为动词concern的现在分词形式，表示“涉及、关联”或“使担忧、使挂念”的动作正在发生或作为定语、状语使用 ;;
- definitionEn: the present participle of the verb "concern", meaning to relate to something, or to make someone feel worried or anxious ;;
- example: The problem currently concerning most residents is the rising cost of living. || 目前让大多数居民担忧的问题是不断上涨的生活成本。
- example: The research concerning climate change has attracted global attention. || 这项关乎气候变化的研究已经引起了全球关注。
- example: The new policy, concerning small business subsidies, will take effect next month. || 这项涉及小企业补贴的新政策将于下月生效。

## word: exactly
- uk: /ɪɡˈzæktli/
- us: /ɪɡˈzæktli/
- synonyms: precisely || 精确地，准确地 ;; accurately || 准确无误地 ;; strictly || 严格地，确切地 ;; perfectly || 完全地，十足地 ;;
- antonyms: approximately || 大约，大概 ;; roughly || 粗略地，大致上 ;; vaguely || 模糊地，含糊地 ;;
- phrases: exactly right || 完全正确，恰到好处 ;; exactly the same || 一模一样，完全相同 ;; know exactly || 清楚知道，确切了解 ;; exactly what I need || 正是我需要的 ;;
- collocations: match exactly || 完全匹配 ;; follow exactly || 严格遵照 ;; fit exactly || 严丝合缝地适配 ;; remember exactly || 清楚记得 ;;
- sentencePatterns: exactly + 形容词/副词 || 用于加强形容词或副词的程度，表“完全，十足” ;; exactly + what/when/where/how 引导的从句 || 用于强调对具体信息的明确掌握 ;; That's exactly + 名词性成分/从句 || 用于表示完全认同对方的观点或描述 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Exactly! || 一点不错！说得对！ ;; Not exactly. || 不全是，不尽然 ;; Exactly what I thought. || 我就是这么想的 ;;
- idioms: exactly the ticket || 正合需要，正合适 ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 精确地，准确地 ;; 恰好，正好 ;; 完全地，全然 ;; （用于应答）一点不错，正是如此 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示完全符合事实、标准或预期，没有丝毫偏差 ;; 用于强调数量、时间、位置等完全吻合 ;; 用于回应时表示完全同意对方的说法 ;;
- definitionEn: used to emphasize that something is completely correct, accurate, or true without any mistake ;; used to say that a number, time, position etc is perfect and has no difference from what is needed ;; used as a reply to show that you completely agree with what someone has said ;;
- example: It's exactly 9 o'clock now, so we should start the meeting on time. || 现在正好9点，我们该准时开会了。
- example: That's exactly the reason why I decided to quit my former job. || 那正是我决定辞去之前那份工作的原因。
- example: — So you mean we have to finish the project before Friday? — Exactly! || — 所以你的意思是我们得在周五之前完成这个项目？—— 一点没错！
- example: I don't exactly remember what she said at the party last night, but it was something about moving abroad. || 我不太记得她昨晚在派对上说了什么，不过是关于移居国外的事。

## word: precisely
- uk: /prɪˈsaɪsli/
- us: /prɪˈsaɪsli/
- synonyms: exactly || 精确地，准确地 ;; accurately || 准确无误地 ;; strictly || 严格地，确切地 ;; specifically || 明确地，具体地 ;; rigorously || 严谨地，精确地 ;;
- antonyms: approximately || 大约，大概 ;; roughly || 粗略地，大致上 ;; vaguely || 模糊地，不明确地 ;;
- phrases: precisely because || 正是因为 ;; precisely defined || 明确定义的 ;; precisely timed || 计时精确的 ;; precisely speaking || 准确来说 ;; precisely equal || 完全相等的 ;;
- collocations: precisely calculate || 精确计算 ;; precisely control || 精准控制 ;; precisely describe || 准确描述 ;; precisely match || 完全匹配 ;; precisely target || 精准定位 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is precisely + 名词/从句 + that... || 强调句型，用于突出正是某个事物导致了某个结果 ;; Precisely because + 原因状语从句, + 主句 || 用于说明正是某个特定原因导致后续的情况 ;; That is precisely why + 从句 || 用于解释正是某个理由导致了某个结论 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Precisely! || 正是如此！一点没错！ ;; More precisely, ... || 更准确地说，…… ;; Precisely what I mean! || 这正是我想表达的！ ;;
- idioms: at precisely the wrong moment || 偏偏在错误的时机，不巧得很 ;;

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 精确地，准确地 ;; 恰好，正好 ;; （用于强调同意）一点不错，正是如此 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示完全符合事实、标准或特定要求，没有误差 ;; 用于强调某个时间、数量或情况刚好是所说的那样 ;; 用于对话中表示完全赞同对方的说法 ;;
- definitionEn: used to indicate that something is completely accurate and without any error ;; used to emphasize that a particular time, amount, or situation is exactly as stated ;; used in conversation to show that you completely agree with what someone has said ;;
- example: The satellite can precisely locate the target within a range of one meter. || 这颗卫星可以在一米的范围内精准定位目标。
- example: It was precisely 7 o'clock when the first guest arrived at the party. || 第一位客人到达派对的时候正好是7点钟。
- example: "So you think we should postpone the project until the funding is confirmed?" "Precisely!" || “所以你认为我们应该把项目推迟到资金确认之后？”“正是如此！”
- example: Precisely because of his careful preparation, he won the first prize in the speech contest without any surprise. || 正是因为他的精心准备，他毫无悬念地拿下了演讲比赛的第一名。

## word: above
- uk: /əˈbʌv/
- us: /əˈbʌv/
- synonyms: over || 在…上方 ;; higher than || 高于 ;; beyond || 超过 ;; upon || 在…之上 ;;
- antonyms: below || 在…下方 ;; under || 在…下面 ;; beneath || 在…之下 ;;
- phrases: above all || 最重要的是 ;; above average || 高于平均水平 ;; above board || 公开透明的 ;; rise above || 克服，超越 ;;
- collocations: above the law || 凌驾于法律之上 ;; above sea level || 海拔 ;; above suspicion || 无可怀疑 ;; above one's head || 超出某人的理解能力 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + above + noun || 描述事物的位置、级别或程度高于某对象 ;; It is above sb to do sth || 表示做某事超出某人的能力/身份范围 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Above all else, ... || 最重要的是，…… ;; That's above me. || 那个我搞不懂。 ;; Keep it above board, okay? || 要光明正大，好吗？ ;;
- idioms: above oneself || 自高自大，妄自尊大 ;; have one's head above water || 勉强逃脱困境，仅能维持生计 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在（或向）…上面 ;; （数量、水平、级别）超过，高于 ;;
- definitionZh: 位置高于某物，或朝向某物的上方 ;; 数值、程度、地位等超出特定的标准或对象 ;;
- definitionEn: in a higher position than something, or moving to a higher position than something ;; greater in number, level, or rank than a particular standard or thing ;;
- example: The moon was above the trees in the east. || 月亮挂在东边的树林上方。
- example: Temperatures were above average for the time of year. || 这段时间的气温高于往年同期的平均水平。
- example: He is above me in the company hierarchy. || 在公司的层级体系中，他的级别比我高。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 在（或向）上面 ;; 上文，前文 ;;
- definitionZh: 处于更高的位置，或向更高的位置移动 ;; 指在书面内容、讲话的前面部分 ;;
- definitionEn: in or to a higher position ;; in an earlier part of a piece of writing or speech ;;
- example: Please write to us at the address given above. || 请按照上面给出的地址给我们写信。
- example: The clouds above began to get darker as the storm approached. || 随着暴风雨逼近，上方的云层开始变得更暗。
- example: As was mentioned above, this issue will be discussed in detail at the next meeting. || 正如前文提到的，这个问题将在下次会议上详细讨论。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 上述的，前面提到的 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于指代前文已经提到过的事物 ;;
- definitionEn: used to refer to something that has been mentioned earlier in a piece of writing ;;
- example: Please confirm the above information by the end of the week. || 请在本周末之前确认上述信息。
- example: The above rules apply to all staff members without exception. || 上述规定毫无例外适用于所有员工。
- example: If you agree with the above terms, please sign your name at the bottom. || 如果你同意上述条款，请在底部签名。



## word: below
- uk: /bɪˈləʊ/
- us: /bɪˈloʊ/
- synonyms: under || 在…下面 ;; beneath || 在…之下 ;; underneath || 在…底下 ;; lower than || 低于 ;;
- antonyms: above || 在…上方 ;; over || 在…之上 ;; higher than || 高于 ;;
- phrases: below zero || 零度以下 ;; below average || 低于平均水平 ;; below stairs || 在地下室；在仆人住的地方 ;; below par || 低于标准；不舒服 ;;
- collocations: fall below || 降至…以下 ;; rank below || 排名低于 ;; go below || 到甲板以下 ;; temperature below || 温度低于… ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + 形容词 + below sth || 表示主语在某方面低于某事物 ;; below + 名词 + be + 名词 || 用于引出下文内容的倒装结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: See below for details. || 详见下文 ;; It's ten below outside. || 外面是零下十度 ;; You're below the age limit. || 你没到年龄限制 ;;
- idioms: below the belt || 不公正的，暗箭伤人的 ;; below one's breath || 低声地，悄声地 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在…下面 ;; 低于 ;;
- definitionZh: 位置处于某物的更低处 ;; 数值、水平、地位等低于某一标准 ;;
- definitionEn: in or to a lower position than something ;; less than a particular amount, level, or standard ;;
- example: The temperature remained below freezing all day. || 气温一整天都保持在冰点以下。
- example: Her work was well below the standard expected of her. || 她的工作远远低于对她的预期标准。
- example: There is a small lake just below the mountain. || 山脚下正好有一个小湖泊。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 在下面 ;; 下文 ;;
- definitionZh: 处于较低的位置 ;; 在书页、文件等的靠下部分或后文 ;;
- definitionEn: in or to a lower place ;; on a later part of a page or piece of writing ;;
- example: Please fill in the form below. || 请填写下面的表格。
- example: We heard a noise coming from the floor below. || 我们听到楼下传来一阵噪音。
- example: The details are listed below for your reference. || 详情列在下文供你参考。

## word: beyond
- uk: /bɪˈjɒnd/
- us: /bɪˈjɑːnd/
- synonyms: past || 超过，越过 ;; above || 高于，超出 ;; over || 越过，多于 ;;
- antonyms: within || 在…之内 ;; under || 低于，少于 ;;
- phrases: beyond one's reach || 够不着，超出能力范围 ;; beyond doubt || 毫无疑问 ;; beyond repair || 无法修复 ;; beyond comparison || 无与伦比 ;;
- collocations: go beyond || 超出，超越 ;; far beyond || 远远超过 ;; extend beyond || 延伸至…之外 ;; rise beyond || 攀升至…以上 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is beyond sb to do sth || 表示某人无法理解或无法做某事 ;; sth is beyond + 名词（如doubt/recognition/repair） || 表示事物处于某种超出特定范畴的状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Beyond me! || 我可不懂！我搞不定！ ;; It's beyond belief! || 简直难以置信！ ;;
- idioms: beyond the pale || 越轨的，无法接受的 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在（或向）…较远的一边 ;; 超出，超过（数量、水平、范围等） ;; 为…所不及 ;;
- definitionZh: 指位置在某事物的另一边，比某事物更远 ;; 指数量、水平、能力、范围等超出某个界限 ;; 表示某件事超出某人的理解、能力范畴，无法做到或理解 ;;
- definitionEn: on or to the further side of something ;; more than a particular number, level, or limit ;; too difficult or strange for someone to understand or deal with ;;
- example: The lake is beyond those hills. || 湖在那些山的另一边。
- example: The success of the project was beyond our wildest expectations. || 这个项目的成功远远超出了我们的预期。
- example: The technical terms in this paper are beyond the understanding of most ordinary readers. || 这篇论文里的专业术语是大多数普通读者理解不了的。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 在另一边，在更远处 ;; 此外，再者 ;;
- definitionZh: 指位置在更远处的一侧 ;; 用于补充说明除了已经提到的内容之外的部分 ;;
- definitionEn: on or to the further side of a particular place ;; in addition to what has already been mentioned ;;
- example: We could see the mountains in the distance, and the vast plains beyond. || 我们能看到远处的群山，以及山那边辽阔的平原。
- example: He mentioned only the basic plan, and said nothing beyond. || 他只提到了基本方案，除此之外什么都没说。
- example: The path follows the river for a mile and then continues beyond. || 这条小路沿着河流延伸了一英里，之后还向更远处延续。

## word: higher than
- uk: /ˈhaɪə ðæn/
- us: /ˈhaɪər ðæn/
- synonyms: above || 高于，超过 ;; over || 多于，在…之上 ;; exceed || 超出，胜过 ;; outstrip || 超过，比…高 ;;
- antonyms: lower than || 低于，少于 ;; below || 在…之下，低于 ;;
- phrases: higher than average || 高于平均水平 ;; higher than expected || 高于预期 ;; higher than normal || 高于正常水平 ;; higher than the sky || 比天还高 ;;
- collocations: be higher than the threshold || 高于阈值 ;; temperature is higher than usual || 温度比往常高 ;; price is higher than market rate || 价格高于市场价 ;; score is higher than the passing line || 分数高于及格线 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sth + be + higher than + sth || 某物比另一物更高/更多，用于比较两个事物的数值、水平等 ;; sth + have risen + higher than + expected level || 某物的涨幅超过了某一预期标准 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Way higher than I thought! || 比我想的高多了！ ;; It's higher than we can afford. || 这超出我们的承受能力了。 ;; Is this any higher than the last one? || 这个比上一个高吗？ ;;

### sense: 介词短语
- translationZh: 高于；比…高；超过 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于比较两个事物的高度、数值、水平、程度等，表示前者在上述维度上超过后者 ;;
- definitionEn: used to compare the height, value, level, degree, etc. of two things, indicating that the former surpasses the latter in such dimensions ;;
- example: The temperature today is higher than it was yesterday. || 今天的气温比昨天高。
- example: The price of this bag is higher than I expected. || 这个包的价格比我预期的要高。
- example: His academic performance is higher than most of his classmates. || 他的学习成绩比大多数同学都要好。

## word: over
- uk: /ˈəʊvə(r)/
- us: /ˈoʊvər/
- synonyms: above || 在…上方 ;; beyond || 超过 ;; finished || 结束的 ;; across || 从一边到另一边 ;; throughout || 遍及 ;;
- antonyms: under || 在…下方 ;; below || 低于 ;; incomplete || 未完成的 ;;
- phrases: over and over again || 反复地 ;; over there || 在那边 ;; take over || 接管 ;; all over || 到处 ;; go over || 复习，检查 ;;
- collocations: over 18 || 年满18岁 ;; over the weekend || 整个周末 ;; fall over || 摔倒 ;; think over || 仔细考虑 ;; hand over || 移交 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + over || 表示某事已经结束 ;; 主语 + jump/climb + over + 宾语 || 表示越过某个障碍物 ;; It + be + 时间段 + over + since从句 || 表示某事结束已经过去了多久 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Over to you. || 轮到你了，交给你了。 ;; Game over. || 游戏结束，完蛋了。 ;; Come over! || 过来呀！ ;;
- slang: over the moon || 欣喜若狂 ;;
- idioms: over the top || 太夸张，过火 ;; over one's head || 超出某人的理解能力 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在…上方 ;; 超过 ;; 越过 ;; 在…期间 ;; 遍及 ;;
- definitionZh: 位置高于某物且不接触其表面 ;; 数量、程度等超过某个标准 ;; 从某物的一边到另一边 ;; 在某个时间段内 ;; 覆盖某个区域的所有地方 ;;
- definitionEn: in a higher position than something, without touching it ;; more than a particular number, amount, or level ;; from one side of something to the other ;; during a particular period of time ;; existing in or covering all parts of a place ;;
- example: There is a lamp over the desk. || 书桌上方有一盏灯。
- example: The temperature will stay over 30 degrees this week. || 本周气温将保持在30度以上。
- example: We had a nice chat over a cup of coffee. || 我们喝着咖啡聊得很愉快。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 从一侧到另一侧 ;; 落下 ;; 结束 ;; 再一次 ;; 剩余 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示从一个位置向另一个位置移动 ;; 表示从直立的位置倒下 ;; 表示某事已经完成或终止 ;; 表示重复某个动作 ;; 表示剩下、余下 ;;
- definitionEn: from one place or position to another ;; downwards from an upright position ;; used to say that something has finished or ended ;; used to say that something happens again ;; remaining as extra ;;
- example: The car skidded and turned over. || 汽车打滑翻了个身。
- example: The exam is finally over, so we can go out to celebrate. || 考试终于结束了，我们可以出去庆祝了。
- example: Could you say that again? I didn't catch it over the phone. || 你能再说一遍吗？我电话里没听清。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 结束的 ;; 完了的 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示事件、活动等已经完结，不再继续 ;;
- definitionEn: used to describe an event or activity that has finished and will not continue ;;
- example: When the class is over, we'll go to the library. || 下课之后我们会去图书馆。
- example: Their relationship was over after the big argument. || 那场大争吵之后他们的关系就结束了。

## word: under
- uk: /ˈʌndə(r)/
- us: /ˈʌndər/
- synonyms: beneath || 在…下方 ;; below || 在…下面 ;; underneath || 在…底下 ;; lower than || 低于 ;;
- antonyms: above || 在…上方 ;; over || 在…之上 ;; on top of || 在…顶端 ;;
- phrases: under control || 处于控制之下 ;; under pressure || 承受压力 ;; under construction || 正在建造中 ;; under way || 正在进行中 ;; under the weather || 身体不适 ;;
- collocations: under the table || 在桌子下面 ;; under age || 未成年 ;; under attack || 遭到攻击 ;; under the impression || 以为，认为 ;; under no circumstances || 绝不 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + under + noun || 表示处于某种状态（名词多为抽象名词） ;; 动词 + sb/sth + under + noun || 表示将人/物置于某种情况或位置下 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Understood? || 听懂了吗？ ;; Under no way. || 绝对不行。 ;; Keep it under your hat. || 保密。 ;;
- idioms: under the gun || 面临巨大压力，处境艰难 ;; under someone's thumb || 受某人控制，在某人的支配下 ;; under the radar || 不引人注意，低调行事 ;;

### sense: 介词
- translationZh: 在（或到、通过）…下面 ;; 少于，低于 ;; 由…控制（或管理、经营） ;; 根据，按照（协议、法律或制度） ;;
- definitionZh: 位置低于某物，或在某物的下方穿过；数量、程度、年龄等小于某一标准；处于某一机构、规则或人的管辖、约束之下；依据某一规定、体系行事；
- definitionEn: in or to a position lower than something, or moving through a space below something; less than a particular amount, level, age etc; controlled or managed by a particular organization, person, or set of rules; according to a particular agreement, law, or system;
- example: The cat is sleeping under the table. || 猫正在桌子下面睡觉。
- example: Children under 12 can enter the museum for free. || 12岁以下的儿童可以免费进入博物馆。
- example: Under the terms of the contract, you have to give three months' notice if you want to leave. || 根据合同条款，如果你想要离职，必须提前三个月通知。
- example: The team is performing well under the new coach. || 这支队伍在新教练的带领下表现很好。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 在下面，在下方 ;; 少于，小于 ;; 昏迷，失去知觉 ;;
- definitionZh: 处于较低的位置，在下方；数量、程度等低于某一标准；失去意识的状态；
- definitionEn: in or into a lower position, especially below something else; less than a particular amount or level; unconscious;
- example: The boat went under during the storm. || 小船在暴风雨中沉没了。
- example: The temperature stayed ten degrees under for the whole week. || 整整一周气温都低于十度。
- example: He was knocked under by the falling branch. || 他被掉落的树枝砸晕了。

## word: accept
- uk: /əkˈsept/
- us: /əkˈsept/
- synonyms: receive || 接收 ;; adopt || 采纳 ;; agree || 同意 ;; acknowledge || 承认 ;; embrace || 欣然接受 ;;
- antonyms: refuse || 拒绝 ;; reject || 驳回 ;; decline || 谢绝 ;;
- phrases: accept an invitation || 接受邀请 ;; accept a gift || 接收礼物 ;; accept responsibility || 承担责任 ;; accept the truth || 接受事实 ;; accept terms || 接受条款 ;;
- collocations: readily accept || 欣然接受 ;; reluctantly accept || 勉强接受 ;; officially accept || 正式接受 ;; accept graciously || 大方接受 ;; accept unconditionally || 无条件接受 ;;
- sentencePatterns: accept + noun/pronoun || 后接名词或代词作宾语，表示接受某事物 ;; accept that-clause || 后接that引导的宾语从句，表示承认某一事实 ;; accept sb/sth as + noun/adjective || 后接as引导的补足语，表示认为某人/某物是…… ;;
- spokenExpressions: I accept your apology. || 我接受你的道歉。 ;; Do you accept credit cards? || 你们收信用卡吗？ ;; I can't accept that. || 我没法认同这件事。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms: accept the inevitable || 接受不可避免的事实 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 接受，收受 ;; 同意，认可 ;; 承认，承担 ;; 接纳，容纳 ;;
- definitionZh: 接收别人给出的物品、邀请、建议等；同意某种观点、要求或条件；承认某件事的真实性或自己需承担的责任；允许某人加入某个团体、组织等 ;;
- definitionEn: to receive something that is offered or given to you; to agree to a suggestion, idea, or condition; to admit that something is true or that you are responsible for something; to allow someone to join a group, organization, etc. ;;
- example: She accepted the job offer from the international company last week. || 她上周接受了那家跨国公司的工作邀约。
- example: Most scientists accept that climate change is largely caused by human activities. || 大多数科学家都承认气候变化很大程度上是由人类活动导致的。
- example: The local community has warmly accepted the new residents who moved here last month. || 当地社区热情接纳了上个月搬到这里的新居民。
- example: He refused to accept any blame for the failure of the project. || 他拒绝对项目的失败承担任何责任。



## word: adopt
- uk: /əˈdɒpt/
- us: /əˈdɑːpt/
- synonyms: take in || 收养，领养 ;; embrace || 采纳，接受 ;; assume || 承担，承袭 ;; acquire || 获得，取得 ;;
- antonyms: abandon || 遗弃，抛弃 ;; reject || 拒绝，驳回 ;; relinquish || 放弃，让出 ;;
- phrases: adopt a child || 收养儿童 ;; adopt a policy || 采纳政策 ;; adopt an attitude || 采取态度 ;; adopt a resolution || 通过决议 ;;
- collocations: adopt unanimously || 一致通过 ;; adopt formally || 正式采纳 ;; adopt reluctantly || 勉强接受 ;; adopt widely || 广泛采用 ;;
- sentencePatterns: adopt + noun || 后接具体名词作宾语，表示采纳/收养/承担某事物 ;; It is adopted that + clause || it作形式主语，that引导主语从句，表示某决议/方案被通过 ;; adopt sb as + 身份名词 || 表示收养某人作为某身份，或选定某人为某职位 ;;
- spokenExpressions: adopt a new mindset, okay? || 换个新想法吧，行吗？ ;; They decided to adopt last year. || 他们去年决定领养孩子了。 ;; I think we should adopt this plan right away. || 我觉得我们应该立刻采纳这个方案。 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 收养，领养 ;; 采纳，采用 ;; 通过（决议等） ;; 承袭，承担（责任、身份等） ;;
- definitionZh: 合法地将他人子女收为自己的子女抚养； ;; 接受并开始使用某种方法、政策、态度等； ;; 正式通过某项决议、提案等； ;; 承担起某种责任、身份，或沿用某种传统、名字等。
- definitionEn: To legally take another person's child into your own family and raise him or her as your own child; ;; To start using a particular method, policy, attitude, etc.; ;; To formally accept a proposal, resolution, etc. by voting; ;; To take on a responsibility, identity, or follow a tradition, name, etc.
- example: The couple decided to adopt a little girl from the orphanage. || 这对夫妇决定从孤儿院领养一个小女孩。
- example: The company will adopt a new marketing strategy to boost sales next quarter. || 公司下个季度将采用新的营销策略来提升销量。
- example: The committee voted to adopt the amendment to the environmental protection law. || 委员会投票通过了环境保护法的修正案。
- example: He chose to adopt his grandfather's surname after the old man passed away. || 老人去世后，他选择承袭祖父的姓氏。

## word: agree
- uk: /əˈɡriː/
- us: /əˈɡriː/
- synonyms: consent || 同意，准许 ;; assent || 赞成，同意 ;; concur || 一致同意，赞同 ;; accede || 答应，同意 ;; approve || 认可，赞成 ;;
- antonyms: disagree || 不同意，有分歧 ;; oppose || 反对，抵制 ;; reject || 拒绝，驳回 ;;
- phrases: agree with || 同意，和…意见一致 ;; agree on || 对…达成一致 ;; agree to || 同意，接受（提议等） ;; agree about || 对…看法相同 ;; could not agree more || 完全同意 ;;
- collocations: agree fully || 完全同意 ;; agree tentatively || 暂定同意 ;; agree publicly || 公开同意 ;; agree a deal || 达成交易 ;; agree a plan || 商定计划 ;;
- sentencePatterns: agree with sb about/on sth || 表示和某人在某件事上意见一致 ;; agree to do sth || 表示同意做某事 ;; It is agreed that... || 表示大家一致同意…… ;;
- spokenExpressions: I couldn't agree more! || 我完全同意！ ;; Agree to disagree. || 各自保留不同意见吧。 ;; We're agreed then? || 那我们就算达成一致了？ ;;
- idioms: agree to differ || 同意各自保留不同意见 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 同意，赞成 ;; 一致，相符 ;; 商定，约定 ;; （气候、食物等）适合，相宜 ;;
- definitionZh: 对某事持有相同的意见，或认可他人的提议、观点等 ;; 两者之间在内容、性质等方面保持一致，没有冲突 ;; 多方共同商议确定某件事；；指环境、食物等对人的健康或状态没有不良影响 ;;
- definitionEn: to have the same opinion as someone, or to accept a suggestion, idea, etc. ;; to be the same as something, or to match with it ;; to decide on something with other people ;; if food, weather, etc. agrees with you, it makes you feel healthy and good ;;
- example: I completely agree with your view on environmental protection. || 我完全同意你在环境保护方面的观点。
- example: The two sides agreed to sign the cooperation contract next month. || 双方商定下个月签署合作合同。
- example: The data from the two experiments don't agree, so we need to redo the test. || 两次实验的数据不一致，所以我们需要重新测试。
- example: Seafood doesn't agree with me, so I never eat it when I travel to coastal cities. || 我吃海鲜不舒服，所以去沿海城市旅行的时候我从来不吃海鲜。

## word: receive
- uk: /rɪˈsiːv/
- us: /rɪˈsiːv/

- antonyms: send || 发送，寄出 ;; give || 给予，赠送 ;;

- spokenExpressions: Did you receive my message? || 你收到我的消息了吗？ ;; I received your gift, thank you so much! || 我收到你的礼物了，太感谢你了！ ;; How did the proposal receive? || 大家对这个提议反响怎么样？ ;;

- definitionEn: to get something that is sent or given to you; to experience a particular type of treatment or reaction; to welcome or meet someone who arrives ;;
- example: I received a parcel from my parents yesterday. || 我昨天收到了父母寄来的一个包裹。
- example: The new policy received widespread criticism from the public. || 这项新政策遭到了公众的广泛批评。
- example: The hotel staff received us with big smiles when we arrived. || 我们到达时，酒店工作人员笑容满面地接待了我们。

## word: refuse
- uk: /rɪˈfjuːz/ (v); /ˈrefjuːs/ (n)
- us: /rɪˈfjuːz/ (v); /ˈrefjuːs/ (n)
- synonyms: reject || 拒绝 ;; decline || 谢绝 ;; repudiate || 否认，拒绝接受 ;; spurn || 摒弃，唾弃 ;;
- antonyms: accept || 接受 ;; agree || 同意 ;; consent || 应允，同意 ;;
- phrases: refuse to do sth || 拒绝做某事 ;; refuse collection || 垃圾收集 ;; household refuse || 生活垃圾 ;; refuse disposal || 垃圾处理 ;;
- collocations: flatly refuse || 断然拒绝 ;; politely refuse || 礼貌地拒绝 ;; refuse an offer || 拒绝提议 ;; refuse a request || 拒绝请求 ;;
- sentencePatterns: refuse + to-infinitive || 后接不定式作宾语，表示拒绝做某个动作 ;; refuse + sb + sth || 接双宾语，表示拒绝给予某人某物 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I can't refuse. || 我没法拒绝。 ;; No one can refuse that. || 没人能拒绝那个。 ;; Why did you refuse? || 你为什么拒绝了？ ;;
- idioms: refuse to take no for an answer || 不接受否定答复，非让人同意不可 ;;

### sense: 动词 (v.)
- translationZh: 拒绝，回绝 ;; 拒绝给予，不准许 ;;
- definitionZh: 明确表示不愿意做某事、接受某物或同意某个请求 ;; 不将某人想要的事物提供给对方 ;;
- definitionEn: To state firmly that you will not do something, accept something, or agree to a request ;; To not give someone something that they have asked for ;;
- example: He refused to comment on the controversial issue. || 他拒绝对这个有争议的问题发表评论。
- example: The bank refused him a loan because of his poor credit record. || 银行因为他信用记录不好拒绝给他贷款。
- example: She politely refused the invitation to the dinner party as she had other plans. || 她因为有其他安排，礼貌地拒绝了晚宴的邀请。

### sense: 名词 (n.)
- translationZh: 垃圾，废弃物 ;;
- definitionZh: 被丢弃的、没有用处的物品 ;;
- definitionEn: Waste material that people throw away because it is no longer useful or wanted ;;
- example: Local residents are required to sort their refuse before putting it in the bins. || 当地居民被要求在把垃圾扔进垃圾桶之前先进行分类。
- example: The weekly refuse collection is scheduled for every Tuesday morning in this community. || 这个小区的每周垃圾收集定在每周二上午。
- example: Illegal dumping of industrial refuse is strictly prohibited and will result in heavy fines. || 非法倾倒工业垃圾是被严格禁止的，会导致高额罚款。

## word: reject
- uk: /rɪˈdʒekt/
- us: /rɪˈdʒekt/
- synonyms: refuse || 拒绝 ;; decline || 谢绝 ;; turn down || 驳回 ;; repudiate || 否定 ;; discard || 丢弃 ;;
- antonyms: accept || 接受 ;; approve || 批准 ;; adopt || 采纳 ;;
- phrases: reject a proposal || 拒绝提案 ;; reject an application || 驳回申请 ;; reject out of hand || 断然拒绝 ;; reject faulty goods || 退回次品 ;;
- collocations: officially reject || 正式驳回 ;; flatly reject || 断然拒绝 ;; reluctantly reject || 不情愿地拒绝 ;; reject an argument || 驳斥论点 ;; reject a request || 拒绝请求 ;;
- sentencePatterns: reject + sth || 后接名词/代词作宾语，表示拒绝某事物 ;; reject + sb/sth + as + adj/n || 表示认为某人/某物是某种情况而拒绝 ;; be rejected by + sb/sth || 被动语态，表示被某人/某机构拒绝 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I had to reject it. || 我只能拒绝它。 ;; My application got rejected. || 我的申请被拒了。 ;; Don't reject the idea out of hand. || 别一下子就否定这个想法。 ;;
- idioms: reject the null hypothesis || 否定零假设（统计学术语，引申为推翻原有假设） ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 拒绝 ;; 驳回 ;; 拒收 ;; 不录用 ;; 排斥 ;;
- definitionZh: 拒绝接受或同意某事物 ;; 不认可、不通过申请、提案等 ;; 因质量问题退回物品 ;; 不录用求职者、不录取申请者 ;; 生物机体对移植器官等产生排异反应 ;;
- definitionEn: to refuse to accept, believe in, or agree with something ;; to officially refuse to allow a request, application, or plan to succeed ;; to send back goods that are not good enough to be sold or used ;; to decide not to hire someone or accept them for a course of study ;; if a person's body rejects a transplanted organ, it reacts to the organ as if it is harmful and tries to destroy it ;;
- example: The committee unanimously rejected the proposal to build a new shopping mall in the residential area. || 委员会一致否决了在居民区新建购物中心的提案。
- example: My visa application was rejected because I didn't provide sufficient proof of financial support. || 我的签证申请被驳回了，因为我没有提供足够的资金证明。
- example: Patients who receive organ transplants need to take special medicine so that their bodies do not reject the new organ. || 接受器官移植的病人需要服用特殊药物，避免身体对新器官产生排异反应。

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 被拒绝的人 ;; 次品 ;; 不合格产品 ;;
- definitionZh: 未被选中、未被录取的人 ;; 因质量不合格被淘汰的产品 ;;
- definitionEn: a person who has been rejected by a particular group, organization, or society ;; a product that cannot be sold or used because it has something wrong with it ;;
- example: He felt like a social reject after none of the universities he applied to sent him an offer. || 在申请的大学都没有发来录取通知书后，他觉得自己是个被社会排斥的人。
- example: These rejects from the factory are sold at a discounted price in the outlet store. || 这些工厂的不合格次品在折扣店里低价出售。
- example: The quality inspection team threw all the manufacturing rejects into the recycling bin. || 质检团队把所有生产残次品都扔进了回收箱。

## word: accident
- uk: /ˈæksɪdənt/
- us: /ˈæksɪdənt/
- synonyms: mishap || 不幸事件，小事故 ;; misfortune || 厄运，不幸遭遇 ;; incident || 事件，事变 ;; casualty || 意外事故，伤亡人员 ;;
- antonyms: intention || 故意，意图 ;; plan || 计划，规划 ;;
- phrases: traffic accident || 交通事故 ;; by accident || 偶然，意外地 ;; industrial accident || 工伤事故 ;; accident insurance || 意外保险 ;;
- collocations: cause an accident || 引发事故 ;; avoid an accident || 避免事故 ;; serious accident || 严重事故 ;; minor accident || 轻微事故 ;; report an accident || 上报事故 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is reported that + 事故相关内容 || 用于通报事故发生的情况 ;; sb. have an accident + 地点/时间状语 || 用于说明某人在某时某地遭遇事故 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It was a pure accident. || 这纯粹是个意外。 ;; No one was hurt in the accident, right? || 事故里没人受伤吧？ ;; It happened completely by accident. || 这事完全是碰巧发生的。 ;;
- idioms: an accident waiting to happen || 早晚会出问题的事，隐患 ;;
### sense: noun
- translationZh: 意外事故 ;; 偶然，意外 ;;
- definitionZh: 指意料之外、突然发生的不幸事件，通常造成损伤或损失 ;; 指非刻意安排、偶然发生的情况 ;;
- definitionEn: an unexpected and unpleasant event that often causes injury or damage ;; something that happens without being planned or intended ;;
- example: A serious car accident happened on the highway this morning. || 今天早上高速路上发生了一起严重的车祸。
- example: I deleted the important file by accident yesterday. || 我昨天不小心删掉了那份重要文件。
- example: The factory has taken strict measures to prevent industrial accidents. || 这家工厂采取了严格措施防范工伤事故。



## word: incident
- uk: /ˈɪnsɪdənt/
- us: /ˈɪnsɪdənt/
- synonyms: event || 事件 ;; occurrence || 发生的事情 ;; mishap || 小事故 ;; episode || 一段经历，插曲 ;;
- antonyms: routine || 常规，惯例 ;; norm || 常态，正常标准 ;;
- phrases: security incident || 安全事件 ;; border incident || 边境事件 ;; isolated incident || 孤立事件 ;; traffic incident || 交通事故 ;;
- collocations: report an incident || 上报事件 ;; investigate an incident || 调查事件 ;; cause an incident || 引发事件 ;; serious incident || 严重事件 ;; minor incident || 轻微事件 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There was an incident at + 地点 || 表示某地发生了某起事件 ;; The incident occurred when + 时间/条件从句 || 说明事件发生的时间或触发条件 ;;
- spokenExpressions: There was a little incident earlier. || 早前出了点小状况。;; Let's not make an incident out of this. || 我们别把这事闹大了。;; That incident was so embarrassing! || 那事也太尴尬了！;;
- idioms: without incident || 平安无事，顺利地 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: （通常指不愉快的）事件，事故 ;; （两国间的）冲突，摩擦 ;;
- definitionZh: 发生的不寻常或令人不快的事情，尤指造成一定影响的意外状况；也指国家、团体之间的小型冲突事件 ;; 文学、叙事中一段相对独立的情节、插曲 ;;
- definitionEn: an event, especially one that is unusual, important, or unpleasant; a small conflict or disagreement between countries or groups ;; a separate and distinct part of a story or series of events ;;
- example: The police are investigating the incident that happened outside the nightclub last night. || 警方正在调查昨晚发生在夜总会外的那起事件。
- example: The border incident led to increased tensions between the two countries. || 这起边境冲突导致两国之间的紧张局势加剧。
- example: Apart from a small delay at the airport, our trip passed without incident. || 除了在机场有一点延误之外，我们的旅途全程都很顺利。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 伴随而来的，附带的 ;; 入射的（物理术语） ;;
- definitionZh: 作为某一事件、情况的附带结果而产生的；物理学中用来描述光线、辐射等投射到某个表面的 ;;
- definitionEn: happening as a natural result or part of something else; (in physics) falling on or striking a surface, used of light, radiation, etc. ;;
- example: There are many risks incident to the job of a firefighter. || 消防员这份工作伴随有很多风险。
- example: The incident light is reflected off the mirror into the sensor. || 入射光经镜子反射到传感器上。
- example: The difficulties incident to the project were far more than we had expected. || 该项目附带的难题比我们预想的多得多。

## word: intention
- uk: /ɪnˈtenʃən/
- us: /ɪnˈtenʃən/
- synonyms: intent || 意图，目的 ;; purpose || 目的，目标 ;; aim || 目标，打算 ;; motive || 动机，目的 ;; goal || 目标 ;;
- antonyms: accident || 意外 ;; coincidence || 巧合 ;; inadvertence || 疏忽，无心之举 ;;
- phrases: original intention || 初衷 ;; good intention || 善意，好意 ;; with the intention of || 抱有…的目的 ;; have no intention of || 无意做… ;; declare one's intention || 表明意图 ;;
- collocations: clear intention || 明确的意图 ;; hidden intention || 隐藏的意图 ;; real intention || 真实意图 ;; express an intention || 表达意图 ;; fulfill one's intention || 实现自己的打算 ;;
- sentencePatterns: have (no) intention of doing sth || 表示（不）打算做某事 ;; with the intention of doing sth || 作状语说明做某事的目的 ;; It is not sb's intention to do sth || 用于表示某人并非有意做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It wasn't my intention. || 我不是故意的。 ;; What's your intention here? || 你这是什么意思？ ;; I have every intention of keeping my promise. || 我绝对会遵守诺言的。 ;;
- idioms: with the best of intentions || 出于一片好心，好心好意 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 意图 ;; 目的 ;; 打算 ;;
- definitionZh: 某人想要做某事的计划、想法或目的 ;; 言行背后暗含的想法或动机 ;;
- definitionEn: a plan or desire to do something ;; the aim or meaning that is behind what someone says or does ;;
- example: He announced his intention to run for president next year. || 他宣布了明年竞选总统的打算。
- example: She went to the town with the intention of visiting her old friend. || 她去那个镇子是为了看望她的老朋友。
- example: I'm sure he had no intention of hurting your feelings when he said that. || 我确定他说那番话的时候无意伤害你的感情。

## word: misfortune
- uk: /ˌmɪsˈfɔːtʃuːn/
- us: /ˌmɪsˈfɔːrtʃuːn/
- synonyms: adversity || 逆境 ;; bad luck || 厄运 ;; mishap || 小灾祸 ;; hardship || 困苦 ;; ill fortune || 不幸 ;;
- antonyms: fortune || 好运 ;; luck || 幸运 ;; blessing || 幸事 ;;
- phrases: suffer misfortune || 遭受不幸 ;; a stroke of misfortune || 一次厄运 ;; misfortune befalls sb || 不幸降临到某人身上 ;; through no misfortune of one's own || 并非由于自身的过错 ;;
- collocations: great misfortune || 巨大的不幸 ;; personal misfortune || 个人不幸 ;; financial misfortune || 财务困境 ;; unexpected misfortune || 意外灾祸 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is a misfortune that + 从句 || 表示“……是一件不幸的事” ;; sb has the misfortune to do sth || 表示“某人不幸做了某事” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Misfortunes never come singly. || 祸不单行。 ;; Every cloud has a silver lining, even in misfortune. || 就算遭遇不幸，也总会有好的一面。 ;; Don't gloat over other people's misfortunes. || 别对别人的不幸幸灾乐祸。 ;;
- idioms: Misfortunes tell us what fortune is. || 不经灾难不知福。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 不幸 ;; 厄运 ;; 不幸事故 ;;
- definitionZh: 不好的运气或令人痛苦、不利的处境 ;; 意外发生的倒霉事件 ;;
- definitionEn: bad luck, or an unfortunate event or situation ;; an unpleasant or unlucky event that happens to someone ;;
- example: He had the misfortune to lose his job just weeks after buying a new house. || 他刚买了新房几周就不幸丢了工作。
- example: It's a terrible misfortune that the whole village was destroyed by the flood. || 整个村庄被洪水冲毁，这是一场可怕的灾难。
- example: She bore her misfortunes bravely and never complained to anyone. || 她勇敢地承受着自己的不幸，从不向任何人抱怨。

## word: mishap
- uk: /ˈmɪshæp/
- us: /ˈmɪshæp/
- synonyms: misfortune || 不幸 ;; accident || 意外 ;; blunder || 失误 ;; mishap || 小灾祸 ;; misadventure || 不幸遭遇 ;;
- antonyms: fortune || 好运 ;; success || 顺利 ;; luck || 幸运 ;;
- phrases: minor mishap || 小意外 ;; without mishap || 平安无事地 ;; travel mishap || 旅行意外 ;; domestic mishap || 家庭小事故 ;; work mishap || 工作失误 ;;
- collocations: cause a mishap || 引发意外 ;; suffer a mishap || 遭遇不幸 ;; avoid a mishap || 避免失误 ;; a slight mishap || 轻微的小事故 ;; a series of mishaps || 一连串的倒霉事 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sth be a mishap for sb || 某事对某人来说是一场意外 ;; Sb do sth without mishap || 某人平安无事地做完某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Oh, just a little mishap! || 哦，就是个小意外而已！ ;; No mishaps so far, right? || 到目前为止都没出问题，对吧？ ;; It's just a tiny mishap, no big deal. || 就是个小失误，没什么大不了的。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 小事故 ;; 不幸 ;; 小灾祸 ;;
- definitionZh: 轻微的、通常不严重的意外事件或不幸遭遇 ;; 较小的失误或倒霉事 ;;
- definitionEn: a small accident or unlucky event that is usually not serious ;; a minor mistake or unfortunate occurrence ;;
- example: We arrived at the destination without any mishap. || 我们平安无事地抵达了目的地。
- example: The only mishap during the trip was that my suitcase got lost for two hours. || 旅途中唯一的小意外是我的行李箱丢失了两个小时。
- example: A slight mishap in the kitchen delayed the dinner for half an hour. || 厨房里的一个小事故让晚餐推迟了半个小时。
- example: He had a series of mishaps last week, from missing the bus to spilling coffee on his laptop. || 他上周遭遇了一连串的倒霉事，从错过公交到把咖啡洒在笔记本电脑上。
- example: The event went smoothly with no major mishaps. || 活动进展顺利，没有出现重大意外。

## word: plan
- uk: /plæn/
- us: /plæn/
- synonyms: scheme || 计划，方案 ;; program || 计划，规划 ;; project || 计划，项目 ;; blueprint || 蓝图，行动方案 ;;
- antonyms: improvisation || 即兴创作，临时应对 ;; randomness || 随机，无计划 ;;
- phrases: plan for || 为……做计划 ;; work out a plan || 制定计划 ;; carry out a plan || 执行计划 ;; give up a plan || 放弃计划 ;;
- collocations: detailed plan || 详细计划 ;; long-term plan || 长期计划 ;; contingency plan || 应急计划 ;; realistic plan || 切实可行的计划 ;;
- sentencePatterns: plan to do sth || 表示“计划做某事”的常用结构 ;; make a plan for (doing) sth || 表示“为（做）某事制定计划”的结构 ;; It is planned that... || 表示“据计划……”的被动结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Plan ahead! || 提前做计划！ ;; What's your plan for the weekend? || 你周末有什么打算？ ;; That's the plan! || 就这么定了！ ;;
- idioms: best-laid plans || 世事难料，计划再好也可能出问题 ;; go according to plan || 进展顺利，按计划进行 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 计划，方案 ;; 规划，蓝图 ;;
- definitionZh: 为实现某个目标而预先制定的具体行动安排、步骤或构想 ;; 对未来较长时间的发展、工作等做出的系统性安排 ;;
- definitionEn: a detailed proposal for doing or achieving something ;; a systematic arrangement of future activities or developments ;;
- example: We need to come up with a feasible plan to finish the project on time. || 我们需要想出一个可行的方案来按时完成这个项目。
- example: The government has released a new urban development plan for the next five years. || 政府公布了未来五年新的城市发展规划。
- example: If everything goes according to plan, we will arrive in Paris at 3 p.m. local time. || 如果一切按计划进行，我们将在当地时间下午3点抵达巴黎。

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 计划，打算 ;; 规划，安排 ;;
- definitionZh: 预先决定做某事、安排行动的具体内容和时间 ;; 对某件事的流程、细节等做系统性的筹备 ;;
- definitionEn: to decide on and arrange in advance what you are going to do ;; to make preparations for something in a systematic way ;;
- example: My family plans to go hiking in the mountains this Saturday if the weather is nice. || 如果天气好的话，我家计划这周六去山里徒步。
- example: The travel agency has planned a 10-day route for us covering three European countries. || 旅行社已经为我们规划了一条涵盖三个欧洲国家的10天行程。
- example: You should plan your budget carefully before you start decorating the apartment. || 在开始装修公寓之前，你应该仔细规划你的预算。

## word: ache
- uk: /eɪk/
- us: /eɪk/
- synonyms: pain || 疼痛 ;; soreness || 酸痛 ;; throbbing || 阵痛 ;; pang || 剧痛 ;; twinge || 刺痛 ;;
- antonyms: comfort || 舒适 ;; ease || 安逸 ;; relief || 缓解 ;;
- phrases: stomach ache || 胃痛 ;; tooth ache || 牙痛 ;; head ache || 头痛 ;; muscle ache || 肌肉酸痛 ;; heart ache || 心痛 ;;
- collocations: ache badly || 痛得厉害 ;; ache dull || 隐隐作痛 ;; ache continuously || 持续疼痛 ;; ache all over || 浑身疼痛 ;; ache with fatigue || 因疲劳疼痛 ;;
- sentencePatterns: 主语 + ache + 状语 || 描述某个部位疼痛的状态 ;; 主语 + ache for + 宾语 || 表达强烈渴望某人/某物 ;;
- spokenExpressions: My whole body aches. || 我浑身都疼。 ;; My heart aches for them. || 我很心疼他们。 ;; That's going to ache tomorrow. || 那地方明天肯定会疼的。 ;;
- idioms: ache all over || 浑身疼痛；极度疲惫 ;;

### sense: 不及物动词
- translationZh: 疼痛 ;; 渴望 ;;
- definitionZh: 身体某个部位持续地隐隐作痛；因思念、同情等情感产生强烈的渴望或心痛感 ;;
- definitionEn: If a part of your body aches, you feel a continuous dull pain in that part; if you ache for someone or something, you feel a strong desire for them, often with sadness ;;
- example: After running the marathon, my legs ached for days. || 跑完马拉松之后，我的腿疼了好几天。
- example: She ached to see her family who lived overseas. || 她非常渴望见到住在海外的家人。
- example: My shoulders ache from sitting at the desk all day. || 我因为一整天坐在书桌前，肩膀很疼。

### sense: 可数名词
- translationZh: 疼痛 ;; 隐痛 ;;
- definitionZh: 身体部位持续的、不剧烈的疼痛感；也可指情感上的痛苦 ;;
- definitionEn: A continuous dull pain that you feel in part of your body; a feeling of emotional pain ;;
- example: The dull ache in her lower back made it hard to walk. || 她后背下方的隐痛让她走路都很困难。
- example: There was a constant ache in his chest after he heard the bad news. || 听到坏消息之后，他的胸口一直隐隐作痛。
- example: This muscle ache is a common side effect of the workout. || 这种肌肉酸痛是锻炼后的常见副作用。



## word: comfort
- uk: /ˈkʌmfət/
- us: /ˈkʌmfərt/
- synonyms: consolation || 安慰，慰藉 ;; ease || 舒适，安逸 ;; solace || 安慰，抚慰 ;; relief || 宽慰，解脱 ;;
- antonyms: discomfort || 不适，不安 ;; distress || 痛苦，苦恼 ;; misery || 痛苦，悲惨 ;;
- phrases: comfort zone || 舒适区 ;; creature comforts || 物质享受 ;; comfort food || 治愈食物（给人带来慰藉的食物） ;; take comfort in || 从…中得到安慰 ;;
- collocations: provide comfort || 提供安慰 ;; bring comfort || 带来慰藉 ;; emotional comfort || 情感慰藉 ;; comfort level || 舒适度 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is a comfort to do sth || 做某事是一种慰藉 ;; take comfort in (doing) sth || 从（做）某事中获得安慰 ;; comfort sb for sth || 因某事安慰某人 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Take comfort, it'll get better. || 放宽心，情况会好起来的。 ;; This is my go-to comfort when I'm down. || 这是我心情不好的时候常用的慰藉物。 ;; I need a little comfort right now. || 我现在需要点安慰。 ;;
- idioms: cold comfort || 无用的安慰，于事无补的慰藉 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 舒适，安逸 ;; 安慰，慰藉 ;; 令人感到安慰的人/物 ;;
- definitionZh: 身体或精神上放松、没有痛苦的状态 ;; 用来缓解他人悲伤、忧虑的话语或行为 ;; 能给人带来安心感的人或事物 ;;
- definitionEn: The state of being physically relaxed and free from pain ;; Words or actions intended to make someone who is sad or worried feel better ;; A person or thing that makes you feel calm or less anxious ;;
- example: The hotel room was designed for maximum comfort. || 这间酒店客房的设计追求极致舒适。
- example: Her kind words were a great comfort to me when my father passed away. || 我父亲去世时，她友善的话语给了我莫大的安慰。
- example: For many people, a warm cup of tea is a small comfort on a cold day. || 对很多人来说，一杯热茶是寒冷天气里的小小慰藉。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 安慰，抚慰 ;; 使舒适，使放松 ;;
- definitionZh: 对感到悲伤、焦虑的人说友善的话或做体贴的事，让其感觉好一些 ;; 让某人处于放松、没有不适的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: To say or do kind things to someone who is sad or worried to make them feel better ;; To make someone feel relaxed and free from discomfort ;;
- example: She comforted the crying child by giving him a hug. || 她抱了抱那个哭闹的孩子，安慰他。
- example: The soft couch comforted my aching back after a long day of work. || 工作了一整天后，柔软的沙发缓解了我背部的疼痛。
- example: When her friend failed the exam, she stayed to comfort her and help her review for the retake. || 她朋友考试失利时，她留下来安慰她，还帮她复习备考重考。

## word: ease
- uk: /iːz/
- us: /iːz/
- synonyms: comfort || 舒适 ;; relief || 宽慰 ;; facility || 轻松 ;; tranquility || 安宁 ;;
- antonyms: difficulty || 困难 ;; anxiety || 焦虑 ;; hardship || 困苦 ;;
- phrases: ease of use || 易用性 ;; ease up || 放松；缓和 ;; at ease || 自在；安逸 ;; with ease || 轻而易举地 ;;
- collocations: ease the pain || 缓解疼痛 ;; ease the burden || 减轻负担 ;; ease into sth || 慢慢适应某事 ;; ease restrictions || 放宽限制 ;;
- sentencePatterns: ease sb's mind || 打消某人的顾虑，说明：ease后接表示担忧、顾虑类的名词，表达缓解某人的情绪 ;; ease off/up on sth || 减少对某事的力度，说明：后接具体的管控、施压对象，表达放宽要求 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Take it easy! || 放轻松！ ;; Put/Set sb at ease. || 让某人放松下来。 ;; Ease up a bit! || 缓一缓！ ;;
- idioms: ill at ease || 局促不安；不自在 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 舒适；安逸 ;; 容易；轻松 ;; 自在；不拘束 ;;
- definitionZh: 没有痛苦、担忧或压力的舒适状态 ;; 做某事不费力的状态 ;; 放松、不拘谨的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: The state of being comfortable, without pain, worry, or pressure ;; The quality of being easy to do or achieve ;; A relaxed and uninhibited state ;;
- example: The medicine gave her some ease from the headache. || 这种药缓解了她的头痛，让她舒服了些。
- example: He passed the exam with ease, as he had studied for months. || 他轻而易举地通过了考试，因为他已经学习了好几个月。
- example: The warm smile of the host put all the guests at ease. || 主人温暖的笑容让所有客人都感到自在。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 减轻；缓解 ;; 使放松 ;; 缓慢小心地移动 ;;
- definitionZh: 减少痛苦、负担、困难等的程度 ;; 让某人不再紧张、担忧 ;; 缓慢且谨慎地移动到某个位置 ;;
- definitionEn: To make pain, burden, difficulty etc. less severe ;; To make someone feel less nervous or worried ;; To move slowly and carefully into a particular position ;;
- example: The new policy is designed to ease the financial pressure on low-income families. || 这项新政策旨在缓解低收入家庭的经济压力。
- example: She eased herself into the armchair after a long day at work. || 工作了一整天后，她小心翼翼地坐到扶手椅上。
- example: The government decided to ease the travel restrictions next month. || 政府决定下个月放宽旅行限制。

## word: pain
- uk: /peɪn/
- us: /peɪn/
- synonyms: ache || 疼痛 ;; suffering || 痛苦 ;; agony || 剧痛 ;; distress || 苦恼 ;; soreness || 酸痛 ;;
- antonyms: pleasure || 愉悦 ;; comfort || 舒适 ;; ease || 安逸 ;;
- phrases: physical pain || 身体疼痛 ;; emotional pain || 情感痛苦 ;; pain relief || 止痛 ;; sharp pain || 剧痛 ;; chronic pain || 慢性疼痛 ;;
- collocations: feel pain || 感到疼痛 ;; cause pain || 造成疼痛 ;; ease pain || 缓解疼痛 ;; bear pain || 忍受疼痛 ;; inflict pain on sb || 给某人施加痛苦 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It pains sb to do sth || 表示“做某事让某人感到痛苦” ;; take (great) pains to do sth || 表示“煞费苦心做某事” ;; be in pain || 表示“处于痛苦中” ;;
- spokenExpressions: No pain, no gain. || 一分耕耘一分收获。 ;; It's a pain in the neck. || 这真烦人。 ;; I feel your pain. || 我理解你的感受。 ;;
- idioms: a pain in the backside || 极其讨厌的人（或事） ;; for one's pains || 作为辛苦的酬劳 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 疼痛 ;; 痛苦 ;; 烦恼 ;;
- definitionZh: 身体受伤或患病时产生的不舒服的感觉 ;; 精神或情感上的难过、苦恼的感受 ;; 令人厌烦的人或事物 ;;
- definitionEn: the unpleasant physical feeling that you have when you are hurt or ill ;; the unpleasant emotional feeling that you have when something bad happens ;; a person or thing that is annoying ;;
- example: The pain in my knee is getting worse after running. || 跑步之后我膝盖的疼痛加剧了。
- example: It took her years to get over the pain of losing her parents. || 她花了很多年才走出失去父母的痛苦。
- example: That kid who always makes noise in class is a real pain. || 那个总在课上吵闹的小孩真的很烦人。

### sense: v.
- translationZh: 使痛苦 ;; 使苦恼 ;;
- definitionZh: 让某人感到身体或精神上的痛苦 ;;
- definitionEn: to make someone feel emotional or physical pain ;;
- example: It pains me to see my best friend going through such a hard time. || 看到我最好的朋友经历这么艰难的时期，我很心疼。
- example: His unkind words pained her deeply. || 他不友善的话深深地伤了她的心。
- example: My shoulder pains me whenever the weather gets cold. || 每次天气变冷的时候我的肩膀就疼。

## word: soreness
- uk: /ˈsɔːnəs/
- us: /ˈsɔːrnəs/
- synonyms: ache || 疼痛 ;; tenderness || 触痛 ;; stiffness || 僵硬酸痛 ;; throbbing || 抽痛 ;; discomfort || 不适感 ;;
- antonyms: comfort || 舒适 ;; numbness || 麻木 ;; painlessness || 无痛 ;;
- phrases: muscle soreness || 肌肉酸痛 ;; delayed onset muscle soreness || 迟发性肌肉酸痛 ;; throat soreness || 喉咙痛 ;; joint soreness || 关节酸痛 ;; skin soreness || 皮肤灼痛 ;;
- collocations: cause soreness || 引发酸痛 ;; relieve soreness || 缓解酸痛 ;; reduce soreness || 减轻酸痛 ;; persistent soreness || 持续性酸痛 ;; mild soreness || 轻微酸痛 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Soreness in + 身体部位 + occurs after + 活动 || 用于说明某部位在特定活动后出现酸痛 ;; + 动词 + soreness caused by + 原因 || 用于描述处理某种原因导致的酸痛症状 ;; Soreness usually + 变化趋势 + within + 时间段 || 用于说明酸痛的持续时长规律 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Oh, the soreness in my legs is killing me today! || 哦，我今天腿酸得要命！ ;; A bit of soreness after working out is totally normal. || 健身后有点酸痛是完全正常的。 ;; This cream should help take the edge off the soreness. || 这个药膏应该能稍微缓解酸痛。 ;;

### sense: noun [U]
- translationZh: 酸痛 ;; （身体部位的）疼痛、不适感 ;;
- definitionZh: 身体部位因受伤、过度使用或炎症产生的疼痛、酸胀的不适感 ;; 因摩擦、刺激导致的皮肤或黏膜的触痛感 ;;
- definitionEn: A painful, aching feeling in a part of your body, usually caused by injury, overuse, or inflammation. ;; A tender, uncomfortable feeling of skin or mucous membrane caused by friction or irritation. ;;
- example: The soreness in your shoulders will fade away after a few days of rest. || 你肩膀的酸痛休息几天就会消退的。
- example: Delayed onset muscle soreness often peaks 24 to 72 hours after a strenuous workout. || 迟发性肌肉酸痛通常在高强度锻炼后的24到72小时达到峰值。
- example: Sucking on lozenges can help ease the soreness of a sore throat caused by a cold. || 含润喉糖有助于缓解感冒引起的喉咙疼痛。

## word: throbbing
- uk: /ˈθrɒbɪŋ/
- us: /ˈθrɑːbɪŋ/
- synonyms: pounding || 剧烈跳动的 ;; throbbing || 悸动的 ;; palpitating || 突突跳的 ;; pulsating || 脉动的 ;; beating || 跳动的 ;;
- antonyms: still || 静止的 ;; calm || 平稳的 ;; motionless || 不动的 ;;
- phrases: throbbing pain || 搏动性疼痛 ;; throbbing headache || 搏动性头痛 ;; throbbing pulse || 跳动的脉搏 ;; throbbing music || 节奏强烈的音乐 ;;
- collocations: throbbing violently || 剧烈地跳动 ;; throbbing constantly || 持续地抽动 ;; throbbing with excitement || 激动得怦怦跳 ;; throbbing with pain || 疼得突突跳 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sth + be + throbbing + 状语 || 表示某物（通常是身体部位、心脏等）正处于跳动/抽动的状态 ;; There be + a throbbing + 名词 + in + 身体部位 || 表示身体某个部位有搏动性的不适感 ;;
- spokenExpressions: My head's throbbing like crazy. || 我头疼得突突直跳。 ;; My heart's throbbing so fast right now. || 我现在心跳得好快。 ;; The cut on my hand is throbbing so bad. || 我手上的伤口疼得一抽一抽的。 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 抽动的，阵痛的 ;; 跳动的，悸动的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指身体部位因疼痛、激动等有规律地强烈跳动的；也可形容音乐、节奏等有强烈跳动感的 ;; 描述心跳、脉搏等有节律地快速跳动的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: (of a part of the body) beating or hurting with a strong, regular rhythm ;; having a strong, regular pulsating rhythm ;;
- example: I have a throbbing pain in my temple after working for 12 hours straight. || 连续工作12小时后，我的太阳穴一阵阵抽痛。
- example: The throbbing beat of the rock concert could be heard from a block away. || 摇滚演唱会强烈的节奏在一个街区外都能听到。
- example: She felt a throbbing sensation in her wrist when she twisted it accidentally. || 她不小心扭到手腕时，感到手腕一阵阵突突地疼。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 搏动，跳动 ;; 抽痛，阵痛 ;;
- definitionZh: 有规律的强烈跳动的动作或感觉；也指这种跳动带来的疼痛感 ;;
- definitionEn: a strong, regular pulsating movement or feeling, especially one that is accompanied by pain ;;
- example: The throbbing in his sprained ankle got worse when he tried to walk. || 他试着走路时，扭伤的脚踝的抽痛感更强烈了。
- example: She could feel the steady throbbing of the drum against her chest as she stood near the stage. || 她站在舞台附近时，能感受到鼓点稳定的震动传到她胸口。
- example: A dull throbbing in her head kept her awake all night. || 脑袋里隐隐的抽痛让她一整夜都没睡着。

### sense: verb (present participle of throb)
- translationZh: （有规律地）跳动，抽动 ;; （随疼痛）突突跳 ;;
- definitionZh: 动词throb的现在分词形式，指（身体部位、心脏等）有规律地强烈跳动，常伴随疼痛或激动的情绪 ;;
- definitionEn: the present participle of throb, meaning to beat or vibrate with a strong, regular rhythm, especially as a result of pain, excitement, or exertion ;;
- example: His heart was throbbing wildly as he waited for the exam results to be announced. || 他等待考试结果公布时，心脏疯狂地怦怦跳。
- example: The old steam engine was throbbing gently as it pulled out of the station. || 那台老式蒸汽机驶离车站时，轻轻地震动着。
- example: Her temples were throbbing after she cried for almost an hour. || 她哭了快一个小时之后，太阳穴突突地疼。

## word: achieve
- uk: /əˈtʃiːv/
- us: /əˈtʃiːv/
- synonyms: attain || 获得，实现 ;; accomplish || 完成，达成 ;; fulfil || 履行，实现 ;; reach || 达到，抵达 ;;
- antonyms: fail || 失败，未达成 ;; abandon || 放弃，遗弃 ;; forfeit || 丧失，失去 ;;
- phrases: achieve success || 获得成功 ;; achieve a goal || 实现目标 ;; achieve results || 取得成果 ;; achieve recognition || 获得认可 ;;
- collocations: achieve greatly || 取得巨大成就 ;; achieve through hard work || 通过努力实现 ;; achieve one's ambition || 实现抱负 ;; achieve unprecedented progress || 取得前所未有的进步 ;;
- sentencePatterns: achieve sth || 后直接接名词作宾语，表实现/获得某事物 ;; achieve what one set out to do || 接宾语从句，表完成原本计划做的事 ;; it is achieved by doing sth || 被动结构，表某成果通过某种方式取得 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Well done, you've achieved it! || 做得好，你做到了！ ;; It's a great feeling to achieve what you wanted. || 实现自己想要的东西感觉超棒。 ;; You can achieve anything if you put your mind to it. || 只要你用心，什么事都能做成。 ;;
- idioms: achieve the impossible || 完成看似不可能的事，创造奇迹 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 实现，达到 ;; 获得，取得 ;;
- definitionZh: 通过努力、技能或勇气成功完成某件事或获得想要的结果 ;; 经过持续付出后得到某种成就、地位或认可 ;;
- definitionEn: to successfully complete something or get a good result, especially by working hard ;; to gain something such as respect, fame, or an advantage as a result of your efforts ;;
- example: She achieved her dream of becoming a doctor after years of hard study. || 经过多年的刻苦学习，她实现了成为医生的梦想。
- example: The team achieved a remarkable victory in the final match. || 这支队伍在决赛中取得了出色的胜利。
- example: You can achieve a lot if you stay focused and don't give up easily. || 如果你保持专注、不轻易放弃，就能取得很多成就。



## word: abandon
- uk: /əˈbændən/
- us: /əˈbændən/
- synonyms: desert || 抛弃，遗弃 ;; forsake || 舍弃，放弃 ;; discard || 丢弃，抛弃 ;; relinquish || 放弃，放手 ;; renounce || 宣布放弃，断绝关系 ;;
- antonyms: retain || 保留，保持 ;; maintain || 维持，坚守 ;; possess || 拥有，持有 ;;
- phrases: abandon oneself to || 沉湎于，放纵于 ;; with abandon || 尽情地，毫无顾忌地 ;; abandon hope || 放弃希望 ;; abandon ship || 弃船 ;; abandon a project || 放弃项目 ;;
- collocations: completely abandon || 完全放弃 ;; reluctantly abandon || 不情愿地放弃 ;; abandon a plan || 放弃计划 ;; abandon a child || 遗弃儿童 ;; abandon an attempt || 放弃尝试 ;;
- sentencePatterns: abandon + n. || 后接名词作宾语，表示放弃/遗弃某事物或人 ;; abandon + doing sth. || 后接动名词作宾语，表示放弃做某事 ;; abandon oneself to + n./doing sth. || 表示放纵自己陷入某种情绪或行为中 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Abandon ship! || （危急情况下的指令）弃船！；快撤！ ;; Don't abandon hope yet! || 先别放弃希望！ ;; He drank with abandon at the party. || 他在派对上开怀畅饮。 ;;
- idioms: abandon ship || （企业、组织等遇到困难时）撇下他人不管，脱身 ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 放弃，舍弃 ;; 遗弃，抛弃 ;; 中止，停止 ;;
- definitionZh: 指自愿离开自己原本负有责任或义务的人、地方或事物，不再继续持有、从事或支持 ;; 指故意丢弃、遗弃需要照顾的人（如儿童、亲属）或物品 ;; 指中途停止正在进行的活动、计划、尝试等 ;;
- definitionEn: To leave someone or something that you are responsible for, with no intention of returning or taking care of them in the future ;; To stop doing something, especially an activity or plan, before it is finished ;; To stop having a feeling, belief, or attitude ;;
- example: The crew was forced to abandon the sinking ship. || 船员们被迫放弃了正在下沉的船。
- example: He abandoned his research because of lack of funding. || 由于缺乏资金，他放弃了自己的研究。
- example: It is immoral to abandon a newborn baby. || 遗弃新生儿是不道德的行为。

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 放任，放纵 ;; 无拘无束，尽情 ;;
- definitionZh: 指不加克制、不受约束的状态，通常用于描述人尽情释放情绪、毫无顾忌行事的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: A complete lack of inhibition or self-control when you are behaving in an uncontrolled, excited, or enthusiastic way ;;
- example: The children cheered and ran around with wild abandon. || 孩子们尽情欢呼，毫无顾忌地四处奔跑。
- example: She danced with abandon at the celebration, not caring who was watching. || 她在庆祝活动上尽情跳舞，毫不在意谁在看她。
- example: The fans cheered with abandon when their team scored the winning goal. || 当自己支持的球队踢进制胜球时，球迷们肆意欢呼。

## word: accomplish
- uk: /əˈkʌmplɪʃ/
- us: /əˈkɑːmplɪʃ/
- synonyms: achieve || 实现，达成 ;; complete || 完成，结束 ;; fulfill || 履行，满足 ;; attain || 获得，达到 ;; execute || 执行，实施 ;;

- phrases: accomplish a goal || 实现目标 ;; accomplish a task || 完成任务 ;; accomplish nothing || 一事无成 ;; accomplish great feats || 取得伟大功绩 ;;
- collocations: successfully accomplish || 成功完成 ;; hardly accomplish || 难以完成 ;; accomplish sth together || 共同完成某事 ;; accomplish an objective || 达成目标 ;;
- sentencePatterns: accomplish + n. || 后接名词或名词短语，表示完成/实现某事物 ;; accomplish + what/where 等引导的宾语从句 || 后接从句，表示完成某件描述的事情 ;; be accomplished in + n./doing sth. || 表示擅长/精通某领域或做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: You did accomplish a lot! || 你确实做成了不少事！ ;; We can accomplish it together. || 我们一起就能把它做成。 ;; There's nothing you can't accomplish. || 没有你做不成的事。 ;;

- definitionEn: to succeed in finishing something difficult or important that you have been trying to do; to achieve a particular aim or task ;;
- example: The team worked for months to accomplish the project on schedule. || 这个团队工作了数月，按时完成了该项目。

## word: attain
- uk: /əˈteɪn/
- us: /əˈteɪn/

- antonyms: lose || 失去，丢失 ;; fail || 失败，未达成 ;; forfeit || 丧失，失去 ;;
- phrases: attain one's goal || 实现目标 ;; attain success || 获得成功 ;; attain maturity || 达到成熟 ;; attain high status || 获得高地位 ;;
- collocations: attain through hard work || 通过努力获得 ;; attain a high level || 达到高水平 ;; attain a position of power || 获得权位 ;; attain desired results || 取得预期结果 ;;
- sentencePatterns: attain + n. || 后接表示目标、成就、地位等的名词作宾语 ;; attain to + n. || 正式用法，表达到（某状态、级别等） ;;
- spokenExpressions: Attain it step by step! || 一步步去实现它！ ;; You'll attain what you deserve. || 你会得到你应得的。 ;;

### sense: v.

- definitionEn: to succeed in getting or achieving something, especially after a lot of effort; to reach a particular level, age, state etc. ;;
- example: After years of hard work, she finally attained the position of CEO. || 经过多年努力，她终于获得了首席执行官的职位。
- example: The country has attained a 7% economic growth rate this year. || 该国今年实现了7%的经济增长率。
- example: These plants can attain a height of over 2 meters in warm climates. || 在温暖的气候下，这些植物可以长到2米多高。

## word: fail
- uk: /feɪl/
- us: /feɪl/
- synonyms: flunk || （考试、测验等）不及格，通不过 ;; fizzle || 失败，虎头蛇尾地结束 ;; collapse || 失败，垮掉 ;; flop || 砸锅，彻底失败 ;;
- antonyms: succeed || 成功 ;; pass || 通过（考试、检查等） ;; triumph || 获胜，成功 ;;
- phrases: fail to do sth || 未能做某事 ;; fail in sth || 在某方面失败 ;; never fail to do sth || 必定会做某事 ;; without fail || 务必，一定 ;;
- collocations: fail an exam || 考试不及格 ;; fail a test || 测试没通过 ;; fail completely || 彻底失败 ;; fail miserably || 惨败 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb fail to do sth || 主语为人，表示某人没能完成某件事 ;; sth fail sb || 主语为事物，表示某物让某人失望、达不到某人的需求 ;; If sth fails, ... || 条件状语结构，说明某事物失效后的情况 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Words fail me. || 我无语了，我不知道说什么好。 ;; If all else fails... || 实在不行的话，万不得已的话 ;; I failed you. || 我辜负了你。 ;;
- slang: fail || （感叹词）太差劲了，真失败 ;;
- idioms: fail of one's purpose || 达不到目的 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 失败，未能做到；； 不及格，未通过；； 失灵，出故障；； 辜负，使失望
- definitionZh: 没有达到预期的目的、标准或要求；； 在考试、测试等中没有获得合格的成绩；； 设备、系统等无法正常工作；； 没有满足他人的期望，让他人失望
- definitionEn: To not succeed in achieving a goal, meeting a standard, or fulfilling a requirement; To not achieve a passing grade in an exam, test, or course; A device, system, etc. stops working properly; To not meet someone's expectations and make them feel disappointed
- example: He failed to finish the project before the deadline. || 他没能在截止日期前完成这个项目。
- example: My car failed on the highway this morning, so I was late for work. || 我的车今天早上在高速上出故障了，所以我上班迟到了。
- example: I don't want to fail my parents who have supported me for so many years. || 我不想辜负这么多年来一直支持我的父母。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 失败，失利；； （考试）不及格
- definitionZh: 不成功的结果；； 考试未通过的情况
- definitionEn: An unsuccessful result or outcome; A situation where someone does not pass an exam or test
- example: The project was a total fail because of poor planning. || 由于规划不当，这个项目彻底失败了。
- example: He got a fail in the final math exam and had to take a make-up test. || 他数学期末考试不及格，不得不参加补考。

## word: fulfil
- uk: /fʊlˈfɪl/
- us: /fʊlˈfɪl/
- synonyms: accomplish || 完成，实现 ;; satisfy || 满足，使满意 ;; achieve || 达到，获得 ;; perform || 执行，履行 ;; meet || 满足，符合 ;;
- antonyms: fail || 失败，未做到 ;; neglect || 疏忽，不履行 ;; abandon || 放弃，抛弃 ;;
