- collocations: fully fulfil || 完全履行 ;; successfully fulfil || 成功实现 ;; fail to fulfil || 未能履行 ;; fulfil a contract || 履行合同 ;; fulfil a role || 发挥作用 ;;
- sentencePatterns: fulfil + noun || 后接名词作宾语，表示履行、实现某事物 ;; fulfil sb + (of sth) || 表示满足某人的某种需求、愿望 ;; be fulfilled || 被动结构，表示被履行、被满足，也可指人感到满足 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'll fulfil my end of the deal || 我会履行我这部分的约定 ;; Did you fulfil all the entry requirements? || 你满足所有的入学要求了吗？ ;; It feels great to finally fulfil a long-held goal || 终于实现了一个长期的目标，感觉太棒了 ;;
- slang:
- idioms:

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 履行，执行 ;; 实现，达到 ;; 满足，使满意 ;; 发挥，发扬 ;;
- definitionZh: 做到自己承诺、有责任去做的事 ;; 实现想要达成的愿望、目标、梦想等 ;; 符合、满足某种要求、条件或者他人的需求 ;; 使某人充分发挥能力、潜力，获得成就感 ;;
- definitionEn: to do something that you have promised or are expected to do ;; to achieve something that you wanted to do ;; to satisfy a need, requirement, or condition ;; to make someone feel happy and satisfied because they are using their abilities and qualities ;;
- example: We need to fulfil all the terms of the contract. || 我们需要履行合同的所有条款。
- example: She worked hard for years to fulfil her dream of becoming a doctor. || 她努力了多年，实现了成为一名医生的梦想。

## word: across
- uk: /əˈkrɒs/
- us: /əˈkrɔːs/
- synonyms: crosswise || 交叉地；横过 ;; from side to side || 从一边到另一边 ;; throughout || 遍及；到处 ;; opposite || 在对面 ;;
- antonyms: along || 沿着 ;; alongside || 沿着旁边 ;;
- phrases: across from || 在…对面 ;; come across || 偶然遇见；无意中发现 ;; get across || 讲清楚；使被理解 ;; cut across || 抄近路穿过；超越 ;; run across || 偶然碰到；跑过 ;;
- collocations: walk across || 步行穿过 ;; swim across || 游过 ;; across the country || 遍及全国 ;; across the board || 全面地；包括一切地 ;; across the street || 在街对面 ;;
- sentencePatterns: prep. It is + 距离 + across sth. || 说明某物的横向长度是多少 ;; adv. sb. + verb + across + 状语 || 说明某人做某事时是横跨着进行的 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Across the board, everyone has to follow the rules. || 所有人都得遵守规则，没有例外。 ;; How do I get across to the other side of the river? || 我怎么才能到河对岸去？ ;; I came across your old photo yesterday. || 我昨天碰巧看到你的旧照片了。 ;;
- idioms: across the board || 全面的；适用于所有情况的 ;;
- slang: （无）

### sense: 介词 (prep.)
- translationZh: 从一边到另一边，横过；在…对面；遍及，在…各处；
- definitionZh: 从某物的一边延伸到另一边；在某个区域的对面位置；覆盖某个区域的全部范围；
- definitionEn: from one side of something to the other; on the opposite side of a particular area; existing or happening in every part of a particular area;
- example: She walked across the park to meet her friend. || 她穿过公园去见她的朋友。
- example: There's a supermarket just across the street. || 街对面就有一家超市。
- example: The news spread across the whole city within hours. || 这条消息几个小时内就传遍了整座城市。

### sense: 副词 (adv.)
- translationZh: 从一边到另一边；在对面，向对面；宽；
- definitionZh: 表示从一个边到另一个边的动作或位置；表示朝向对面的方向；用于描述物体的宽度；
- definitionEn: from one side to the other side of something; towards or on the opposite side of an area; used to say how wide something is;
- example: The river is 100 metres across at its narrowest point. || 这条河最窄的地方有100米宽。
- example: When I saw him on the other side of the road, I shouted to him to come across. || 我看到他在路对面的时候，喊他过来。
- example: The bridge was destroyed, so we couldn't get across. || 桥被毁了，所以我们过不去。



## word: along
- uk: /əˈlɒŋ/
- us: /əˈlɔːŋ/
- synonyms: alongside || 沿着，靠着 ;; forward || 向前 ;; onward || 向前，前进 ;; together || 一起，一同 ;; abreast || 并肩，并排 ;;
- antonyms: across || 横过，穿过 ;; opposite || 在对面 ;; backward || 向后 ;;
- phrases: along with || 和…一起，随同 ;; get along || 相处融洽，进展 ;; come along || 出现，一起来 ;; all along || 一直，自始至终 ;; go along || 赞同，陪同前往 ;;
- collocations: walk along || 沿着…走 ;; drive along || 沿着…开车 ;; run along || 走开，沿着…跑 ;; bring along || 带来，带上 ;; move along || 往前走，向前移动 ;;
- sentencePatterns: 主语 + 谓语 + along + 地点名词 || 表示“沿着某个地点做动作” ;; 主语 + 谓语 + along + with + 宾语 || 表示“和…一起做某事” ;; It is + 形容词 + to get along with sb || 表示“和某人相处是…的” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Come along! || 快点！来吧！ ;; Move along, please. || 请往前走。 ;; How are you getting along? || 你最近过得怎么样？ ;;

### sense: 介词

- definitionZh: 表示顺着某个线性的路线前进或存在 ;; 表示在某物的边缘位置 ;;
- definitionEn: following the length or direction of a line, road, river etc. ;; next to the edge of something long ;;
- example: We walked along the beach at sunset. || 日落时分我们沿着海滩散步。
- example: There are many shops along the main street. || 主街上有很多商店。
- example: The little boy was running along the river bank. || 那个小男孩正沿着河岸跑。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 向前 ;; 一起，一同 ;; 进展 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示向前移动的状态 ;; 表示和他人一同进行某个活动 ;; 表示某事的进展情况 ;;
- definitionEn: moving forward ;; in the company of someone else ;; used to talk about how well something is progressing ;;
- example: The project is coming along very well. || 这个项目进展得非常顺利。
- example: I brought my sister along to the party. || 我带我妹妹一起来参加派对了。
- example: She waved and drove along without stopping. || 她挥了挥手，没有停车继续往前开了。

## word: alongside

- us: /əˌlɔːŋˈsaɪd/

- example: The two boats moored alongside. || 两艘船并排停泊着。

## word: crosswise
- uk: /ˈkrɒswaɪz/
- us: /ˈkrɔːswaɪz/
- synonyms: transversely || 横向地，横断地 ;; diagonally || 对角地，斜向地 ;; athwart || 横跨地，横穿地 ;; sidewise || 向侧面地，横向地 ;; obliquely || 倾斜地，斜交地 ;;
- antonyms: lengthwise || 纵向地，纵长地 ;; vertically || 垂直地，竖直地 ;; longitudinally || 纵向地，经度方向地 ;;
- phrases: cut crosswise || 横向切割 ;; lay crosswise || 横向放置 ;; crosswise arrangement || 交叉排列 ;; crosswise intersection || 十字交叉口 ;; crosswise movement || 横向运动 ;;
- collocations: run crosswise || 横向延伸 ;; fold crosswise || 十字交叉折叠 ;; crosswise pattern || 交叉纹样 ;; crosswise force || 横向力 ;; crosswise comparison || 横向对比 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sth. is placed crosswise. || 某物被横向/交叉放置 ;; Sth. runs crosswise to sth. || 某物与另一物呈交叉方向延伸 ;; Do sth. crosswise to achieve a certain effect. || 以交叉/横向的方式做某事以达到特定效果 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Lay it crosswise, will you? || 把它横着放，行吗？ ;; Don't cut that log crosswise yet. || 先别横着砍那根木头。 ;; The path goes crosswise right through the field. || 这条路斜着直接穿过整片田野。 ;;
- idioms: crosswise to sth. || 与…相抵触，与…相悖 ;;

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 横向地，横断地 ;; 对角地，斜向地 ;; 交叉地 ;; 与…相反地，相抵触地 ;;
- definitionZh: 沿着与物体长度或常规方向成直角的方向；呈对角方向延伸或放置；以交叉的姿态；与某个目标、规则或预期方向相反的状态。 ;;
- definitionEn: In a direction at right angles to the length of something or to a usual direction; extending or placed in a diagonal direction; in a crossing or intersecting position; in a way that goes against a goal, rule, or expected direction. ;;
- example: Fold the sheet crosswise before putting it into the drawer. || 把床单十字交叉折叠后再放进抽屉。
- example: The fence was built crosswise across the path to stop hikers from entering the restricted area. || 围栏横穿小路搭建，阻止徒步旅行者进入管制区域。
- example: His suggestion went crosswise to the original plan we had agreed on last week. || 他的提议和我们上周商定的原有方案相抵触。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 横向的，交叉的 ;; 对角的，斜穿的 ;;
- definitionZh: 呈现交叉、横向或对角方向的，与常规纵向走向成角度的。 ;;
- definitionEn: Having a crossing, transverse, or diagonal direction, forming an angle with the usual longitudinal orientation. ;;
- example: The crosswise stripes on the shirt make the wearer look a little wider. || 衬衫上的横向条纹让穿的人看起来稍微显胖一点。
- example: The worker marked a crosswise line on the wooden board to guide the cutting. || 工人在木板上画了一条横向的线来指引切割。
- example: We need to add a few crosswise supports to make the shelf more stable. || 我们需要加几根横向支撑，让架子更稳固。

## word: from side to side
- uk: /frəm saɪd tuː saɪd/
- us: /frʌm saɪd tuː saɪd/
- synonyms: back and forth || 来回地，往复地 ;; side to side || 左右地 ;; to and fro || 来来往往地 ;;
- antonyms: straight ahead || 径直向前 ;; motionlessly || 静止不动地 ;;
- phrases: shake from side to side || 左右摇晃 ;; nod from side to side || 左右摇头（表示否定） ;; sweep from side to side || 左右扫视 ;; swing from side to side || 左右摆动 ;;
- collocations: move from side to side || 左右移动 ;; rock from side to side || 左右晃动 ;; turn one's head from side to side || 左右转头 ;; wag one's tail from side to side || 尾巴左右摇摆 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb/sth + move/shake + from side to side || 描述人/物做出左右移动、摇晃的动作 ;; sb + look/scan + from side to side + 状语 || 描述人左右张望、扫视的状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Shake your head from side to side if you don't agree. || 如果你不同意就左右摇摇头。 ;; The sign says you should look from side to side before crossing the road. || 标识说过马路前要左右看看。 ;; I was so nervous I kept rocking from side to side on my feet. || 我太紧张了，脚一直来回晃着站不稳。 ;;
- idioms: sway from side to side || （意见、立场）左右摇摆，犹豫不决 ;;

### sense: 副词短语
- translationZh: 左右地；来回地；从一边到另一边 ;;
- definitionZh: 描述动作在物体或空间的左右两侧之间反复发生的状态；也可引申为立场、意见在不同选项之间摇摆不定 ;; 表示位置或动作的范围覆盖两个相对的侧边之间的区域 ;;
- definitionEn: describes a state where an action happens repeatedly between the left and right sides of an object or space; can also be extended to mean that one's position or opinion wavers between different options ;; indicates that the scope of a position or action covers the area between two opposite sides ;;
- example: The pendulum of the old clock swung slowly from side to side. || 旧钟的钟摆慢悠悠地左右摆动。
- example: When I asked if he wanted to eat spicy food, he shook his head from side to side immediately. || 我问他想不想吃辣的时候，他立刻左右摇了摇头。
- example: The referee waved the flag from side to side to signal that the goal was invalid. || 裁判左右挥舞着旗帜，示意进球无效。
- example: Don't sway from side to side on this issue—you need to give us a clear answer. || 在这个问题上别左右摇摆了，你得给我们一个明确的答复。

## word: throughout

- spokenExpressions: Throughout the whole thing, I was so nervous. || 整件事过程中我都特别紧张。 ;; It rained throughout our trip, which was such a bummer. || 我们旅行全程都在下雨，太扫兴了。 ;; The event was fun throughout, I really enjoyed it. || 活动从头到尾都很好玩，我特别喜欢。 ;;

- example: The material is waterproof throughout, so you don't need to worry about getting wet. || 这种材料整体都防水，所以你不用担心会被淋湿。

## word: act
- uk: /ækt/
- us: /ækt/
- synonyms: perform || 执行，表演 ;; behave || 表现 ;; deed || 行为，行动 ;; function || 起作用 ;; operation || 行动，操作 ;;
- antonyms: refrain || 克制，避免 ;; inaction || 不行动，无为 ;; cease || 停止，终止 ;;
- phrases: act as || 担任，充当 ;; act on || 按照…行事，对…起作用 ;; act out || 把…表演出来，付诸行动 ;; act up || 出毛病，调皮捣蛋 ;; in the act of || 正在做…的时候 ;;
- collocations: act decisively || 果断行动 ;; act responsibly || 负责任地行事 ;; criminal act || 犯罪行为 ;; brave act || 勇敢的行为 ;; act in accordance with || 依照…行事 ;;
- sentencePatterns: act + as + 职位/角色 || 表示担任某种角色或发挥某种功能 ;; act + on/upon + 建议/信息 || 表示根据某种信息、建议采取行动 ;; act + 副词(方式状语) || 描述行动的方式、状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Act your age! || 别那么孩子气！举止要符合你的年龄！ ;; Act fast! || 赶紧行动！ ;; Don't act like you don't know! || 别装得你好像不知道似的！ ;;
- idioms: act of God || 不可抗力，天灾 ;; get in on the act || 插手，参与（ profitable的活动） ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 行动 ;; 表演 ;; 起作用 ;; 表现 ;;
- definitionZh: 采取行动做某事；在戏剧、影视中扮演角色表演；（机器、药物等）发挥功能、产生效果；以某种方式表现、举止 ;;
- definitionEn: to take action to do something; to perform a role in a play, film or other performance; (of a machine, medicine etc.) to function or produce an effect; to behave in a particular way ;;
- example: We need to act immediately to stop the spread of the virus. || 我们需要立即行动以阻止病毒传播。
- example: She acted the role of Juliet in the school play last semester. || 她上学期在学校戏剧里饰演朱丽叶这个角色。
- example: The medicine will start to act in about half an hour, so you'll feel better soon. || 这个药大约半小时后会开始起效，所以你很快就会舒服些了。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 行为，行动 ;; 法案，法令 ;; （戏剧的）一幕 ;; 表演 ;;
- definitionZh: 具体做的某件事、行为；议会通过的正式法律、法案；戏剧作品中划分的段落；故意做出来的虚假表现、表演 ;;
- definitionEn: a particular thing that someone does; a formal law passed by a parliament; one of the main parts into which a play is divided; a way of behaving that is not genuine and is intended to make people believe something that is not true ;;
- example: Helping the elderly cross the road is a kind act that everyone should appreciate. || 扶老人过马路是值得所有人赞赏的善意行为。
- example: The government has passed a new act to protect the rights of disabled people. || 政府已经通过了一项保护残疾人权利的新法案。
- example: The most dramatic scene appears in the third act of the classic tragedy. || 最具戏剧性的场景出现在这部经典悲剧的第三幕。



## word: behave
- uk: /bɪˈheɪv/
- us: /bɪˈheɪv/
- synonyms: act || 表现，行动 ;; conduct || 表现，行事 ;; comport || 举止，表现 ;;
- antonyms: misbehave || 行为不端，失礼 ;; act up || 调皮捣蛋，出毛病 ;;
- phrases: behave well || 表现良好 ;; behave badly || 表现恶劣 ;; behave oneself || 守规矩，听话 ;;
- collocations: behave properly || 举止得体 ;; behave politely || 举止礼貌 ;; behave aggressively || 表现得咄咄逼人 ;;
- sentencePatterns: behave + adverb || 说明：描述行为的方式，后接修饰动作的副词 ;; behave + (towards sb) + prepositional phrase || 说明：描述对某人的行为态度，后接表示对象的介词短语 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Behave yourself! || 规矩点！ ;; They behaved perfectly. || 他们表现得好极了。 ;; How's the new car behaving? || 新车用着怎么样？ ;;
- idioms: behave as if you own the place || 表现得就像这地方是你的一样，举止嚣张放肆 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 表现 ;; 举止得体 ;; （机器、设备等）运行，工作 ;;
- definitionZh: 以特定的方式行事，表现出某种行为 ;; 举止得当，遵守社会规范或他人要求 ;; 机器、设备等正常发挥功能，稳定运行 ;;
- definitionEn: to act in a particular way, especially towards other people ;; to behave in a way that people think is correct and acceptable ;; if a machine, substance etc behaves in a particular way, it works or reacts in that way ;;
- example: She always behaves well when her grandparents come to visit. || 她祖父母来做客的时候她总是表现得很好。
- example: The children were told to behave themselves at the museum. || 孩子们被告知在博物馆里要守规矩。
- example: My old laptop is behaving strangely lately — it keeps crashing for no reason. || 我的旧笔记本最近运行得很奇怪，总是毫无缘由地崩溃。

## word: deed
- uk: /diːd/
- us: /diːd/
- synonyms: act || 行为，行动 ;; action || 行为，举动 ;; feat || 功绩，壮举 ;; accomplishment || 成就，成绩 ;;
- antonyms: misdeed || 恶行，罪行 ;; wrongdoing || 不端行为，坏事 ;;
- phrases: good deed || 善行，好事 ;; evil deed || 恶行，劣迹 ;; title deed || 地契，所有权凭证 ;; deed of trust || 信托契约 ;;
- collocations: noble deed || 高尚的行为 ;; brave deed || 勇敢的事迹 ;; do a deed || 做一件事 ;; heroic deed || 英雄事迹 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + adj. + of sb. to do such a deed || 用于评价某人的行为性质 ;; One's deeds speak louder than one's words || 用于表达行动比言语更有说服力 ;;
- spokenExpressions: A good deed deserves to be rewarded. || 善举理应得到回报。 ;; Deeds, not words. || 要行动，不要空话。 ;;
- idioms: in deed as well as in name || 名副其实，表里如一 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 行为，行动 ;; 功绩，事迹 ;; 契约，证书 ;;
- definitionZh: 人所做出的具体行为或行动； ;; 值得称赞的、有影响力的成就或事迹； ;; 证明财产、权利等所属的正式法律文件。 ;;
- definitionEn: A specific action or act performed by a person. ;; An achievement or action that is worthy of praise and attention. ;; An official legal document that proves ownership of property or rights. ;;
- example: He is remembered for his selfless deeds during the war. || 他因战争期间的无私事迹被人们铭记。
- example: We should judge people by their deeds, not just their words. || 我们评判人应该看他们的行动，而不只是言语。
- example: The lawyer kept the deed to the house in a safe. || 律师把房产契约保存在保险箱里。
- example: Doing a good deed every day can make you feel more positive. || 每天做一件善事会让你感觉更积极。

### sense: v.
- translationZh: 立契转让（财产等） ;;
- definitionZh: 通过签署正式契约的方式将财产或权利转让给他人。 ;;
- definitionEn: To transfer property or rights to someone by signing an official deed. ;;
- example: He decided to deed the family farm to his youngest son. || 他决定把家族农场立契转让给他的小儿子。
- example: The land was deeded to the local government for public use. || 这块土地被立契转让给当地政府作公共用途。

## word: inaction
- uk: /ɪnˈækʃn/
- us: /ɪnˈækʃn/
- synonyms: idleness || 懒散，无所事事 ;; passivity || 被动，消极 ;; inactivity || 不活动，停滞 ;; stagnation || 停滞，不发展 ;; inertia || 惰性，惯性 ;;
- antonyms: action || 行动，行动过程 ;; activity || 活动，活跃 ;; intervention || 干预，介入 ;;
- phrases: government inaction || 政府不作为 ;; policy inaction || 政策停滞 ;; collective inaction || 集体不作为 ;; costly inaction || 代价高昂的不作为 ;;
- collocations: accuse sb of inaction || 指责某人不作为 ;; condemn inaction || 谴责不作为 ;; result from inaction || 由不作为导致 ;; end years of inaction || 结束多年的停滞状态 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The criticism over + n. + for inaction is growing. || 针对某主体不作为的批评日益增多 ;; Inaction on + issue + will lead to + negative consequence. || 在某问题上的不作为将导致负面后果 ;; There is growing pressure on sb to address the problem of inaction. || 要求某人解决不作为问题的压力越来越大 ;;
- spokenExpressions: No more inaction, okay? || 别再不作为了，好吗？ ;; We can't afford this inaction any longer. || 我们再也承担不起这种不作为的代价了 ;; His inaction on this matter is really frustrating. || 他在这件事上的不作为真的很让人恼火 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 不作为 ;; 不行动，无行动 ;; 停滞 ;;
- definitionZh: 指没有采取必要的行动、措施去应对或解决某件事的状态 ;; 缺乏主动行动、处理问题的行为的情况 ;;
- definitionEn: The failure to take action or measures that are necessary to deal with a problem or situation. ;; A state of not doing anything to address issues that require attention. ;;
- example: Environmental groups have strongly criticized the government's inaction on climate change. || 环保组织强烈批评政府在气候变化问题上的不作为。
- example: The company's inaction over the safety hazard eventually led to a serious industrial accident. || 该公司对安全隐患的不作为最终导致了一起严重的工业事故。
- example: Many residents are angry about the local council's inaction in repairing the damaged public facilities. || 许多居民对地方议会在修复受损公共设施方面的不作为感到愤怒。

- example: The new computer system performs much faster than the old one. || 这套新的电脑系统运转起来比旧的快得多。

## word: refrain
- uk: /rɪˈfreɪn/
- us: /rɪˈfreɪn/
- synonyms: abstain || 戒除，避免 ;; desist || 停止，克制 ;; forbear || 克制，忍耐 ;; avoid || 避免，避开 ;; hold back || 抑制，忍住 ;;
- antonyms: indulge || 沉溺，放纵 ;; commit || 从事，做（不当行为） ;; persist || 坚持，执意 ;;
- phrases: refrain from || 抑制，避免 ;; choral refrain || 合唱副歌 ;; popular refrain || 常见论调，流行副歌 ;; recurring refrain || 反复出现的话题/副歌 ;;
- collocations: refrain from smoking || 禁止吸烟，克制不吸烟 ;; refrain from comment || 不发表评论 ;; sing the refrain || 唱副歌 ;; hear a familiar refrain || 听到熟悉的论调/副歌 ;;
- sentencePatterns: refrain from (doing) sth || 表示克制不做某事的固定结构 ;; sb would do well to refrain from sth || 用来建议某人最好不要做某事 ;; the refrain of sth is that... || 用来引出某类反复出现的观点/内容 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Please refrain from that! || 请别那么做！ ;; I had to refrain from laughing. || 我强忍着才没笑出来。 ;; That's a refrain I hear all the time. || 这话我都听腻了。 ;;
- idioms: a familiar refrain || 老生常谈，老调重弹 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 克制，避免 ;; 忍住，戒除 ;;
- definitionZh: 有意识地控制自己不做某件想做或可能做的事 ;; 主动停止或避免某种行为 ;;
- definitionEn: to stop oneself from doing something, especially something that you want to do ;; to avoid or stop doing an action deliberately ;;
- example: Please refrain from using your mobile phone during the flight. || 请在飞行途中不要使用手机。
- example: He refrained from making any rude remarks even when he was provoked. || 即使被激怒了，他也忍住没有说任何粗鲁的话。
- example: Doctors advise patients to refrain from alcohol after the surgery. || 医生建议病人术后不要饮酒。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: （歌曲的）副歌，叠句 ;; 反复说的话，老调 ;;
- definitionZh: 歌曲中重复演唱的部分，通常在每段主歌之后 ;; 被人反复提及的观点、抱怨或话题 ;;
- definitionEn: a part of a song that is repeated, usually after each verse ;; a comment or complaint that is often repeated ;;
- example: The audience joined in to sing the refrain of the hit song. || 观众一起跟着唱这首热门歌曲的副歌。
- example: The refrain among employees is that the company needs better welfare policies. || 员工们反复提及的诉求是公司需要更好的福利政策。
- example: The poem uses a simple refrain to emphasize its main theme. || 这首诗用了简单的叠句来突出核心主题。

## word: action
- uk: /ˈækʃən/
- us: /ˈækʃən/
- synonyms: deed || 行为；行动 ;; act || 行为；举动 ;; operation || 操作；运作 ;; activity || 活动 ;; measure || 措施 ;;
- antonyms: inaction || 不作为；不活动 ;; rest || 休息；静止 ;; idleness || 懒惰；闲散 ;;
- phrases: take action || 采取行动 ;; action movie || 动作电影 ;; out of action || 失灵；无法工作 ;; in action || 在活动中；在起作用 ;; call to action || 行动号召 ;;
- collocations: immediate action || 立即行动 ;; decisive action || 果断行动 ;; legal action || 法律诉讼 ;; military action || 军事行动 ;; corrective action || 纠正措施 ;;
- sentencePatterns: take action to do sth. || 表示“采取行动做某事”的结构 ;; sth. be put into action || 表示“某事被付诸实施”的被动结构 ;; call for action on sth. || 表示“呼吁针对某事采取行动”的结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Actions speak louder than words. || 事实胜于雄辩。 ;; Let's get this action started! || 咱们开始干吧！ ;; You're all talk, no action. || 你只会光说不练。 ;;
- idioms: bring/put sth into action || 把某事付诸实施 ;; a piece of the action || 分一杯羹；参与获利 ;;

### sense: n.（名词）
- translationZh: 行动；行为 ;; 动作；活动 ;; 诉讼 ;; 作用 ;; 情节 ;;
- definitionZh: 人或团体为实现某个目的而做出的具体行为或开展的活动 ;; 身体做出的动作、肢体活动 ;; 针对某一问题向法院提起的法律诉讼程序 ;; 某事物对其他事物产生的影响、效用 ;; 故事、影视等作品的情节发展脉络 ;;
- definitionEn: The specific behavior or activities carried out by a person or group to achieve a certain purpose ;; Physical movements or activities performed by the body ;; A legal process filed in court to address a particular issue ;; The effect or influence that one thing has on another ;; The plot development sequence of a story, film or other work ;;
- example: The government promised to take immediate action to reduce air pollution. || 政府承诺立即采取行动减少空气污染。
- example: The doctor is studying the action of this new drug on the human body. || 医生正在研究这种新药对人体的作用。
- example: He decided to file a legal action against the company for unfair dismissal. || 他决定以不公平解雇为由对该公司提起法律诉讼。

### sense: v.（动词）
- translationZh: 对…采取行动；处理 ;; 起诉 ;;
- definitionZh: 针对某件事或某个问题采取相应的措施进行处理 ;; 就某一纠纷向法院提起诉讼 ;;
- definitionEn: To take corresponding measures to deal with a matter or problem ;; To file a lawsuit in court over a dispute ;;
- example: The manager will action your request as soon as possible. || 经理会尽快处理你的请求。
- example: The company decided to action the breach of contract by its supplier. || 该公司决定对供应商的违约行为提起诉讼。
- example: The local council has promised to action the residents' complaints about road damage. || 地方议会承诺会处理居民关于道路破损的投诉。



## word: act
- uk: /ækt/
- us: /ækt/
- synonyms: perform || 执行，表演 ;; behave || 表现 ;; deed || 行为，行动 ;; function || 起作用，行使职责 ;;
- antonyms: refrain || 克制，避免 ;; omit || 省略，不做 ;;
- phrases: act as || 担任，充当 ;; act on || 按照…行事，对…起作用 ;; act out || 将…表演出来，付诸行动 ;; act up || 出毛病，调皮捣蛋 ;;
- collocations: act quickly || 迅速行动 ;; act responsibly || 负责任地行事 ;; act a part || 扮演一个角色 ;; act with caution || 谨慎行事 ;;
- sentencePatterns: act + (adv/prep phrase) || 表示行动/表现的方式或对象 ;; act as + 身份/角色 || 表示充当某种角色 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Act now! || 现在就行动！ ;; Act your age! || 举止成熟点，别孩子气！ ;; You acted wisely. || 你做得很明智。 ;;
- idioms: act of God || 不可抗力，天灾 ;; catch sb in the act || 当场抓住某人（做坏事） ;;

### sense: v.（动词）
- translationZh: 行动；做事 ;; 扮演；表演 ;; 表现；举止 ;; 起作用；生效 ;;
- definitionZh: 采取行动来完成某件事；为达成某个目的做出行为 ;; 在戏剧、影视中饰演某个角色，进行表演 ;; 以特定的方式表现出自己的行为举止 ;; 某物产生预期的效果、发挥功能 ;;
- definitionEn: To take action in order to achieve something or do a particular task ;; To perform a role in a play, film, or other performance ;; To behave in a particular way ;; To have the effect or function that is expected ;;
- example: We need to act immediately to solve this problem. || 我们需要立即采取行动解决这个问题。
- example: She acted the role of Juliet in the school play. || 她在校园戏剧里饰演朱丽叶这个角色。
- example: The medicine acts quickly to relieve pain. || 这种药能快速起效缓解疼痛。

### sense: n.（名词）

- definitionZh: 人所做出的具体的行为、举动 ;; 由立法机构正式通过的法律文件 ;; 戏剧等演出中划分的段落单元 ;;
- definitionEn: A particular thing that someone does ;; A formal law that has been officially passed by a government or legislative body ;; One of the main parts into which a play, opera, etc. is divided ;;
- example: Helping the elderly cross the road is a kind act. || 扶老人过马路是一个善良的举动。
- example: The government passed a new act to protect endangered animals. || 政府通过了一项保护濒危动物的新法案。
- example: The first act of the play was a bit boring, but the rest was wonderful. || 这部剧的第一幕有点无聊，但剩下的部分很精彩。

- uk: /ɪnˈækʃn/

- example: He was criticized for his inaction when the team was facing a critical crisis. || 他因在团队面临重大危机时不作为而受到批评。

## word: operation
- uk: /ˌɒpəˈreɪʃn/
- us: /ˌɑːpəˈreɪʃn/

- antonyms: inaction || 不活动，不作为 ;; malfunction || 故障，失灵 ;;
- phrases: military operation || 军事行动 ;; surgical operation || 外科手术 ;; business operation || 业务运营 ;; rescue operation || 救援行动 ;;
- collocations: perform an operation || 实施手术/操作 ;; run daily operations || 管理日常运营 ;; launch an operation || 发起行动/项目 ;; resume operation || 恢复运营 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The operation of + 机构/设备 + is + 形容词 || 用于描述某机构、设备的运行状态 ;; Sb + perform/carry out + an operation + on sb || 用于描述医生给病人做手术的场景 ;; The company + has expanded its operations + to + 地点 || 用于描述企业拓展业务范围的情况 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Is the operation going smoothly? || 手术/操作进展顺利吗？ ;; The factory is back in operation now. || 工厂现在恢复运营了。 ;; We need to coordinate the whole operation. || 我们得协调整个行动的安排。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 操作，运作 ;; 手术 ;; 行动，活动 ;; 运算 ;;
- definitionZh: 机器、系统、组织等运行或发挥功能的过程 ;; 医生为病人切除病变部位、修复器官等的医疗程序 ;; 有组织、有特定目的的军事、救援等行动 ;; 数学中的加减乘除等计算过程 ;;
- definitionEn: The process of a machine, system, or organization working or fulfilling its function ;; A medical procedure in which a doctor cuts into a patient's body to remove a damaged part or repair an organ ;; An organized activity with a specific purpose, especially military or rescue missions ;; A calculation process such as addition, subtraction, multiplication and division in mathematics ;;
- example: The regular maintenance ensures the smooth operation of the production line. || 定期维护确保了生产线的平稳运作。
- example: The doctor decided to perform an emergency operation on the patient who suffered a heart attack. || 医生决定给这位心脏病发作的病人做急诊手术。
- example: The police launched a special operation to crack down on online fraud. || 警方发起了一项打击网络诈骗的专项行动。
- example: Primary school students first learn the four basic operations: addition, subtraction, multiplication and division. || 小学生首先学习加减乘除这四种基本运算。

## word: rest
- uk: /rest/
- us: /rest/
- synonyms: repose || 休息，休憩 ;; relaxation || 放松，松弛 ;; break || 休息时间，间歇 ;; pause || 暂停，停顿 ;; residue || 剩余物，残余 ;;
- antonyms: work || 工作，劳动 ;; exertion || 费力，劳累 ;; activity || 活动，活跃 ;;
- phrases: rest on || 依靠，依赖；基于 ;; rest up || 充分休息，养精蓄锐 ;; the rest of || ……的其余部分 ;; rest assured || 放心，确信 ;; at rest || 静止的；安息的 ;;
- collocations: get some rest || 休息一下 ;; need rest || 需要休息 ;; adequate rest || 充足的休息 ;; rest one's case || （律）陈述完毕，停止举证 ;; rest one's eyes || 让眼睛休息 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is important to rest after + doing sth || 做某事之后休息很重要 ;; The rest of + n. + be + adj./v-ed || 剩余的……处于某种状态/被做了某事 ;; sb rest + adj./prep. phrase || 某人处于某种休息/静止状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Give it a rest! || 别闹了！消停点！ ;; Rest easy! || 放心吧！别担心！ ;; You need to get some rest. || 你得休息会儿。 ;;
- idioms: rest on one's laurels || 吃老本，满足于已有的成绩 ;; rest on one's oars || 暂停努力，歇口气 ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 休息，歇息；停靠，倚靠；取决于，在于；使休息，使轻松 ;;
- definitionZh: 暂停工作、运动或活动以恢复体力或精力；将某物靠在或放在某个支撑物上；某件事由某个因素决定、取决于；让身体或身体部位停止活动以恢复状态 ;;
- definitionEn: To stop working, exercising or doing an activity in order to recover strength or energy; to place something against or on a support for stability; to be dependent or based on a particular factor; to allow your body or a part of your body to stop being active in order to recover. ;;
- example: You should rest for a few days after the surgery. || 手术后你应该休息几天。
- example: The success of the project rests on the cooperation of all team members. || 这个项目的成功取决于所有团队成员的合作。
- example: She rested her head on his shoulder and fell asleep quickly. || 她把头靠在他的肩膀上，很快就睡着了。

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 休息，睡眠；剩余部分，其余的人；静止，停歇；支撑物，支架 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于恢复精力的休息或睡眠时间；剩下的人、事物或部分；没有活动或移动的静止状态；用于支撑某物的结构或装置 ;;
- definitionEn: A period of time when you sleep or relax in order to get back your energy; the remaining parts of something or the remaining people in a group; the state of not being active or moving; a structure or object that is used to support something. ;;
- example: Make sure you get plenty of rest before the final exam. || 期末考试前你要确保充足的休息。
- example: I will finish the rest of the report tomorrow morning. || 我明天早上会完成剩余的报告内容。
- example: The seat has a comfortable arm rest for long journeys. || 这个座椅有舒适的扶手，适合长途出行。

## word: active
- uk: /ˈæktɪv/
- us: /ˈæktɪv/

- antonyms: inactive || 不活跃的 ;; passive || 被动的 ;; idle || 懒散的 ;;
- phrases: active participation || 积极参与 ;; active role || 积极作用 ;; active duty || 现役 ;; active voice || 主动语态 ;;
- collocations: socially active || 社交活跃的 ;; physically active || 爱运动的 ;; active member || 活跃成员 ;; active support || 大力支持 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be active in (doing) sth. || 表示“在（做）某事方面很积极” ;; remain/stay active || 表示“保持活跃状态” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Stay active! || 保持活力！ ;; Be active about it! || 主动点！ ;;
- idioms: active on all fronts || 全线出击，多面活跃 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 活跃的；积极的 ;; 主动的；起作用的 ;;
- definitionZh: 喜欢参与活动、精力充沛的；态度积极、愿意付出努力的 ;; 不处于被动状态，能发挥作用、产生效果的 ;;
- definitionEn: engaging or ready to engage in physically energetic pursuits; willing to take action and participate actively ;; not passive or inert; functioning or capable of functioning ;;
- example: She's very active in the local community centre. || 她在当地社区中心非常活跃。
- example: Taking an active part in group discussions can improve your communication skills. || 积极参与小组讨论能提升你的沟通能力。
- example: The volcano is still active, so local residents have to stay alert. || 这座火山仍然处于活跃状态，因此当地居民必须保持警惕。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 主动语态 ;;
- definitionZh: 语法中表示主语是动作发出者的语态形式 ;;
- definitionEn: the form of a verb in which the subject is the person or thing that performs the action ;;
- example: In writing, using the active often makes your sentences clearer and more direct. || 写作时使用主动语态通常会让你的句子更清晰、更直接。
- example: This sentence is in the active, while the other one uses the passive. || 这个句子是主动语态，而另一个用的是被动语态。

- antonyms: static || 静态的 ;; lethargic || 无精打采的 ;; inert || 惰性的，不活跃的 ;;

- definitionEn: (of a person) full of energy, enthusiasm and new ideas, and able to motivate others; (of a process or system) constantly changing and developing; relating to the forces or processes that produce movement, in physics ;;
- example: He's a dynamic young entrepreneur who has built three successful startups in five years. || 他是个精力充沛的年轻企业家，五年内创办了三家成功的创业公司。

- definitionEn: the way in which people or things behave and react to each other in a particular situation; the force or set of forces that causes something to develop or change ;;
- example: The dynamic between the two lead actors makes the film's emotional scenes much more convincing. || 两位主演之间的互动关系让这部电影的情感场景更有说服力。
- example: Shifts in consumer preference are a key dynamic driving the development of plant-based food products. || 消费者偏好的转变是推动植物性食品发展的关键驱动力。
- example: We need to analyze the social dynamics of the community before launching the public welfare project. || 在推出这个公益项目之前，我们需要分析该社区的社会动态。

## word: passive
- uk: /ˈpæsɪv/
- us: /ˈpæsɪv/
- synonyms: inactive || 不活跃的，消极的 ;; submissive || 顺从的，服从的 ;; unresisting || 不抵抗的，顺从的 ;; indifferent || 漠不关心的 ;; compliant || 顺从的，服从的 ;;
- antonyms: active || 积极的，主动的 ;; aggressive || 好斗的，有进取心的 ;; assertive || 坚定自信的，果断的 ;;
- phrases: passive voice || 被动语态 ;; passive income || 被动收入 ;; passive smoking || 被动吸烟，二手烟 ;; passive resistance || 消极抵抗，非暴力抵抗 ;; passive transport || 被动运输 ;;
- collocations: passive attitude || 消极态度 ;; passive role || 被动角色 ;; passive behavior || 被动行为 ;; passive observer || 被动观察者 ;; passive response || 消极回应 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be passive about sth || 表示对某事持消极被动的态度 ;; It is passive to do sth || 表示做某事是消极被动的 ;; adopt a passive approach to sth || 表示对某事采取消极的方法 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Don't be so passive all the time. || 别一直这么被动。 ;; He's way too passive in relationships. || 他在感情里太被动了。 ;; Stop taking a passive stance on this issue. || 别在这个问题上持消极态度了。 ;;
- idioms: passive aggression || 被动攻击（用消极、隐蔽的方式表达不满的行为） ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 消极的，被动的 ;; 被动语态的 ;; 顺从的，不抵抗的 ;;
- definitionZh: 形容人不主动采取行动，而是接受他人的行为或事情的发展，不做出回应或反抗 ;; 描述语法中主语是动作承受者的语态 ;; 形容人温顺、服从，不会主动表达诉求或反抗 ;;
- definitionEn: Describing someone who does not take active action, but accepts others' actions or the development of things without responding or resisting ;; Used in grammar to describe a voice where the subject is the receiver of the action ;; Describing someone who is meek and obedient, and will not actively express demands or resist ;;
- example: He played a passive role in the negotiation and rarely put forward his own opinions. || 他在谈判中扮演了被动的角色，很少提出自己的观点。
- example: Many students tend to be passive in class, just waiting for the teacher to give answers. || 很多学生在课堂上往往很被动，只是等着老师给出答案。
- example: The passive voice is often used in academic writing to make the expression more objective. || 被动语态经常被用于学术写作中，让表述更客观。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 被动语态 ;; 被动形式 ;;
- definitionZh: 语法中表示主语是动作承受者的动词形式或语态 ;;
- definitionEn: The verb form or voice in grammar that shows the subject is the receiver of the action ;;
- example: In this sentence, the passive is more appropriate than the active to emphasize the result of the action. || 在这个句子里，被动语态比主动语态更合适，用来强调动作的结果。
- example: Students often confuse the use of the passive with the active in English composition. || 学生在英语写作中经常混淆被动语态和主动语态的用法。

## word: action
- uk: /ˈækʃən/
- us: /ˈækʃən/
- synonyms: act || 行为，行动 ;; deed || 事迹，行为 ;; operation || 操作，运作 ;; activity || 活动 ;; measure || 措施 ;;
- antonyms: inaction || 不活动，不作为 ;; idleness || 懒惰，闲散 ;;
- phrases: take action || 采取行动 ;; out of action || 失去作用，损坏 ;; action movie || 动作片 ;; call to action || 行动号召 ;; course of action || 行动方针 ;;
- collocations: immediate action || 立即行动 ;; legal action || 法律诉讼 ;; collective action || 集体行动 ;; disciplinary action || 纪律处分 ;; positive action || 积极行动 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It's time to take action to do sth. || 表示“是时候采取行动做某事了”，用于呼吁行动 ;; The government has promised action on sth. || 表示“政府已承诺就某事采取行动”，用于官方语境 ;; Sth is out of action after sth. || 表示“某物在某事件后无法正常使用”，用于描述物品损坏或人员受伤的情况 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Actions speak louder than words. || 行动胜于空谈 ;; Let's get this action started! || 咱们开始干吧！ ;; What's the action here? || 这儿有什么好玩的/热闹的？ ;;
- idioms: a piece of the action || 分一杯羹，参与某事获利 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 行动；行为 ;; 诉讼；诉讼权 ;; 动作；情节 ;; 作用；效应 ;; 战斗；军事行动 ;;
- definitionZh: 为达到某种目的而进行的活动、做事的过程； ;; 向法院提起的要求维护权益的法律程序； ;; 故事、影视作品中的情节发展，或人/事物的动作姿态； ;; 事物之间产生的影响、效果； ;; 武装冲突、军事任务等相关活动；
- definitionEn: The process of doing something in order to achieve a goal; ;; A legal process brought to a court to demand the protection of one's rights; ;; The plot development in a story, film or work, or the movement posture of a person or thing; ;; The effect or influence that one thing has on another; ;; Activities related to armed conflicts, military missions, etc.;
- example: We need to take urgent action to reduce carbon emissions. || 我们需要采取紧急行动来减少碳排放。
- example: She decided to take legal action against the company for unfair dismissal. || 她决定以不公平解雇为由起诉这家公司。
- example: The film has a lot of exciting action and spectacular special effects. || 这部电影有大量精彩的动作场面和震撼的特效。
- example: The new drug's action on the disease has been proven effective in clinical trials. || 这种新药对该疾病的作用已在临床试验中被证明有效。

### sense: int.
- translationZh: 开拍（拍摄影视时导演的指令） ;; 开始行动（非正式语境下的指令） ;;
- definitionZh: 导演在拍摄影视场景时，示意演员开始表演的指令； ;; 非正式场合中，示意他人开始进行某活动的口头指令；
- definitionEn: A command given by a director when filming a scene to tell actors to start performing; ;; An oral command in informal situations to tell others to start an activity;
- example: The director shouted "Action!" and the actors began their performance. || 导演大喊“开拍！”，演员们便开始了表演。
- example: Okay, everyone's ready—action! Let's see how well this plan works. || 好了，大家都准备好了——开始！咱们看看这个计划效果如何。

## word: event
- uk: /ɪˈvent/
- us: /ɪˈvent/
- synonyms: occurrence || 发生的事件 ;; incident || 事变，插曲 ;; affair || 事务，事件 ;; occasion || 场合，时机 ;; happening || 事件，意外发生的事 ;;
- antonyms: non-event || 扫兴的事，大肆宣传却结果乏味的事 ;; routine || 常规，惯例 ;;
- phrases: sporting event || 体育赛事 ;; historical event || 历史事件 ;; social event || 社交活动 ;; adverse event || 不良事件 ;; main event || 主要活动，压轴项目 ;;
- collocations: attend an event || 参加活动 ;; host an event || 举办活动 ;; cancel an event || 取消活动 ;; record an event || 记录事件 ;; a significant event || 重大事件 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + adj. + that the event + 谓语 || 用于描述事件具备某种属性 ;; The event of sth. has brought about + 影响 || 用于说明某事件带来的后果 ;; When it comes to the event of + 具体事件, + 主句 || 用于引出对某特定事件的讨论 ;;
- spokenExpressions: In any event, we'll be there on time. || 无论如何，我们都会准时到的。 ;; That was quite the event last night! || 昨晚的活动可太精彩了！ ;; The main event starts in ten minutes. || 压轴活动十分钟后就开始了。 ;;
- idioms: in the event of sth. || 倘若，万一发生某事 ;; in any event || 不管怎样，无论如何 ;; after the event || 事后，事后看来 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 事件，大事 ;; 活动，赛事 ;; （尤指重要的）公开活动 ;;
- definitionZh: 发生的重要或值得注意的事情 ;; 有组织的公共活动，如演出、比赛等 ;;
- definitionEn: a thing that happens, especially something important ;; a planned public or social occasion ;;
- example: The election was the main event of 2024 in that country. || 那次选举是该国2024年的头等大事。
- example: The city will host a major international sporting event next year. || 这座城市明年将举办一场大型国际体育赛事。
- example: The unexpected event caused widespread panic among the local residents. || 这起意外事件在当地居民中引发了大范围恐慌。
- example: Over 3000 people attended the charity event last weekend. || 上周末有超过三千人参加了那场慈善活动。

## word: idleness
- uk: /ˈaɪdlnəs/
- us: /ˈaɪdlnəs/
- synonyms: inactivity || 不活动，懒散 ;; laziness || 懒惰，怠惰 ;; indolence || 怠惰，好逸恶劳 ;; sloth || 懒散，怠惰 ;;
- antonyms: industry || 勤奋，勤劳 ;; diligence || 勤勉，用功 ;; activity || 活跃，活动 ;;
- phrases: fall into idleness || 陷入闲散状态 ;; living in idleness || 过着游手好闲的生活 ;; the sin of idleness || 懒惰之罪 ;; idleness among youth || 青年群体的闲散问题 ;;
- collocations: widespread idleness || 普遍的闲散现象 ;; enforced idleness || 被迫闲置/无事可做 ;; waste time in idleness || 虚度光阴 ;; idleness of equipment || 设备闲置 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Idleness is the root cause of + 名词短语 || 用于表达闲散是某类负面结果的根源 ;; There is a growing problem of idleness among + 群体名词 || 用于说明某一群体中闲散问题日益严重 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Idleness never did anyone any good. || 闲散对谁都没好处。 ;; Don't let idleness take over your life. || 别让懒散支配你的生活。 ;; All this idleness is making me antsy. || 这么闲下来我浑身不自在。 ;;
- idioms: Idleness is the root of all evil. || 闲散是万恶之源。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 懒散，怠惰 ;; 空闲，闲散 ;; 闲置（状态） ;;
- definitionZh: 指不愿工作或活动的懒惰状态 ;; 指无事可做、没有被占用的状态 ;; 指机器、设备等未被使用的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: The state of being unwilling to work or use energy ;; The state of having nothing to do or not being occupied ;; The state of a machine, facility, etc. not being used ;;
- example: His idleness at work eventually led to him being fired. || 他工作上的怠惰最终导致他被解雇了。
- example: Many workers were forced into idleness when the factory closed temporarily. || 工厂临时停业时，很多工人被迫无事可做。
- example: The long period of idleness caused the old machine to rust. || 长期闲置导致这台旧机器生锈了。
- example: The school launched vocational courses to reduce idleness among local teenagers. || 学校开设了职业课程来减少当地青少年的闲散情况。

## word: inactivity
- uk: /ˌɪnækˈtɪvəti/
- us: /ˌɪnækˈtɪvəti/
- synonyms: idleness || 懒散，无所事事 ;; lethargy || 无精打采，倦怠 ;; stagnation || 停滞，不发展 ;; sloth || 懒惰，怠惰 ;; immobility || 静止，不动 ;;
- antonyms: activity || 活动，活跃 ;; dynamism || 活力，精力 ;; motion || 运动，移动 ;;
- phrases: physical inactivity || 缺乏身体活动 ;; prolonged inactivity || 长期不活动 ;; economic inactivity || 经济不活跃 ;; muscle atrophy from inactivity || 闲置导致的肌肉萎缩 ;; period of inactivity || 闲置期，休止期 ;;
- collocations: suffer from inactivity || 受不活动的困扰 ;; lead to inactivity || 导致停滞 ;; avoid prolonged inactivity || 避免长期久坐不动 ;; long-term inactivity || 长期闲置 ;; widespread inactivity || 普遍的怠惰 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Inactivity + be + linked to + n. || 说明：用于阐述不活动引发的关联后果，主语为inactivity，后接系动词和被动结构引出相关事物 ;; Too much + inactivity + can + cause + n. || 说明：用于说明过度怠惰/停滞带来的具体问题，主语由too much修饰inactivity构成，后接情态动词和实义动词引出结果 ;; A period of + inactivity + be + needed after + n. || 说明：用于表达某类事件后需要一段休整/停滞期，主语为a period of inactivity，后接系动词和表语说明需求 ;;
- spokenExpressions: The inactivity is killing me. || 整天无所事事我快闷死了 ;; A little inactivity never hurt anyone. || 偶尔偷会儿懒没什么坏处 ;; You've got to shake off this inactivity. || 你得摆脱这种没干劲的状态 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 不活动，怠惰 ;; 停滞，无运作 ;;
- definitionZh: 长时间不进行身体活动、工作或行动的状态 ;; 组织、系统、经济等没有发展或运作的静止状态 ;;
- definitionEn: The state of not doing any physical activity, work, or action for a long time ;; The static state in which organizations, systems, economies, etc. do not develop or operate ;;
- example: Regular exercise can reduce the health risks caused by physical inactivity. || 定期锻炼可以降低缺乏身体活动带来的健康风险。
- example: The factory has been in a state of inactivity since the production line broke down. || 自从生产线出故障后，这家工厂就一直处于停滞状态。
- example: Many experts warn that prolonged inactivity among young people will affect their long-term physical development. || 很多专家提醒，年轻人长期久坐不动会影响他们的长期身体发育。

## word: pursuit
- uk: /pəˈsjuːt/
- us: /pərˈsuːt/
- synonyms: chase || 追赶，追逐 ;; quest || 追求，探索 ;; search || 搜寻，寻找 ;; endeavor || 努力，尝试 ;;
- antonyms: abandonment || 放弃，遗弃 ;; relinquishment || 放手，放弃 ;;
- phrases: in pursuit of || 追求，寻求 ;; hot pursuit || 紧追不舍 ;; pursuit of happiness || 追求幸福 ;;
- collocations: relentless pursuit || 不懈的追求 ;; academic pursuit || 学术追求 ;; leisure pursuit || 休闲爱好 ;; criminal pursuit || 追捕罪犯 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb be engaged in the pursuit of sth || 某人致力于追求某物/某事 ;; The pursuit of sth requires sb to do sth || 对某事的追求要求某人做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: In pursuit of what? || 你在追求什么啊？ ;; It's all part of the pursuit. || 这都是追求过程的一部分嘛。 ;;
- idioms: hell-for-leather pursuit || 全力追赶，拼命追击 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 追求，追寻 ;; 追赶，追逐 ;; 工作，爱好，事业 ;;
- definitionZh: 为了获得、实现某事物而付出的努力过程； ;; 追赶、追捕某人或某物的行动； ;; 人们投入时间精力从事的活动、事业或爱好；
- definitionEn: the act of trying to achieve or obtain something over a period of time; ;; the action of following or chasing someone or something in order to catch them; ;; an activity, hobby, or career that someone spends time and effort on;
- example: She moved to New York in pursuit of a career in acting. || 她搬到纽约，追求演艺事业。
- example: The police car sped through the streets in pursuit of the stolen vehicle. || 警车在街道上飞驰，追赶被盗车辆。
- example: Outdoor pursuits like hiking and rock climbing are his favourite ways to spend weekends. || 徒步、攀岩这类户外活动是他最喜欢的周末消遣方式。

## word: add
- uk: /æd/
- us: /æd/
- synonyms: include || 包含，加入 ;; attach || 附上，附加 ;; supplement || 补充，增补 ;; append || 附加，添加 ;;
- antonyms: remove || 移除，去掉 ;; subtract || 减去，扣除 ;; delete || 删除，清除 ;;
- phrases: add up || 合计，加起来 ;; add to || 增加，增添 ;; add in || 包括，把…算在内 ;; add up to || 总计达，意味着 ;;
- collocations: add information || 补充信息 ;; add fuel to the fire || 火上浇油 ;; add salt || 加盐 ;; add a comment || 发表评论 ;; add value || 增加价值 ;;
- sentencePatterns: add sth to sth || 表示“把某物添加到某物中”的基础结构 ;; add that + 从句 || 表示“补充说某内容”的宾语从句结构 ;; It adds that + 从句 || 用于正式文本中表示“（文件/声明等）补充说明”的结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Add me on WeChat! || 加我微信！ ;; That adds to the fun, doesn't it? || 那更有意思了，不是吗？ ;; Let me add a quick point here. || 我简单补充一点。 ;;
- idioms: add fuel to the flames || 火上浇油，使情况更糟 ;; add insult to injury || 落井下石，更糟的是 ;;

### sense: 及物动词
- translationZh: 添加，加入 ;; 补充说 ;; 计算…的总和 ;;
- definitionZh: 把某物放到另一物中，使数量、内容等增加 ;; 在说完内容后额外补充说明信息 ;; 将多个数字加起来计算总和 ;;
- definitionEn: to put something with another thing so that the amount, content etc. increases ;; to say something more in addition to what you have already said ;; to calculate the total of several numbers ;;
- example: Please add some sugar to my coffee. || 请给我的咖啡里加些糖。
- example: He added that he would come back next week. || 他补充说他下周会回来。
- example: If you add 5 and 3, you get 8. || 你把5和3加起来，得到8。

### sense: 不及物动词
- translationZh: 增加，增添 ;; 加起来，总计 ;;
- definitionZh: 使原有事物的程度、数量等上升 ;; 多个数字合计得到某个总数 ;;
- definitionEn: to make the degree, amount etc. of an original thing rise ;; if several numbers add up to a total, they make that total when combined ;;
- example: The bad weather only added to our difficulties. || 恶劣的天气只会增加我们的困难。
- example: These numbers add up to exactly 100. || 这些数字加起来正好是100。
- example: Every mistake you make adds to the risk of failure. || 你犯的每一个错误都会增加失败的风险。



## word: attach
- uk: /əˈtætʃ/
- us: /əˈtætʃ/
- synonyms: fasten || 固定，系牢 ;; affix || 粘贴，附上 ;; connect || 连接，关联 ;; bind || 捆绑，绑定 ;;
- antonyms: detach || 拆卸，分离 ;; remove || 移除，去掉 ;; unfasten || 解开，松开 ;;
- phrases: attach importance to || 重视 ;; attach to || 依附于，与…有关 ;; attach file || 附件 ;; attach label || 贴标签 ;;
- collocations: attach firmly || 牢牢固定 ;; attach legally || 依法绑定 ;; attach personally || 个人认为（重要性） ;; attach electronically || 电子附加 ;;
- sentencePatterns: attach sth to sth || 表示“把某物附着/附加到某物上”的动宾结构 ;; be attached to sth/sb || 表示“依恋某物/某人；附属于某机构”的被动结构 ;; attach importance/significance to sth || 表示“重视某物”的固定搭配结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Attach it here, please. || 请把它贴在这儿。 ;; I'm really attached to my old laptop. || 我真的很舍不得我的旧笔记本电脑。 ;; Don't attach too much meaning to his words. || 别过度解读他的话。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms: attach no strings || 不附加任何条件 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 固定，系，贴 ;; 附上，附加 ;; 重视，赋予（重要性） ;; 依恋，喜爱 ;; 与…有关联 ;;
- definitionZh: 把某物固定或连接到另一物体上 ;; 在邮件、文件等中添加额外内容 ;; 认为某事物具有特定的重要性、意义等 ;; 对人或事物产生深厚的情感依赖 ;; 某事物与另一事物存在关联或归属关系 ;;
- definitionEn: to fasten or join one thing to another ;; to add something extra to a document, email etc ;; to believe that something has a particular quality, importance, or meaning ;; to feel a strong emotional connection to someone or something ;; to be connected with or belong to something ;;
- example: Please attach a recent photo to your application form. || 请在你的申请表上附上一张近照。
- example: This research institute is attached to Peking University. || 这个研究所隶属于北京大学。
- example: Most parents attach great importance to their children's education. || 大多数父母都非常重视孩子的教育。
- example: She has grown very attached to the foster dog she took in last month. || 她对上个月收留的那只流浪狗已经产生了很深的感情。
- example: No blame attaches to you for this accident. || 这次事故你不需要承担任何责任。

## word: include
- uk: /ɪnˈkluːd/
- us: /ɪnˈkluːd/
- synonyms: contain || 包含，含有 ;; incorporate || 纳入，吸收 ;; comprise || 由…组成 ;; cover || 涵盖，包括 ;; embrace || 包括，包含 ;;
- antonyms: exclude || 排除，不包括 ;; omit || 省略，遗漏 ;; exclude || 排斥 ;;
- phrases: include in || 把…列入，包含在…中 ;; include as || 把…列为 ;; include on || 把…列在…上 ;; include among || 把…归入…之列 ;;
- collocations: include tax || 包含税费 ;; include service charge || 包含服务费 ;; include examples || 包含例子 ;; include details || 包含细节 ;; include participants || 涵盖参与者 ;;
- sentencePatterns: include sth in sth || 表示将某物包含在某个范围/集合中 ;; sb/sth includes sth || 表示人/事物包含某内容 ;; be included in sth || 表示被包含在某个范围内 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Does that include drinks? || 那里面包含饮品吗？ ;; The price should include delivery, right? || 这个价格应该包含配送费吧？ ;; I'll include you in the group chat later. || 我一会儿把你拉进群聊里。 ;;
- idioms: include sb/sth in the fold || 把某人/某物纳入团体/组织中 ;;

### sense: 及物动词
- translationZh: 包含，含有 ;; 把…列为一部分，纳入 ;;
- definitionZh: 指某个整体中包含特定的人、事物或内容作为组成部分 ;; 特意将某人或某物归入某个范围、清单或群体中 ;;
- definitionEn: to have something or someone as a part of a whole ;; to deliberately add someone or something to a list, group, or range ;;
- example: The tour package includes three nights' accommodation and all meals. || 这个旅行套餐包含三晚住宿和所有餐食。
- example: Remember to include your contact information in the application form. || 记得在申请表里附上你的联系方式。
- example: The research project included over 500 volunteers from different age groups. || 这个研究项目纳入了来自不同年龄段的500多名志愿者。

### sense: 不及物动词
- translationZh: 被包括，被包含 ;;
- definitionZh: 作为组成部分被归入某个整体中 ;;
- definitionEn: to be contained as a part of a whole ;;
- example: All expenses include, the trip cost us around 2000 yuan. || 算上所有开支，这次旅行我们花了大约2000元。
- example: Service charge includes, the total bill is 85 pounds. || 含服务费在内，账单总额是85英镑。

## word: remove
- uk: /rɪˈmuːv/
- us: /rɪˈmuːv/
- synonyms: eliminate || 消除，排除 ;; delete || 删除 ;; extract || 提取，取出 ;; discard || 丢弃，抛弃 ;; expel || 驱逐，开除 ;;
- antonyms: add || 添加 ;; install || 安装，设置 ;; retain || 保留，保持 ;;
- phrases: remove from || 从…移除，从…开除 ;; remove oneself || 离开，脱身 ;; remove obstacles || 清除障碍 ;; remove doubt || 消除疑虑 ;; remove stains || 去除污渍 ;;
- collocations: completely remove || 完全移除 ;; manually remove || 手动删除 ;; surgically remove || 手术切除 ;; remove restrictions || 取消限制 ;; remove a user || 删除用户 ;;
- sentencePatterns: remove sth from sth || 表示“把某物从某处移除”的基础结构 ;; be removed from sth || 被动语态，表示“被从…移除/调离” ;; It is difficult to remove sth || 形式主语结构，表示“移除某物很困难” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Could you remove this? || 你能把这个拿走吗？ ;; Let me remove that for you. || 我来帮你把那个拿掉吧。 ;; He's been removed from his post. || 他被撤职了。 ;;
- idioms: remove the scales from someone's eyes || 使某人认清事实，擦亮某人的眼睛 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 移开，拿开 ;; 移除，删除 ;; 开除，免职 ;; 去除（污渍、感觉等） ;;
- definitionZh: 把人或物从原来的位置移走 ;; 从某个系统、列表、组织中除去某事物或某人 ;; 消除某种不需要的事物（如污渍、疑虑、疼痛等） ;;
- definitionEn: to take sth or sb away from a particular place ;; to take sth off or away from a surface, place, list, or organization ;; to get rid of sth that is not wanted, such as a mark, a feeling, or a problem ;;
- example: Please remove your shoes before entering the house. || 进屋前请脱掉你的鞋子。
- example: The company decided to remove the outdated product from the market. || 公司决定把这款过时产品从市场上下架。
- example: This special detergent can help remove coffee stains from the shirt. || 这种特殊洗涤剂可以帮你去除衬衫上的咖啡渍。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 距离，间距 ;; 差异，差距 ;;
- definitionZh: 两者之间存在的空间或时间上的距离 ;; 抽象意义上的差异、隔阂 ;;
- definitionEn: a degree or amount of separation between two people, things, or ideas ;; a distance in space or time between two things ;;
- example: What he said was only one remove from the truth. || 他说的话和事实只有一线之差。
- example: They live at several removes from the downtown area. || 他们住的地方离市区有好几段距离。
- example: There is a remove between his words and his actual actions. || 他的言辞和实际行动之间存在差距。

## word: subtract
- uk: /səbˈtrækt/
- us: /səbˈtrækt/
- synonyms: deduct || 扣除，减去 ;; take away || 拿走，减去 ;; minus || 减去，扣除 ;;
- antonyms: add || 加，添加 ;; increase || 增加，增长 ;;
- phrases: subtract from || 从…中减去 ;; subtract sth from sth || 把某物从某物中扣除 ;; subtract tax from salary || 从工资中扣税 ;;
- collocations: subtract numbers || 计算数字的减法 ;; subtract funds || 扣除资金 ;; subtract points || 扣分 ;; subtract a small amount || 减去少量 ;;
- sentencePatterns: subtract A from B || 表示“将A从B中扣除/减去”的基础句型 ;; be subtracted from || 被动语态结构，表示“被从…中扣除” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Subtract three from eight, what do you get? || 八减三等于多少？ ;; Let me subtract the cost of the materials first. || 我先把材料成本扣掉啊。 ;; Don't forget to subtract the service fee. || 别忘了扣服务费哦。 ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 减，减去 ;; 扣除，减掉 ;;
- definitionZh: 从一个数或总量中去掉另一个数或部分 ;; 从整体中除去某一部分 ;;
- definitionEn: to take a number or an amount away from another number or amount ;; to remove a part of something from the whole ;;
- example: If you subtract 5 from 10, you get 5. || 10减5等于5。
- example: The company will subtract travel expenses from your reimbursement. || 公司会从你的报销款里扣除差旅费用。
- example: One mistake will subtract six points from your final score. || 出现一个错误就会从你的最终得分里扣掉六分。

- definitionEn: something that is added to something else to improve or complete it ;; an additional part at the end of a book, report, etc. ;; a product that you take to add to the food you eat, to improve your health ;; an extra amount of money that you have to pay ;;
- example: The doctor advised me to take vitamin supplements during the winter. || 医生建议我冬天服用维生素补充剂。
- example: There is a supplement to the dictionary that includes new words. || 这本词典有一个收录新词的补编。

### sense: verb

- definitionZh: 通过添加某物来使某物更完善或更充足 ;;
- definitionEn: to add something to something in order to improve it or make it complete ;;
- example: Many people supplement their income by doing part-time jobs. || 很多人通过做兼职来补贴收入。
- example: She supplements the textbook with extra reading materials for her students. || 她给学生们额外补充阅读材料来配合课本使用。
- example: The data in the report was supplemented by recent research findings. || 报告里的数据由最近的研究结果做了补充。

- example: The government is taking steps to address the rising cost of living. || 政府正在采取措施解决不断上涨的生活成本问题。
- example: She addressed the audience and explained her new project. || 她向听众致辞，介绍了她的新项目。

## word: avoid
- uk: /əˈvɔɪd/
- us: /əˈvɔɪd/
- synonyms: evade || 逃避，躲避 ;; shun || 避开，回避 ;; eschew || 避开，远避 ;; dodge || 躲闪，避开 ;;
- antonyms: seek || 寻找，追求 ;; confront || 面对，直面 ;; encounter || 遭遇，遇见 ;;
- phrases: avoid doing sth || 避免做某事 ;; avoid contact with || 避免与…接触 ;; avoid the issue || 回避问题 ;; avoid risk || 规避风险 ;;
- collocations: deliberately avoid || 故意避开 ;; carefully avoid || 小心避免 ;; avoid trouble || 避免麻烦 ;; avoid mistakes || 避免错误 ;;
- sentencePatterns: avoid + (doing) sth || 后接名词或动名词作宾语，不能接不定式 ;; It is important to avoid sth/doing sth || 表达做某事很重要的常用结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Try to avoid rush hour. || 尽量避开高峰期。 ;; You can't avoid the problem forever. || 你不可能永远回避这个问题。 ;; I deliberately avoided talking about that topic. || 我特意避开聊那个话题。 ;;
- idioms: avoid sb/sth like the plague || 像躲瘟疫一样避开某人/某物 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 避免，防止 ;; 避开，躲避 ;; 回避，避开（问题、话题等） ;;
- definitionZh: 采取措施阻止某事发生，或不做某类可能产生不良后果的事 ;; 有意远离某人、某地，或者不提及某个话题，以避免麻烦或不快 ;;
- definitionEn: To prevent something bad from happening, or to stop yourself from doing something that might have bad results ;; To deliberately stay away from someone or something, or not talk about a particular subject because you want to avoid problems or unpleasant situations ;;
- example: She wore a mask to avoid catching the flu. || 她戴了口罩以免传染流感。
- example: He always avoids eye contact when he is lying. || 他撒谎的时候总是避免眼神接触。
- example: The driver swerved sharply to avoid hitting the stray dog. || 司机猛地转向，以免撞到那只流浪狗。

## word: ignore
- uk: /ɪɡˈnɔː(r)/
- us: /ɪɡˈnɔːr/
- synonyms: disregard || 忽视，不理会 ;; neglect || 疏忽，忽略 ;; overlook ||  overlooking是动词，哦不对，overlook作为动词是忽略，未注意到 ;; dismiss || 不予理会，驳回 ;;
- antonyms: notice || 注意到 ;; heed || 听从，留意 ;; attend to || 关注，照料 ;;
- phrases: ignore the rules || 无视规则 ;; ignore sb's advice || 忽视某人的建议 ;; ignore the fact || 忽略事实 ;; ignore warning signs || 无视警示信号 ;; ignore personal feelings || 不顾个人感受 ;;
- collocations: deliberately ignore || 故意忽视 ;; completely ignore || 完全无视 ;; largely ignore || 基本上忽略 ;; publicly ignore || 公开无视 ;; tend to ignore || 往往会忽略 ;;
- sentencePatterns: ignore + n./pron. || 后接名词或代词作宾语，表示忽视某事物/某人 ;; ignore + v-ing || 后接动名词作宾语，表示忽视做某事的行为 ;; It is unwise to ignore... || 表示“忽视……是不明智的”，用于提出劝告 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Don't ignore me! || 别不理我啊！ ;; Just ignore him, he's just being silly. || 别理他，他就是在犯傻。 ;; We can't ignore this problem any longer. || 我们不能再对这个问题视而不见了。 ;;
- idioms: ignore the elephant in the room || 无视明摆着的棘手问题 ;;

### sense: 动词（及物）
- translationZh: 忽视，不理会 ;; 无视，不予考虑 ;;
- definitionZh: 故意不注意、不搭理某人或某事物；对应该关注的情况、建议等刻意不予理会 ;; 明知某事物存在或有合理性，却刻意不承认、不考虑其影响 ;;
- definitionEn: to deliberately pay no attention to someone or something ;; to refuse to consider or acknowledge something that you know is important or real ;;
- example: She ignored his text messages and didn't call him back. || 她没理他的短信，也没给他回电话。
- example: The company chose to ignore the safety risks of the new equipment, which led to a serious accident. || 该公司选择无视新设备的安全隐患，最终引发了严重事故。
- example: You can't ignore the fact that many people still can't afford basic medical care in this region. || 你不能忽略这个地区仍有很多人负担不起基础医疗的事实。
- example: He ignored all the negative comments and focused on finishing his project. || 他不理会所有负面评论，专心完成自己的项目。

## word: advantage
- uk: /ədˈvɑːntɪdʒ/
- us: /ədˈvæntɪdʒ/
- synonyms: benefit || 益处，好处 ;; edge || 优势，上风 ;; merit || 优点，价值 ;; upside || 积极面，好处 ;;
- antonyms: disadvantage || 劣势，缺点 ;; drawback || 弊端，缺陷 ;; shortcoming || 短处，缺点 ;;
- phrases: competitive advantage || 竞争优势 ;; take advantage of || 利用 ;; have an advantage over || 比…有优势 ;; to sb's advantage || 对某人有利 ;;
- collocations: distinct advantage || 明显的优势 ;; unfair advantage || 不公平的优势 ;; natural advantage || 先天优势 ;; gain an advantage || 获得优势 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is an advantage (for sb) to do sth || （对某人来说）做某事是一种优势 ;; Sth gives sb an advantage over sb else || 某事物使某人比他人更具优势 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Take advantage of the opportunity! || 抓住这个机会！;; The advantage is that we don't have to rush. || 好处是我们不用着急。;; What's the advantage of doing that? || 那么做有什么好处？;;
- idioms: turn sth to advantage || 使某物转化为有利条件 ;; play to your advantages || 发挥你的优势 ;;

### sense: n. 名词
- translationZh: 有利条件，优势 ;; 益处，好处 ;;
- definitionZh: 能让人比他人更可能成功的条件或特质 ;; 某事物带来的积极益处或好的结果 ;;
- definitionEn: A condition or characteristic that puts someone in a more favourable or superior position than others; A positive benefit or good result that comes from a particular thing.
- example: Being fluent in English is a big advantage when applying for international jobs. || 英语流利在申请国际职位时是一个很大的优势。
- example: One of the main advantages of living in the countryside is the fresh air. || 住在乡村的主要好处之一是空气新鲜。
- example: The home team has the advantage of knowing the stadium very well. || 主队具备十分熟悉场馆的有利条件。

### sense: v. 动词
- translationZh: 有利于，使处于有利地位 ;;
- definitionZh: 让某人或某事物获得好处，处于更有利的位置 ;;
- definitionEn: To put someone or something in a more favourable or beneficial position.
- example: The new tax policy clearly advantages small business owners. || 新的税收政策显然对小企业主有利。
- example: The current market situation advantages brands that focus on eco-friendly products. || 当前的市场形势有利于主打环保产品的品牌。
- example: The special rule was designed to advantage students from low-income families. || 这项特殊规定的设立是为了照顾低收入家庭的学生，让他们处于有利地位。



## word: benefit
- uk: /ˈbenɪfɪt/
- us: /ˈbenɪfɪt/
- synonyms: advantage || 优势，好处 ;; profit || 利润，收益 ;; gain || 获得，获利 ;; perk || 额外待遇，好处 ;;
- antonyms: disadvantage || 劣势，弊端 ;; harm || 伤害，损害 ;; loss || 损失，亏损 ;;
- phrases: benefit from || 从…中获益 ;; mutual benefit || 互利共赢 ;; social benefit || 社会效益 ;; unemployment benefit || 失业救济金 ;;
- collocations: great benefit || 巨大的好处 ;; health benefit || 健康益处 ;; economic benefit || 经济效益 ;; derive benefit || 获得益处 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb benefit from sth || 某人从某事物中获益，主语通常是人 ;; sth benefit sb || 某事物对某人有益，主语通常是事物 ;; It is to sb's benefit to do sth || 做某事对某人有好处，it作形式主语 ;;
- spokenExpressions: For your benefit, I'll repeat that. || 为了让你听清楚，我再重复一遍。 ;; Everyone stands to benefit from this plan. || 所有人都会从这个计划里获益的。 ;; The benefits far outweigh the risks. || 好处远远大于风险。 ;;
- idioms: reap the benefits (of sth) || （因过去的所作所为）获得收益，享受到好处 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 好处，益处 ;; 救济金，补助金 ;; 优势，成效 ;;
- definitionZh: 对人或事物有帮助的积极作用、优势 ;; 政府或机构向符合条件的人群发放的补助性资金 ;;
- definitionEn: an advantage or positive effect that helps you or improves your life ;; money given by the government or an organization to people who need financial help ;;
- example: Regular exercise has many health benefits. || 定期锻炼有很多健康益处。
- example: She's been receiving unemployment benefit since she lost her job. || 她失业后一直在领失业救济金。
- example: One of the benefits of working here is the free gym membership. || 在这里工作的好处之一是有免费的健身会员。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 对…有益，有利于 ;; 获益，得到好处 ;;
- definitionZh: 给某对象带来积极的、有利的影响 ;; 从某个事件、情况或行为中获得好处 ;;
- definitionEn: to be useful or helpful to someone or something ;; to get an advantage or improvement from a situation or action ;;
- example: The new policy will benefit low-income families greatly. || 新政策将极大地惠及低收入家庭。
- example: I benefited a lot from the online courses I took last year. || 我从去年上的线上课程中获益良多。
- example: The local community will benefit from the new park project. || 当地社区将从这个新公园项目中获益。

## word: disadvantage
- uk: /ˌdɪsədˈvɑːntɪdʒ/
- us: /ˌdɪsədˈvæntɪdʒ/
- synonyms: drawback || 缺点，不利条件 ;; downside || 不利方面，弊端 ;; handicap || 障碍，不利条件 ;; flaw || 缺陷，瑕疵 ;; shortcoming || 短处，缺点 ;;
- antonyms: advantage || 优势，有利条件 ;; benefit || 益处，好处 ;; merit || 优点，价值 ;;
- phrases: at a disadvantage || 处于不利地位 ;; to the disadvantage of sb || 对某人不利 ;; disadvantage factor || 不利因素 ;; competitive disadvantage || 竞争劣势 ;; overcome disadvantage || 克服不利条件 ;;
- collocations: main disadvantage || 主要劣势 ;; serious disadvantage || 严重弊端 ;; inherent disadvantage || 固有缺陷 ;; put sb at a disadvantage || 使某人处于不利地位 ;; offset a disadvantage || 抵消不利条件 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There is/are + [adj] + disadvantage(s) + of/in + (doing) sth || 用于说明做某事存在某种不利条件 ;; Sth + puts/keeps + sb + at a (serious/great) disadvantage || 用于表述某事物使某人处于不利境地 ;; The main disadvantage of sth is that + 从句 || 用于阐述某事物的主要弊端是什么 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That's a big disadvantage. || 那可是个很大的弊端。 ;; You'll be at a disadvantage if you don't prepare. || 你要是不准备的话会处于劣势的。 ;; The only disadvantage I can see is... || 我能想到的唯一不利之处是… ;;
- idioms: take advantage of one's disadvantage || 乘人之危 ;;

### sense: n. 名词
- translationZh: 不利条件，劣势 ;; 缺点，弊端 ;;
- definitionZh: 会阻碍某人成功或使某事物效果变差的情况、条件或特征 ;; 某事物存在的不足或负面属性 ;;
- definitionEn: A condition or situation that makes it difficult for someone to succeed or for something to be as effective as it should be ;; A fault or negative quality that something has ;;
- example: One major disadvantage of living in the countryside is the lack of public transport. || 住在乡村的一大弊端是公共交通匮乏。
- example: His lack of work experience put him at a disadvantage during the job interview. || 他缺乏工作经验，这让他在求职面试中处于劣势。
- example: The team managed to win the game despite the disadvantage of playing without their captain. || 尽管没有队长参赛处于不利局面，这支队伍还是赢得了比赛。

### sense: v. 动词
- translationZh: 使处于不利地位，损害 ;;
- definitionZh: 使某人在特定情况中比其他人更难取得成功 ;;
- definitionEn: To make someone in a situation less likely to succeed than other people ;;
- example: The new tax policy disadvantages low-income families. || 新的税收政策对低收入家庭不利。
- example: Critics argue that the exam system disadvantages students from non-English speaking backgrounds. || 批评者认为该考试体系对来自非英语背景的学生不利。

## word: drawback
- uk: /ˈdrɔːbæk/
- us: /ˈdrɔːbæk/
- synonyms: disadvantage || 不利条件，缺点 ;; shortcoming || 短处，缺点 ;; flaw || 缺陷，瑕疵 ;; defect || 缺点，缺陷 ;; demerit || 过失，短处 ;;
- antonyms: advantage || 优势，优点 ;; benefit || 益处，好处 ;; merit || 优点，价值 ;;
- phrases: main drawback || 主要缺点 ;; potential drawback || 潜在弊端 ;; major drawback || 重大缺陷 ;; serious drawback || 严重弊端 ;; inherent drawback || 固有缺陷 ;;
- collocations: have a drawback || 有一个缺点 ;; overcome a drawback || 克服弊端 ;; point out a drawback || 指出缺陷 ;; suffer from a drawback || 受某一弊端困扰 ;; compensate for a drawback || 弥补缺陷 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The main drawback of sth is that... || 某事物的主要缺点是…… ;; One major drawback to doing sth is... || 做某事的一个重大弊端是…… ;; Despite its drawbacks, sth is still widely used. || 尽管存在缺点，某事物仍被广泛使用 ;;
- spokenExpressions: The only drawback is... || 唯一的缺点是…… ;; There's one small drawback, though. || 不过有个小问题。 ;; That's a pretty big drawback, isn't it? || 那可是个相当大的弊端，不是吗？ ;;
- idioms: no drawback without a corresponding advantage || 有弊必有利 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 缺点，劣势 ;; 弊端，不利条件 ;;
- definitionZh: 指事物存在的不足、缺陷，或者会带来负面影响的特征 ;; 指计划、系统、产品等存在的会降低其价值或实用性的问题 ;;
- definitionEn: a feature of something that makes it less useful, acceptable, or satisfactory than it could be ;; a problem or disadvantage that reduces the value or effectiveness of a plan, system, product etc. ;;
- example: The main drawback of the new software is its high cost. || 这款新软件的主要缺点是成本太高。
- example: One major drawback to living in the countryside is the lack of public transport. || 住在乡下的一大弊端是公共交通不足。
- example: Although the job pays well, its biggest drawback is the long working hours. || 虽然这份工作薪资不错，但最大的缺点是工作时间太长。

## word: edge
- uk: /edʒ/
- us: /edʒ/
- synonyms: brim || 边缘 ;; rim || 边，框 ;; verge || 边界，临界点 ;; margin || 边沿，余地 ;; fringe || 外围，边缘 ;;
- antonyms: center || 中心 ;; interior || 内部 ;; middle || 中间 ;;
- phrases: on the edge of || 在…的边缘 ;; cutting edge || 前沿，最前沿 ;; edge out || 排挤，险胜 ;; have an edge over || 比…有优势 ;; sharp edge || 锋利的刃 ;;
- collocations: sharp edge || 锋利的边缘 ;; competitive edge || 竞争优势 ;; cliff edge || 悬崖边缘 ;; edge forward || 慢慢向前移动 ;; cutting edge technology || 前沿技术 ;;
- sentencePatterns: have an edge over sb/sth || 表示比某人/某物更有优势 ;; edge one's way + 介词短语 || 表示小心翼翼地向某个方向移动 ;; on the edge of doing sth || 表示几乎要做某事，濒临做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: on edge || 紧张不安，烦躁 ;; take the edge off || 缓解，减弱（不快的感觉） ;; edge of your seat || 异常兴奋，全神贯注 ;;
- idioms: edge of one's seat || 看得入神，全神贯注 ;; have the edge on || 略胜一筹 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 边，边缘 ;; 优势 ;; 刃，锋利部分 ;; 尖锐，紧张感 ;;
- definitionZh: 物体的最外沿部分 ;; 相较于其他人或事物的有利条件 ;; 刀、剑等工具的锋利切割面 ;; 紧张、不安的情绪或尖锐的特质 ;;
- definitionEn: the outer or farthest part of an object or area ;; an advantage over other people or things ;; the sharp cutting part of a tool like a knife or sword ;; a feeling of nervous tension or sharp quality ;;
- example: Don't put the glass on the edge of the table, it might fall off. || 别把玻璃杯放在桌子边缘，它可能会掉下来。
- example: Having more work experience gives her an edge over other candidates for the job. || 拥有更多工作经验让她比其他求职候选人更有优势。
- example: The knife's edge is so blunt that it can't cut through the bread. || 这把刀的刃太钝了，连面包都切不动。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 缓慢移动，悄悄移动 ;; 排挤，险胜 ;;
- definitionZh: 小心翼翼地、小幅度地向某个方向移动 ;; 凭借微小的优势击败对手或把他人排挤出去 ;;
- definitionEn: to move slowly and carefully in a particular direction ;; to defeat someone or push them out of a position by a small amount ;;
- example: She edged closer to the door when she heard the strange noise outside. || 听到外面奇怪的声响，她慢慢向门口挪去。
- example: The local team edged out their opponents by one point in the final minute of the game. || 主队在比赛的最后一分钟以一分的优势险胜对手。
- example: He was edged out of his position after the company merged with a larger firm. || 公司和一家更大的企业合并后，他被排挤出了原来的岗位。

## word: merit
- uk: /ˈmerɪt/
- us: /ˈmerɪt/
- synonyms: virtue || 美德，优点 ;; excellence || 优秀，卓越 ;; worth || 价值，长处 ;; advantage || 优势，优点 ;;
- antonyms: demerit || 缺点，过失 ;; flaw || 缺陷，瑕疵 ;; shortcoming || 缺点，短处 ;;
- phrases: merit pay || 绩效工资 ;; merit scholarship || 奖学金， merit-based scholarship 择优奖学金 ;; on merit || 按实力，按优劣 ;; merit system ||  merit-based hiring 功绩制，择优录用制度 ;;
- collocations: artistic merit || 艺术价值 ;; merit consideration || 值得考虑 ;; merit attention || 值得关注 ;; merit award || 功绩奖 ;;
- sentencePatterns: merit + noun || 表示某事物值得拥有某种对待/关注，后接名词作宾语 ;; sth have the merit of (doing) sth || 表示某事物具有某方面的优点 ;; it is merit that + clause || 强调句结构，强调是实力/功绩起到了作用 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It has its merits. || 这有它的可取之处。 ;; Judge it on its own merits. || 要根据它本身的优劣来评判。 ;; The idea merits thinking about. || 这个想法值得琢磨一下。 ;;
- idioms: the merit of the case || 事件本身的是非曲直 ;;

### sense: 名词 n.
- translationZh: 优点，长处 ;; 价值，功绩 ;; （学校奖励的）良好，优等 ;;
- definitionZh: 人或事物具有的值得称赞、有价值的特质或优势 ;; 基于能力、贡献获得的功绩或价值，而非背景、关系等 ;; 教育体系中对学业表现的优等评级 ;;
- definitionEn: a good or worthy quality that someone or something has ;; the quality of being good and deserving praise, reward, or respect, based on ability and achievement rather than social status or personal connections ;; a good grade given to a student for their work ;;
- example: The main merit of this approach is its simplicity. || 这个方法的主要优点是简单易行。
- example: Candidates will be selected entirely on merit, without any preferential treatment. || 候选人将完全按实力选拔，不会有任何优待。
- example: He earned three merits for his excellent performance in the final exams. || 他因为期末考试表现优异获得了三个优等评级。

### sense: 动词 v.
- translationZh: 值得，应受 ;; 应获得 ;;
- definitionZh: 因为自身的特质或行为，理应得到某种对待、关注或奖励 ;;
- definitionEn: to deserve or be worthy of something such as attention, praise, or reward because of the qualities you have ;;
- example: This controversial proposal merits careful discussion before we make any decision. || 这个有争议的提案值得我们在做决定前仔细讨论。
- example: His outstanding contribution to the project merits a special bonus. || 他为这个项目做出的突出贡献理应获得一笔特别奖金。
- example: Such a minor issue hardly merits so much of our attention. || 这么小的问题实在不值得我们投入这么多注意力。

## word: advice
- uk: /ədˈvaɪs/
- us: /ədˈvaɪs/
- synonyms: suggestion || 建议 ;; guidance || 指导 ;; recommendation || 劝告 ;; tip || 提示 ;; counsel || 忠告 ;;
- antonyms: criticism || 批评 ;; opposition || 反对意见 ;; misguidance || 误导 ;;
- phrases: ask for advice || 征求意见 ;; give advice || 提出建议 ;; take/follow advice || 采纳建议 ;; seek expert advice || 咨询专家意见 ;; reject advice || 拒绝劝告 ;;
- collocations: practical advice || 实用建议 ;; legal advice || 法律意见 ;; medical advice || 医疗建议 ;; sound advice || 合理的劝告 ;; unsolicited advice || 主动提供的（不请自来的）建议 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is advisable to do sth on sb's advice || 按照某人的建议做某事是明智的 ;; sb advises that sb (should) do sth （同根词衍生句型）|| 某人建议某人做某事（advice对应的动词advise常用虚拟语气结构）;; Could you give me some advice on sth? || 用于请求对方就某方面给出建议的常用疑问句结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: A word of advice. || 给你个小建议。 ;; Take my advice, you won't regret it. || 听我的准没错。 ;; Let me give you a piece of advice. || 我跟你说句掏心窝的建议。 ;;
- idioms: a piece of advice || 一条建议（注：advice为不可数名词，表达数量需搭配量词）;; take advice on board || 认真考虑并采纳建议 ;;

### sense: noun [U]
- translationZh: 劝告 ;; 建议 ;; 意见 ;; 忠告 ;;
- definitionZh: 针对某一问题、场景，向他人提出的供参考的行动指导或看法 ;; 专业领域的权威指导意见，如法律、医疗等领域的专业建议 ;;
- definitionEn: an opinion or recommendation offered as a guide to action, conduct, etc. ;; formal or professional guidance given by an expert on a specific subject ;;
- example: My teacher gave me some useful advice on how to improve my English writing. || 我的老师就如何提高我的英语写作水平给了我一些很有用的建议。
- example: Before you sign the contract, you should get legal advice from a lawyer. || 在你签合同之前，应该先找律师获取法律意见。
- example: I regret not following my parents' advice when I chose my major. || 我选专业的时候后悔没听父母的劝告。



## word: criticism
- uk: /ˈkrɪtɪsɪzəm/
- us: /ˈkrɪtɪsɪzəm/
- synonyms: critique || 评论，评判 ;; censure || 指责，谴责 ;; reproach || 责备，批评 ;; disparagement || 贬低，诋毁 ;;
- antonyms: praise || 赞扬，称赞 ;; compliment || 恭维，赞美 ;; approval || 认可，赞同 ;;
- phrases: literary criticism || 文学批评 ;; constructive criticism || 建设性批评 ;; self-criticism || 自我批评 ;; public criticism || 公众批评 ;;
- collocations: draw criticism || 招致批评 ;; face criticism || 面临批评 ;; level criticism at sb || 抨击某人 ;; harsh criticism || 严厉批评 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There has been widespread criticism of + n. || 表示某事物遭到广泛批评的句型 ;; sb's criticism of + n. + centres/centers on + n. || 表示某人对某事物的批评集中在某方面的句型 ;; The report came in for heavy criticism from + sb. || 表示报告等遭到某方严厉批评的句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Take it easy, it's just constructive criticism. || 放轻松，这只是建设性的批评而已。 ;; There's no need to take that criticism personally. || 没必要把那个批评当成针对你个人的。 ;; A little bit of criticism never hurt anyone. || 一点批评又不会害到人。 ;;
- idioms: a storm of criticism || 铺天盖地的批评，批评的浪潮 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 批评，指责 ;; 评论，评价 ;;
- definitionZh: 对某人或某事物的缺点、错误进行的指责性表述 ;; 对文学、艺术、作品等的专业分析和评价 ;;
- definitionEn: the act of expressing disapproval of sb/sth and opinions about their faults or bad qualities ;; the activity of making careful judgements about the good and bad qualities of books, films, music, etc. ;;
- example: The plan has attracted fierce criticism from environmental groups. || 该计划遭到了环保组织的猛烈批评。
- example: Her literary criticism focuses on the way 19th-century novels portrayed women. || 她的文学评论聚焦于19世纪小说塑造女性的方式。
- example: We should be open to fair criticism and willing to correct our mistakes. || 我们应该乐于接受合理的批评，并且愿意改正自己的错误。

## word: guidance

- us: /ˈɡaɪdns/

- definitionEn: help and advice that is given to someone, especially about what to do in a particular situation or for their development ;; the act or process of guiding someone or something ;;
- example: Students can seek guidance from their tutors on academic issues. || 学生可以就学术问题向导师寻求指导。
- example: The project was completed smoothly under the guidance of the experienced engineer. || 这个项目在经验丰富的工程师的指导下顺利完成。
- example: Many schools provide career guidance to help graduates choose suitable jobs. || 很多学校会提供职业咨询，帮助毕业生选择合适的工作。

## word: opposition
- uk: /ˌɒpəˈzɪʃn/
- us: /ˌɑːpəˈzɪʃn/
- synonyms: resistance || 抵抗 ;; objection || 反对 ;; rivalry || 对抗 ;; dissent || 异议 ;; counterparty || 对手方 ;;
- antonyms: support || 支持 ;; agreement || 同意 ;; backing || 拥护 ;;
- phrases: in opposition || 反对；处于反对党地位 ;; opposition party || 反对党 ;; meet with opposition || 遭到反对 ;; strong opposition || 强烈反对 ;; opposition to sth || 对某事的反对 ;;
- collocations: face opposition || 面临反对 ;; voice opposition || 表达反对 ;; overcome opposition || 克服反对 ;; fierce opposition || 激烈反对 ;; official opposition || 官方反对党 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There is strong opposition to + noun/doing sth || 表示“对某事存在强烈反对” ;; Opposition to + sth + come from + sb || 表示“对某事的反对来自某群体” ;; be in opposition to + sth || 表示“与某事相悖/反对某事” ;;
- spokenExpressions: There's a lot of opposition to that plan. || 那个计划遭到了很多反对。 ;; The opposition is putting up a good fight. || 对手这边现在打得很猛。 ;; I don't understand why there's so much opposition to this idea. || 我搞不懂为什么这个想法有这么多人反对。 ;;
- idioms: the loyal opposition || 忠诚反对党（指议会中对执政党的政策持反对立场但仍拥护国家体制的反对党） ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 反对，反抗 ;; 对手，反对派；反对党 ;;
- definitionZh: 对某一计划、观点等表示不同意或抵制的态度或行为 ;; 与另一方立场对立的个人、团体或政党 ;;
- definitionEn: Disagreement with something, often actively trying to stop or change it. ;; A person, group, or political party that is against another and competes with them. ;;
- example: The proposal was abandoned in the face of strong public opposition. || 面对公众的强烈反对，这项提案被放弃了。
- example: The opposition has criticized the government's new tax policy severely. || 反对党严厉批评了政府的新税收政策。
- example: We didn't expect to meet so much opposition when we suggested moving the office. || 我们提议搬迁办公室的时候，没料到会遭到这么多反对。

## word: recommendation
- uk: /ˌrekəmenˈdeɪʃn/
- us: /ˌrekəmenˈdeɪʃn/
- synonyms: suggestion || 建议 ;; endorsement || 认可，支持 ;; referral || 推荐，介绍 ;; tip || 贴士，建议 ;;
- antonyms: criticism || 批评 ;; disapproval || 不赞成，反对 ;;
- phrases: letter of recommendation || 推荐信 ;; recommendation letter || 推荐信 ;; job recommendation || 工作推荐 ;; product recommendation || 产品推荐 ;;
- collocations: make a recommendation || 提出建议 ;; accept a recommendation || 接受建议 ;; follow a recommendation || 遵从建议 ;; provide a recommendation || 提供推荐 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is recommended that + (should) do || 用于表达根据建议应当做某事，that从句常用虚拟语气 ;; On the recommendation of sb, sb did sth || 用于说明某人是在他人的推荐下做了某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Do you have any recommendations? || 你有什么推荐的吗？ ;; I can give you my personal recommendation. || 我可以给你我个人的推荐。 ;; Take my recommendation, you won't regret it. || 听我的推荐，你不会后悔的。 ;;
- idioms: recommendation on trust || 信誉推荐，凭信用举荐 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 正式建议，提议 ;; 推荐，介绍 ;; 推荐信 ;;
- definitionZh: 针对某一情况给出的正式的行动建议 ;; 告诉他人某人/某物很好、适合某用途的行为 ;; 由了解你能力的人撰写的、用于申请工作或入学的正式信件 ;;
- definitionEn: an official suggestion about the best thing to do in a particular situation ;; the act of telling someone that a person or thing is good and suitable for a particular purpose ;; an official letter written by someone who knows you well, describing your character and abilities, usually to help you get a job or a place at a college ;;
- example: The committee made a number of recommendations for improving safety standards. || 委员会提出了多项提高安全标准的建议。
- example: I got the job on the recommendation of a former colleague. || 我是在前同事的推荐下得到这份工作的。
- example: She asked her professor to write her a recommendation for graduate school. || 她请教授为她写一份研究生院申请的推荐信。
- example: The restaurant is great, so I will definitely add it to my list of recommendations. || 这家餐厅很棒，所以我肯定会把它加到我的推荐清单里。

## word: suggestion
- uk: /səˈdʒestʃən/
- us: /səˈdʒestʃən/

- phrases: make a suggestion || 提出建议 ;; follow a suggestion || 采纳建议 ;; reject a suggestion || 拒绝建议 ;;

- sentencePatterns: make a suggestion that + (should) do || 提出……的建议，从句用虚拟语气 ;; There is a suggestion that + clause || 有迹象表明/有建议称…… ;;
- spokenExpressions: Any suggestions? || 有什么建议吗？;; Good suggestion! || 好主意！;; Just a suggestion. || 只是个建议哦。;;

### sense: 名词
