- definitionZh: 为改进情况或解决问题而提出的想法或意见 ;; 事物隐约显露的细微特征或可能性 ;;
- definitionEn: an idea or plan that you offer for someone to consider ;; a slight amount or sign of something ;;
- example: Do you have any suggestions for how to improve our team's efficiency? || 你对如何提高我们团队的效率有什么建议吗？
- example: The manager decided to accept the customer's suggestion to optimize the product packaging. || 经理决定采纳客户优化产品包装的建议。
- example: There was a suggestion of annoyance in his voice when he responded to the unreasonable request. || 他回应那个不合理请求时，语气里带着一丝恼怒。

## word: advise
- uk: /ədˈvaɪz/
- us: /ədˈvaɪz/
- synonyms: suggest || 建议 ;; recommend || 推荐，劝告 ;; counsel || 忠告，商议 ;; urge || 敦促，力劝 ;; caution || 提醒，警告 ;;
- antonyms: mislead || 误导 ;; deceive || 欺骗 ;; discourage || 劝阻 ;;
- phrases: advise against || 建议不要做… ;; advise sb on sth || 就某事给某人提建议 ;; advise sb of sth || 告知某人某事 ;; advise to do || 建议做… ;;
- collocations: strongly advise || 强烈建议 ;; advise carefully || 谨慎劝告 ;; professionally advise || 专业建议 ;; advise patients || 给患者提建议 ;; advise students || 指导学生 ;;
- sentencePatterns: advise sb (not) to do sth || 建议某人（不）做某事，后接不定式作宾语补足语 ;; It is advised that... (should) do || 据建议……，从句用虚拟语气，should可省略 ;; advise doing sth || 建议做某事，后接动名词作宾语 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'd advise against that. || 我劝你别那么做。 ;; I'd advise you to think twice. || 我建议你三思而后行。 ;; Please advise. || 请给出建议，烦请告知。 ;;
- idioms: advise with one's pillow || 彻夜思考后再作决定 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 建议，劝告 ;; 通知，告知 ;; 提供咨询，指导 ;;
- definitionZh: 针对某人的行为、决策等给出有用的意见或指导；正式地将某事告知某人；为特定群体提供专业的咨询服务 ;;
- definitionEn: to give someone suggestions about what they should do, how to behave etc.; to formally tell someone about something; to provide professional guidance and suggestions for a specific group of people ;;
- example: The doctor advised him to stop smoking immediately to protect his lung health. || 医生建议他立刻戒烟，以保护肺部健康。
- example: Please advise us of any changes to your contact information as soon as possible. || 如果你的联系方式有任何变动，请尽快告知我们。
- example: Experienced mentors will advise new employees on company policies and work procedures during the onboarding period. || 入职期间，经验丰富的导师会就公司制度和工作流程为新员工提供指导。
- example: I would advise booking the hotel in advance if you plan to travel during the peak tourist season. || 如果你打算在旅游旺季出行，我建议你提前预订酒店。



## word: counsel
- uk: /ˈkaʊnsl/
- us: /ˈkaʊnsl/
- synonyms: advice || 建议 ;; guidance || 指导 ;; consultation || 磋商 ;; attorney || 律师 ;; legal representative || 法定代理人 ;;
- antonyms: misguidance || 误导 ;; opposition || 反对意见 ;;
- phrases: legal counsel || 法律顾问 ;; take counsel || 征求意见 ;; counsel for the defence || 辩护律师 ;; give counsel || 提出建议 ;;
- collocations: seek counsel from sb || 向某人征求建议 ;; provide counsel on sth || 就某事提供指导 ;; independent counsel || 独立检察官 ;; professional counsel || 专业建议 ;;
- sentencePatterns: counsel sb against sth || 建议某人不要做某事 ;; counsel sb to do sth || 建议某人做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: A word of counsel || 给你一句忠告 ;; If you'll take my counsel || 如果你听我的建议 ;;
- idioms: counsel of perfection || 达不到的理想建议 ;; hold counsel with sb || 与某人磋商 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 建议，忠告 ;; 法律顾问，律师 ;;
- definitionZh: 针对特定问题给出的专业指导或建议 ;; 为个人、机构提供法律服务的律师或法律团队 ;;
- definitionEn: Professional advice or guidance given regarding a particular decision or course of action ;; a lawyer or group of lawyers who provide legal advice and representation for a person or organization ;;
- example: The company sought independent legal counsel before signing the contract. || 该公司在签署合同前咨询了独立法律顾问。
- example: Her wise counsel helped me get through the most difficult period of my career. || 她明智的忠告帮我度过了职业生涯中最艰难的时期。
- example: The court appointed counsel for the defendant who could not afford a lawyer. || 法院为请不起律师的被告指定了辩护律师。

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 建议，劝告 ;; 提供专业咨询 ;;
- definitionZh: 向某人给出谨慎、专业的建议，指导其做出决定 ;; 为有需要的人提供专业的咨询服务，尤指心理、法律相关的指导 ;;
- definitionEn: To give advice and guidance to someone, especially about important decisions they need to make ;; to provide professional support and advice to people with personal, legal or psychological problems ;;
- example: The therapist counsels teenagers who are struggling with anxiety and depression. || 这位治疗师为受焦虑和抑郁困扰的青少年提供咨询服务。
- example: We were counselled against making hasty decisions during the negotiation. || 我们被建议不要在谈判期间做出仓促的决定。
- example: The career coach counselled him to consider a career shift to the renewable energy sector. || 职业教练建议他考虑转行到可再生能源领域。

## word: deceive
- uk: /dɪˈsiːv/
- us: /dɪˈsiːv/
- synonyms: trick || 欺骗，哄骗 ;; mislead || 误导，引入歧途 ;; dupe || 诈骗，愚弄 ;; beguile || 欺骗，诱骗 ;; defraud || 欺诈，骗取 ;;
- antonyms: honest || 诚实，坦诚 ;; disclose || 透露，公开 ;; inform || 告知，通知 ;;
- phrases: deceive oneself || 自欺欺人 ;; deceive sb into doing sth || 骗某人做某事 ;; be deceived by appearances || 被表象欺骗 ;; deceive sb out of sth || 骗取某人的某物 ;;
- collocations: deliberately deceive || 故意欺骗 ;; attempt to deceive || 企图欺骗 ;; easily deceive || 轻易欺骗 ;; deceive the public || 欺骗公众 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb deceive sb about sth || 某人在某事上欺骗某人 ;; sb be deceived into doing sth || 某人被骗去做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Don't try to deceive me! || 别想骗我！ ;; You can't deceive yourself any longer. || 你不能再自欺欺人了。 ;; He deceived us all, didn't he? || 他骗了我们所有人，不是吗？ ;;
- idioms: deceive the eye || 掩人耳目 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 欺骗 ;; 蒙骗 ;; 误导 ;;
- definitionZh: 故意向他人提供虚假信息，或隐瞒真实情况，使他人产生错误认知的行为 ;; （事物）给人造成错误的印象，使人产生误解 ;;
- definitionEn: To deliberately make someone believe something that is not true, in order to get an advantage for yourself ;; To give a wrong impression of something, leading people to have an incorrect understanding of it ;;
- example: He tried to deceive the police about his real identity. || 他试图在自己的真实身份上欺骗警方。
- example: Many consumers were deceived into buying counterfeit products by the false advertisement. || 很多消费者被虚假广告误导，购买了假冒产品。
- example: The calm surface of the lake can deceive you into thinking it is safe to swim in, but the water is actually very deep and cold. || 湖面平静的表象会误导你，让你以为在这里游泳很安全，但实际上湖水又深又冷。

## word: mislead
- uk: /ˌmɪsˈliːd/
- us: /ˌmɪsˈliːd/
- synonyms: deceive || 欺骗 ;; misinform || 误导，提供错误信息 ;; delude || 哄骗，迷惑 ;; beguile || 诱骗，哄骗 ;;
- antonyms: guide || 引导，指导 ;; inform || 告知，通知 ;; enlighten || 启发，开导 ;;
- phrases: mislead the public || 误导公众 ;; mislead consumers || 误导消费者 ;; mislead sb into doing sth || 误导某人做某事 ;; deliberately mislead || 故意误导 ;;
- collocations: deliberately mislead || 故意误导 ;; unintentionally mislead || 无意误导 ;; mislead voters || 误导选民 ;; mislead customers || 误导客户 ;; mislead with false information || 用虚假信息误导 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb be misled by sth || 某人被某事误导（被动语态，说明误导的来源） ;; sth mislead sb into doing sth || 某事误导某人做某事（主动语态，说明误导导致的行为） ;; The advertisement mislead sb about sth || 广告在某方面误导某人（说明特定场景下的误导行为） ;;
- spokenExpressions: Don't let their words mislead you. || 别被他们的话误导了。 ;; I think you've been misled. || 我觉得你被误导了。 ;; The information they gave was meant to mislead. || 他们给的信息就是用来误导人的。 ;;
- idioms: mislead someone down the garden path || 误导某人，欺骗某人 ;;

### sense: v.（动词）
- translationZh: 误导，使产生错误印象 ;; 欺骗，哄骗 ;;
- definitionZh: 故意或无意地给他人提供错误信息，引导他人产生错误的想法或做出错误的行为 ;; 用不实信息或虚假表象蒙骗他人，使其偏离正确的判断 ;;
- definitionEn: to give someone false or inaccurate information, often deliberately, in order to make them believe something that is not true ;; to cause someone to have a wrong idea or impression about someone or something ;;
- example: The advertisement was designed to mislead customers into thinking the product was on sale. || 这则广告旨在误导消费者，让他们以为该产品正在促销。
- example: Don't be misled by his friendly appearance—he's actually a very ruthless businessman. || 别被他友善的外表误导了——他实际上是个非常冷酷的商人。
- example: The spokesperson apologized for the statement that had misled the public. || 发言人对那篇误导了公众的声明表示道歉。

## word: recommend

- us: /ˌrekəˈmend/

- sentencePatterns: recommend + sb/sth + for sth || 用于表达推荐人/物用于某用途或岗位等 ;; recommend + (that) sb (should) do sth || that引导宾语从句，从句常用虚拟语气，should可省略 ;; recommend + sb + to do sth || 用于表达建议某人做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I can't recommend it enough. || 我真的超推荐这个。 ;; Would you recommend anything here? || 你能推荐这儿的什么好东西吗？ ;; I'd highly recommend you try it. || 我强烈建议你试试。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms:

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 推荐，举荐 ;; 建议，劝告 ;; 使受欢迎，使可取 ;;
- definitionZh: 向别人介绍认为好的人或事物，希望对方采纳或任用 ;; 针对某个情况给出合理的行动意见，希望对方遵从 ;; 具备某种特质从而显得有吸引力、值得选择 ;;
- definitionEn: to tell someone that a particular person or thing is good or suitable for a particular purpose or job ;; to advise someone to do a particular thing ;; to have a particular good quality that makes something seem attractive and worth choosing ;;
- example: I recommend this restaurant to anyone who likes Italian food. || 我向所有喜欢意大利菜的人推荐这家餐厅。
- example: Doctors recommend that all children should be vaccinated against measles. || 医生建议所有儿童都应该接种麻疹疫苗。
- example: The low price and high durability of this phone really recommends it to students on a tight budget. || 这款手机价格低廉且耐用，对于预算紧张的学生非常适合选择它。

## word: suggest
- uk: /səˈdʒest/
- us: /səˈdʒest/
- synonyms: propose || 提议 ;; recommend || 推荐 ;; advise || 建议 ;; imply || 暗示 ;; indicate || 表明 ;;
- antonyms: dictate || 命令 ;; demand || 要求 ;; order || 指令 ;;
- phrases: suggest doing sth || 建议做某事 ;; suggest that sb (should) do sth || 建议某人应该做某事 ;; it is suggested that || 有人建议 ;; suggest sth to sb || 向某人建议某事 ;;
- collocations: strongly suggest || 强烈建议 ;; tentatively suggest || 试探性地提出 ;; research suggests || 研究表明 ;; suggest an alternative || 提出备选方案 ;;
- sentencePatterns: suggest + gerund || 后接动名词作宾语，表建议的动作 ;; suggest + (that) clause (with subjunctive) || 后接that从句，从句常用(should+)动词原形的虚拟语气，表建议 ;; suggest + noun phrase || 后接名词短语，可表建议、暗示等含义 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'd like to suggest that... || 我想建议… ;; What are you suggesting? || 你这话是什么意思？ ;; Can I suggest something? || 我能提个建议吗？ ;;
- idioms: suggest itself || （想法、念头）自动浮现，出现在脑海中 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 建议，提议 ;; 暗示，表明 ;; 推荐 ;;
- definitionZh: 向他人提出可供参考的想法、计划或行动方案； ;; 间接表达某种意思，或通过迹象、证据等显示某种情况； ;; 介绍认为合适的人或事物供对方考虑。 ;;
- definitionEn: to put forward an idea, plan, or course of action for someone to consider; ;; to imply or indicate something indirectly, or to show something through signs or evidence; ;; to recommend someone or something that you think is suitable for a particular purpose. ;;
- example: I suggest going to the Italian restaurant downtown for our anniversary dinner. || 我建议我们去市中心的意大利餐厅吃周年纪念晚餐。
- example: The dark clouds in the sky suggest that it will rain soon. || 天上的乌云表明很快就要下雨了。
- example: My doctor suggested that I should take a short break from work to reduce stress. || 我的医生建议我暂时停下工作休息一小段时间来缓解压力。

## word: afford
- uk: /əˈfɔːd/
- us: /əˈfɔːrd/
- synonyms: bear || 承担 ;; sustain || 承受 ;; provide || 提供 ;; supply || 供给 ;; furnish || 供应 ;;
- antonyms: lack || 缺乏 ;; deny || 拒绝给予 ;;
- phrases: afford to do || 负担得起做某事 ;; can't afford || 买不起；承担不起 ;; afford sb sth || 给某人提供某物 ;; afford an opportunity || 提供机会 ;;
- collocations: can afford || 负担得起 ;; hardly afford || 几乎负担不起 ;; afford a house || 买得起房子 ;; afford support || 提供支持 ;; afford protection || 提供保护 ;;
- sentencePatterns: afford + sb + sth || 双宾语结构，表示给某人提供某物 ;; can/can't afford + to do sth || 表示有/没有足够的钱或能力做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I can't afford it. || 我买不起。 ;; How can you afford that? || 你怎么买得起那个的？ ;;
- idioms: can't afford to look a gift horse in the mouth || 没资格对送上门的好处挑三拣四 ;;

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 买得起，负担得起；提供，给予；承受得起 ;;
- definitionZh: 有足够的钱或时间去购买、做某件事；为某人提供某种东西、机会等；能够承担某件事带来的后果 ;;
- definitionEn: to have enough money or time to be able to buy or do something; to provide someone with something, such as an opportunity or advantage; to be able to bear the cost or consequence of something ;;
- example: I can't afford to buy a new car right now. || 我现在买不起新车。
- example: The program affords young people the chance to gain work experience. || 这个项目为年轻人提供了获得工作经验的机会。
- example: We can't afford to make any mistakes on this important project. || 在这个重要项目上我们承担不起任何差错的后果。



## word: bear
- uk: /beə(r)/
- us: /ber/
- synonyms: endure || 忍受 ;; tolerate || 容忍 ;; carry || 携带 ;; produce || 出产 ;;
- antonyms: resist || 抗拒 ;; avoid || 避开 ;; discard || 丢弃 ;;
- phrases: bear in mind || 记住 ;; bear fruit || 取得成果 ;; bear with || 耐心对待 ;; bear out || 证实 ;;
- collocations: bear pain || 忍受痛苦 ;; bear responsibility || 承担责任 ;; bear a grudge || 心怀怨恨 ;; bear a child || 生育孩子 ;;
- sentencePatterns: bear + noun/pronoun || 表示承受、携带某个事物 ;; can't bear + doing/to do || 表示无法忍受做某事 ;; bear it that + clause || 表示忍受某种情况 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Bear with me for a second. || 稍等我一下。 ;; I can't bear it anymore. || 我再也受不了了。 ;; Keep that in mind, will you? 不对，应该是Bear that in mind. || 记住这点哦。 ;;
- idioms: bear the brunt of || 首当其冲承受（打击等） ;; bear one's cross || 承受自己的苦难 ;;
- slang: bear market || 熊市（金融俚语） ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 忍受 ;; 承担 ;; 携带 ;; 生育 ;; 结出（果实） ;;
- definitionZh: 承受痛苦、压力等不愉快的事物；担负责任、义务等；随身带着物品；女性或雌性动物生育后代；植物结出果实、花朵；
- definitionEn: to accept or deal with something painful or unpleasant without complaining; to take responsibility for something; to carry something with you; for a woman or female animal to give birth to a baby; for a plant to produce flowers or fruit;
- example: She can't bear being criticized in public. || 她无法忍受在公共场合被批评。
- example: The old tree bears a lot of apples every autumn. || 这棵老树每年秋天都结很多苹果。
- example: You have to bear the consequences of your own actions. || 你必须为自己的行为承担后果。

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 熊 ;; （证券市场的）看跌者，空头 ;;
- definitionZh: 一种大型的哺乳动物，毛发浓密，四肢粗壮；证券市场中预料价格下跌的投资者，对应的市场行情称为熊市；
- definitionEn: a large strong wild animal with thick fur and sharp claws; an investor who expects the price of stocks or other assets to fall, and the market with falling prices is called a bear market;
- example: We saw a brown bear when we hiked in the forest last weekend. || 我们上周末在森林徒步的时候看到了一只棕熊。
- example: Bears are selling a lot of shares recently, pushing the index lower. || 空头最近在大量抛售股票，推动指数走低。
- example: The little kid got a fluffy teddy bear as his birthday gift. || 这个小孩收到了一只毛茸茸的泰迪熊作为生日礼物。

## word: deny
- uk: /dɪˈnaɪ/
- us: /dɪˈnaɪ/
- synonyms: refute || 驳斥，否认 ;; contradict || 反驳，否定 ;; reject || 拒绝，驳回 ;; disavow || 否认，不承认 ;; repudiate || 拒绝接受，否定 ;;
- antonyms: confirm || 确认，证实 ;; admit || 承认，认可 ;; acknowledge || 承认，确认 ;;
- phrases: deny oneself || 克制，节制 ;; deny a request || 拒绝请求 ;; deny the truth || 否认事实 ;; deny access to || 禁止进入，拒绝访问 ;; deny responsibility || 否认责任 ;;
- collocations: flatly deny || 断然否认 ;; publicly deny || 公开否认 ;; categorically deny || 明确否认 ;; deny a claim || 驳回索赔 ;; deny allegations || 否认指控 ;;
- sentencePatterns: deny doing sth || 否认做过某事，后接动名词作宾语 ;; deny sb sth || 拒绝给予某人某物，接双宾语结构 ;; It cannot be denied that... || 不可否认的是……，it作形式主语的主语从句结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: There's no denying it. || 这无可否认。 ;; I can't deny it. || 我不否认这点。 ;; You can't deny the facts. || 你不能否认事实。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms: deny the fact || 否认事实 ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: 否认，不承认 ;; 拒绝给予，拒绝（请求、要求等） ;; 拒绝……进入，剥夺……的权利 ;;
- definitionZh: 声称某事不真实或没有发生 ;; 不允许某人拥有或使用某物，不满足某人的请求 ;; 拒绝让某人进入某个场所或享有某项权利 ;;
- definitionEn: to state that something is not true or did not happen ;; to refuse to give someone something or allow them to have something ;; to refuse to allow someone to enter a place or have a right ;;
- example: He denied that he had stolen the money. || 他否认自己偷了钱。
- example: The government has denied the refugees access to the border. || 政府拒绝让难民进入边境。
- example: She denied any involvement in the scandal. || 她否认与这起丑闻有任何关联。
- example: The insurance company denied his claim for damages. || 保险公司驳回了他的损害赔偿索赔。
- example: You can't deny that she's a very talented singer. || 你不可否认她是个非常有天赋的歌手。

## word: lack
- uk: /læk/
- us: /læk/
- synonyms: shortage || 短缺 ;; deficiency || 不足 ;; absence || 缺失 ;; want || 匮乏 ;; scarcity || 稀少 ;;
- antonyms: abundance || 充足 ;; surplus || 过剩 ;; sufficiency || 足够 ;;
- phrases: lack of || 缺乏，不足 ;; for lack of || 因为缺少 ;; lack confidence || 缺乏信心 ;; lack experience || 缺乏经验 ;;
- collocations: serious lack || 严重缺乏 ;; total lack || 完全没有 ;; lack behind || 落后 ;; lack the skills || 缺少技能 ;;
- sentencePatterns: lack + 名词 || 直接接宾语，表示缺少某事物 ;; there is a lack of + 名词 || 表示某事物存在短缺的情况 ;; for lack of + 名词 || 引导原因状语，表示因为缺少某事物 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I lack words to describe it. || 我都没法用语言形容这个了。 ;; There's a serious lack of options here. || 这儿根本没什么可选的。 ;; We're lacking a bit of time right now. || 我们这会儿时间有点不够。 ;;
- idioms: lack for nothing || 什么都不缺，丰衣足食 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 缺乏；不足；短缺；
- definitionZh: 指某种需要或想要的事物数量不足的状态；某事物不存在或数量不够的情况；
- definitionEn: the state of not having enough of something that you need or want; the absence or insufficiency of something. ;;
- example: The main problem we face is a lack of funding. || 我们面临的主要问题是资金短缺。
- example: Her only problem is a lack of confidence when speaking in public. || 她唯一的问题是当众讲话时缺乏自信。
- example: Many children in the area suffer from a lack of proper nutrition. || 该地区的很多儿童都因缺乏足够的营养而受折磨。

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 缺乏；缺少；没有；
- definitionZh: 不拥有某事物，或拥有的数量不足；在某方面存在不足；
- definitionEn: to not have something, or to not have enough of it; to be deficient in a particular quality or attribute. ;;
- example: He lacks the experience needed for this senior position. || 他缺少这个高级岗位所需的经验。
- example: The town lacks public transport options after 10 p.m. || 晚上10点之后这个小镇就没有什么公共交通可选了。
- example: You will not lack for support if you decide to take the job. || 如果你决定接受这份工作，你不会缺少支持的。

## word: provide
- uk: /prəˈvaɪd/
- us: /prəˈvaɪd/
- synonyms: supply || 供应，提供 ;; offer || 提供，给予 ;; furnish || 供应，配备 ;; afford || 提供，给予 ;; grant || 授予，提供 ;;
- antonyms: withhold || 拒绝给予，扣留 ;; deprive || 剥夺，使丧失 ;; take || 拿走，夺取 ;;
- phrases: provide for || 供养，为…做准备 ;; provide sb with sth || 给某人提供某物 ;; provide sth for sb || 为某人提供某物 ;; provide against || 预防，防备 ;; provide services || 提供服务 ;;
- collocations: provide financial support || 提供资金支持 ;; provide legal advice || 提供法律咨询 ;; provide training opportunities || 提供培训机会 ;; provide adequate protection || 提供充分保护 ;; provide free meals || 提供免费餐食 ;;
- sentencePatterns: provide sb with sth || 双宾语结构，主语+provide+间接宾语+with+直接宾语，表达“给某人提供某物” ;; provide sth for sb || 双宾语转换结构，主语+provide+直接宾语+for+间接宾语，表达“为某人提供某物” ;; It is provided that... || 形式主语句型，it作形式主语，that引导主语从句，表达“规定…” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Can you provide me with more details? || 你能给我提供更多细节吗？ ;; We'll provide everything you need. || 我们会提供你需要的所有东西。 ;; The hotel provides free breakfast for guests. || 这家酒店为客人提供免费早餐。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms:

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 提供，供给 ;; 供养，抚养 ;; 规定，预先约定 ;;
- definitionZh: 为某人或某事提供所需的物品、服务、信息等 ;; 为家人、受抚养者提供生活所需的钱、物资等 ;; 法律、协议等明确写明相关规则或要求 ;;
- definitionEn: to give sb sth that they need or want, especially in order to satisfy a particular purpose ;; to give enough money, food, etc. for sb to live on ;; to state a particular rule, condition, etc. in a law, agreement or official document ;;
- example: The local government plans to provide free medical care for low-income families. || 当地政府计划为低收入家庭提供免费医疗服务。
- example: He has three children and a disabled parent to provide for, so he works two jobs. || 他要供养三个孩子和一位残疾的父母，所以打两份工。
- example: The contract provides that either party can terminate the agreement with 30 days' notice. || 合同规定任何一方提前30天通知即可终止协议。

## word: sustain
- uk: /səˈsteɪn/
- us: /səˈsteɪn/
- synonyms: maintain || 维持，保持 ;; support || 支撑，支持 ;; uphold || 维护，支持 ;; endure || 忍受，承受 ;;
- antonyms: abandon || 放弃，丢弃 ;; terminate || 终止，结束 ;; undermine || 破坏，削弱 ;;
- phrases: sustain economic growth || 维持经济增长 ;; sustain injuries || 遭受伤害 ;; sustain a family || 供养家庭 ;; sustain public interest || 保持公众兴趣 ;;
- collocations: sustain efforts || 持续努力 ;; sustain damage || 蒙受损失 ;; sustain a argument || 支撑论点 ;; sustain life || 维持生命 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sustain sb/sth from sth || 表示保护某人/某物免受某事物伤害 ;; It is difficult to sustain + 名词短语 || 表示维持某事物是困难的 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I can't sustain this pace any longer. || 我再也撑不住这个节奏了。 ;; How do you sustain your energy all day? || 你是怎么一整天都保持精力充沛的？ ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 维持，保持 ;; 支撑，承受 ;; 遭受，蒙受 ;; 供养，赡养 ;;
- definitionZh: 使某事物持续存在或保持正常状态 ;; 承受住重量、压力等不垮掉 ;; 遭受伤害、损失等不好的事情 ;; 提供必要的资源维持某人或生命的存活 ;;
- definitionEn: to make something continue to exist or function normally ;; to bear the weight or pressure of something without breaking or falling ;; to experience something bad such as injury or loss ;; to provide someone or something with the necessary things to live ;;
- example: The company has managed to sustain its leading position in the market for over a decade. || 这家公司成功维持其市场领先地位超过十年。
- example: The ice shelf was too thin to sustain the weight of the heavy truck. || 冰架太薄，承受不住重型卡车的重量。
- example: He sustained severe head injuries in the car accident. || 他在那场车祸中头部受了重伤。
- example: The small farm produces enough food to sustain the whole family. || 这个小农场产出的粮食足够供养全家人。

## word: afraid
- uk: /əˈfreɪd/
- us: /əˈfreɪd/
- synonyms: scared || 害怕的，恐惧的 ;; frightened || 受惊的，害怕的 ;; terrified || 极度惊恐的 ;; fearful || 担心的，害怕的 ;; apprehensive || 忧虑的，不安的 ;;
- antonyms: brave || 勇敢的 ;; fearless || 无畏的 ;; unafraid || 不害怕的 ;;
- phrases: be afraid of || 害怕……，担忧…… ;; be afraid to do sth || 不敢做某事 ;; I'm afraid so || 恐怕是这样 ;; I'm afraid not || 恐怕不是这样 ;; be afraid for sb/sth || 为……担心 ;;
- collocations: deathly afraid || 怕得要死 ;; secretly afraid || 暗自害怕 ;; afraid of the dark || 怕黑 ;; afraid of making mistakes || 害怕犯错 ;; hardly afraid || 几乎不害怕 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be afraid + that从句 || 表示担心、恐怕会发生某事，that可省略 ;; be afraid + of + 名词/动名词 || 表示害怕某事物或害怕做某事 ;; be afraid + to + 动词原形 || 表示因害怕而不敢做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'm afraid I can't || 恐怕我不行 ;; I'm afraid I have to go || 恐怕我得走了 ;; Don't be afraid || 别害怕 ;;
- idioms: be afraid of one's own shadow || 胆小如鼠，极易受惊 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 害怕的，恐惧的 ;; 担心的，忧虑的 ;; 抱歉的，遗憾的（用于礼貌地表示不好的消息或拒绝） ;;
- definitionZh: 因可能发生的危险、痛苦等而感到恐惧的 ;; 对某事可能产生的坏结果感到担忧的 ;; 用于礼貌地告知他人令人不快的消息、拒绝请求等，带有歉意的 ;;
- definitionEn: feeling fear or anxiety because you think something bad might happen or has happened ;; worried that something unpleasant might happen ;; used to politely tell someone something that is not pleasant, or to politely refuse an offer or request ;;
- example: Most children are afraid of the dark. || 大多数孩子都怕黑。
- example: She was afraid to tell her parents that she had failed the exam. || 她不敢告诉父母自己考试不及格。
- example: I'm afraid we can't take your suggestion this time. || 很抱歉，我们这次不能采纳你的建议。



## word: brave
- uk: /breɪv/
- us: /breɪv/
- synonyms: courageous || 勇敢的，有勇气的 ;; fearless || 无畏的，不怕的 ;; bold || 大胆的，果敢的 ;; valiant || 英勇的，骁勇的 ;; intrepid || 无畏的，勇猛的 ;;
- antonyms: cowardly || 胆小的，懦弱的 ;; timid || 羞怯的，胆怯的 ;; fearful || 害怕的，胆怯的 ;;
- phrases: brave it out || 硬着头皮干，坚持到底 ;; brave the storm || 冒着风暴，直面困难 ;; brave new world || 美好的新世界，充满挑战的新领域 ;; brave death || 直面死亡 ;; brave the elements || 不顾恶劣天气 ;;
- collocations: brave man || 勇敢的人 ;; brave decision || 大胆的决定 ;; brave effort || 英勇的尝试 ;; brave smile || 强装的笑容 ;; brave fight || 英勇的战斗 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is brave of sb to do sth || 表示“某人做某事很勇敢”，用来评价他人的行为 ;; brave + n. || 表示“勇敢面对/冒（危险、困难等）”，后接表示困难、恶劣环境等的名词 ;; as brave as a lion || 表示“非常勇敢，勇猛如狮”，用于比喻程度 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Be brave! || 勇敢点！ ;; That was brave of you. || 你可真勇敢。 ;; You've got to brave it out. || 你得硬着头皮撑下去。 ;;
- idioms: as brave as a lion || 勇猛如狮，非常勇敢 ;; brave the odds || 不顾困难，直面不利情况 ;;

### sense: 形容词
- translationZh: 勇敢的，无畏的 ;; 大胆的，果敢的 ;; （面对不幸或困境）强装勇敢的，不动声色的 ;;
- definitionZh: 不害怕危险、困难的；有勇气面对不利情况的； ;; 敢于冒险、敢于尝试新事物或做有风险的事的； ;; 在痛苦、困难面前故意表现得冷静、不害怕的； ;;
- definitionEn: not afraid of danger or difficult situations; having the courage to face negative circumstances; ;; willing to take risks and try new or dangerous things; ;; appearing calm and unafraid even when you are in pain or a difficult situation; ;;
- example: She was brave enough to speak up against the unfair rule. || 她足够勇敢，敢于站出来反对不公平的规定。
- example: He put on a brave face even though he lost the competition. || 尽管输掉了比赛，他还是强装出镇定的样子。
- example: The brave firefighters rushed into the burning building to save the trapped residents. || 勇敢的消防员冲进着火的大楼，营救被困的居民。

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 勇敢面对，冒（风险） ;; 经受，承受（恶劣环境） ;;
- definitionZh: 故意面对危险、困难或恶劣的情况，毫不退缩； ;; 忍受、经受恶劣的天气、环境等不利条件； ;;
- definitionEn: to deliberately face a dangerous, difficult or unpleasant situation without trying to avoid it; ;; to endure or suffer through bad weather or other harsh conditions; ;;
- example: We decided to brave the rain and walk to the concert hall. || 我们决定冒着雨步行去音乐厅。
- example: He braved all the criticisms from the public and stuck to his original plan. || 他勇敢面对公众的所有批评，坚持自己最初的计划。
- example: Thousands of people braved the cold to attend the New Year's Eve celebration. || 数千人冒着严寒参加新年前夜的庆祝活动。

## word: fearless
- uk: /ˈfɪələs/
- us: /ˈfɪrləs/
- synonyms: brave || 勇敢的 ;; courageous || 无畏的 ;; bold || 大胆的 ;; intrepid || 勇猛的 ;; dauntless || 不屈不挠的 ;;
- antonyms: fearful || 害怕的 ;; cowardly || 胆小的 ;; timorous || 胆怯的 ;;
- phrases: fearless spirit || 无畏精神 ;; fearless warrior || 无畏的战士 ;; fearless attitude || 无畏的态度 ;; fearless exploration || 无畏探索 ;; fearless defiance || 无畏反抗 ;;
- collocations: remain fearless || 保持无畏 ;; be fearless of danger || 不惧危险 ;; fearless advocate || 无畏的倡导者 ;; fearless leadership || 无畏的领导力 ;; fearless in the face of adversity || 面对逆境时无畏 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + fearless + of + sth || 表示“不惧怕某事物” ;; it + be + admirable + that + sb + be + fearless + in doing sth || 表示“某人做某事时无所畏惧，这很令人钦佩” ;; sb + prove + (to be) + fearless + through + sth || 表示“某人通过某件事证明自己是无畏的” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Stay fearless! || 保持无畏！ ;; He's totally fearless, isn't he? || 他完全无所畏惧，对吧？ ;; I'm trying to be more fearless when I speak in public. || 我在公开讲话时正试着更无畏一点。 ;;
- idioms: fearless in the face of fire || 烈火面前无所畏惧（形容面对极端险境毫不退缩） ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 无畏的 ;; 勇敢的 ;; 不怕的 ;;
- definitionZh: 没有恐惧的，不害怕危险、困难或痛苦的 ;; 敢于面对风险、挑战而不退缩的 ;;
- definitionEn: not feeling afraid of danger, difficulty, or pain ;; willing to take risks and face challenges without hesitation ;;
- example: The fearless firefighter rushed into the burning building to save the trapped family. || 这位无畏的消防员冲进着火的建筑，营救被困的家庭。
- example: She was fearless in speaking up against unfair policies even when others disagreed with her. || 即使其他人都不赞同，她也无畏地公开反对不公平的政策。
- example: As an explorer, he remained fearless when trekking through the uncharted jungle alone. || 作为一名探险家，他独自徒步穿越未知丛林时始终无所畏惧。

- definitionEn: frightened of something or afraid that something bad might happen ;; feeling fear or nervousness about a particular situation or thing ;;

## word: terrified
- uk: /ˈterɪfaɪd/
- us: /ˈterɪfaɪd/
- synonyms: frightened || 受惊的，害怕的 ;; scared || 害怕的，恐惧的 ;; horrified || 惊骇的，震惊的 ;; petrified || 吓呆的，石化的 ;; spooked || 受惊的，吓坏的 ;;
- antonyms: fearless || 无畏的，勇敢的 ;; bold || 大胆的，果敢的 ;; unafraid || 不害怕的，无惧的 ;;
- phrases: be terrified of || 非常害怕…，对…感到恐惧 ;; be terrified at || 因…而吓了一跳 ;; terrified expression || 惊恐的表情 ;; absolutely terrified || 极度恐惧的，吓坏了的 ;;
- collocations: terrified child || 受惊的孩子 ;; terrified scream || 惊恐的尖叫 ;; feel terrified || 感到恐惧 ;; look terrified || 看起来很害怕 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be terrified of doing sth || 表示害怕做某事的常用句型 ;; be terrified that + 从句 || 表示担心会发生某事的句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: I'm terrified out of my wits! || 我吓得魂都没了！ ;; You look terrified, what happened? || 你看起来吓坏了，怎么了？ ;; I'm terrified of heights, honestly. || 说实话，我特别怕高。 ;;
- idioms: be terrified out of one's mind || 吓得魂不附体，惊恐万分 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 非常害怕的 ;; 极度惊恐的 ;;
- definitionZh: 感到极端恐惧、惊慌的状态 ;; 因为特定的人、事物或场景而产生强烈惧怕情绪的 ;;
- definitionEn: feeling extremely frightened or afraid ;; affected by intense fear caused by a particular person, thing, or situation ;;
- example: She was terrified of being left alone in the dark house. || 她非常害怕被独自留在那栋黑漆漆的房子里。
- example: When the earthquake hit, people were terrified and ran out of the building in a panic. || 地震发生时，人们极度惊恐，慌乱地跑出了大楼。
- example: The little boy was terrified that his parents would leave him at the boarding school forever. || 小男孩非常害怕父母会把他永远留在寄宿学校。

## word: after
- uk: /ˈɑːftə(r)/
- us: /ˈæftər/
- synonyms: following || 紧接着的，在…之后 ;; subsequent to || 继…之后 ;; post || 在…之后 ;; behind || 在…后面 ;;
- antonyms: before || 在…之前 ;; prior to || 先于，在…之前 ;;
- phrases: after all || 毕竟，终究 ;; after hours || 下班后，营业时间后 ;; after a while || 过了一会儿 ;; look after || 照顾，照料 ;; take after || （外貌、性格）与…相像 ;;
- collocations: after work || 下班后 ;; after school || 放学后 ;; after dinner || 晚饭后 ;; after the event || 事后 ;; after years of effort || 经过多年努力 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + 时间段 + after + 从句 || 表示“某事发生后已经过了多久” ;; After doing sth, 主句 || 表示“做完某事后，发生另一动作” ;;
- spokenExpressions: After you! || 您先请！ ;; After what happened last time, ... || 上次那事儿之后，… ;; See you after! || 回头见！ ;;
- idioms: after one's own heart || 正合心意，对胃口 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在……之后 ;; 跟随，在……后面 ;; 鉴于，由于 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示时间、位置或顺序位于某事物的后面 ;; 表示作为对某事物的回应或因为某事物 ;;
- definitionEn: following in time, place, or order behind sb/sth ;; as a result of sth ;;
- example: I went for a walk after breakfast. || 我早饭后去散步了。
- example: He entered the room right after his boss. || 他紧跟着老板进了房间。
- example: After what you said, I don't think I can trust you anymore. || 听了你说的话之后，我觉得我没法再信任你了。

### sense: conjunction
- translationZh: 在……之后 ;;
- definitionZh: 引导时间状语从句，表示主句动作发生在从句动作之后 ;;
- definitionEn: used to introduce a clause that shows the time when the main action happens ;;
- example: I will call you after I arrive at the airport. || 我到机场之后会给你打电话。
- example: After she finished her homework, she watched a cartoon. || 她做完作业之后看了一部动画片。
- example: We went to the cinema after we had dinner together. || 我们一起吃完晚饭后去了电影院。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 后来，之后 ;; 后面，跟随 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示时间上随后发生；表示位置在后方 ;;
- definitionEn: later in time ;; following behind sb/sth ;;
- example: We arrived soon after. || 我们不久之后就到了。
- example: Tom went first, and the rest of us followed after. || 汤姆走在前面，我们其他人跟在后面。
- example: She graduated in 2020, and got a master's degree three years after. || 她2020年毕业，三年后拿到了硕士学位。



## word: before
- uk: /bɪˈfɔː(r)/
- us: /bɪˈfɔːr/
- synonyms: prior to || 在…之前 ;; preceding || 在…前面的；先于 ;; earlier than || 早于 ;; previous to || 先于 ;; ahead of || 在…之前 ;;
- antonyms: after || 在…之后 ;; following || 在…之后 ;; behind || 在…后面 ;;
- phrases: before long || 不久，很快 ;; the day before yesterday || 前天 ;; before now || 此前，以前 ;; before the fact || 事发前 ;; long before || 很久以前 ;;
- collocations: appear before || 出现在…面前（尤指法庭） ;; go before || 先于…发生；走在前面 ;; come before || 被提交给…处理；排在…之前 ;; look before you leap || 三思而后行 ;; stand before || 站在…面前 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It + be + 时间段 + before + 从句 || 表示“过了多久才…” ;; sb + had done sth + before + sb else + did sth || 表示“在某人做某事之前，另一人已经完成了某动作” ;; before + doing sth, 主句 || 表示“在做某事之前，先做…” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Before I forget... || 趁我还没忘… ;; Before we start... || 在我们开始之前… ;; I've told you that a hundred times before! || 这话我之前都跟你说过一百遍了！ ;;
- idioms: before one's time || 在某人出生前；在某人任职前；过早的 ;; put the cart before the horse || 本末倒置 ;;

### sense: 介词
- translationZh: 在…之前；先于；在…面前；
- definitionZh: 指时间、顺序、位置上早于或位于某人/某物前面；也可指出现在重要人物或权威机构面前 ;;
- definitionEn: earlier in time, sequence, or position than someone or something; in front of someone, especially an important person or official body ;;
- example: Please arrive 10 minutes before the meeting starts. || 请在会议开始前10分钟到达。
- example: He had to appear before the judge to explain his actions. || 他必须出庭向法官解释自己的行为。
- example: Safety comes before profit in this company. || 在这家公司，安全比利润更重要。

### sense: 连词
- translationZh: 在…以前；到…为止；以免；不然；
- definitionZh: 引导时间状语从句，表示某事发生在另一件事之前；也可表示“还没来得及…就”“以免”等含义 ;;
- definitionEn: used to connect two clauses, showing that the first event happens earlier than the second; also used to mean "otherwise" or "lest" ;;
- example: Turn off the lights before you leave the room. || 你离开房间前把灯关掉。
- example: I had barely sat down before the phone rang. || 我刚坐下电话就响了。
- example: Lock the door before someone walks in. || 锁好门，免得有人进来。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 以前；过去；已经；
- definitionZh: 表示在过去的某个时间，或在提到的某个时间之前 ;;
- definitionEn: at an earlier time; in the past; already ;;
- example: I've been to Paris once before. || 我以前去过一次巴黎。
- example: That was years before, when I was still a student. || 那是多年以前的事了，当时我还是个学生。
- example: You should have told me that before! || 你之前就该告诉我那件事！

## word: following
- uk: /ˈfɒləʊɪŋ/
- us: /ˈfɑːloʊɪŋ/
- synonyms: subsequent || 随后的 ;; succeeding || 接在后面的 ;; next || 接下来的 ;; devotee || 支持者 ;; supporter || 拥护者 ;;
- antonyms: preceding || 在前的 ;; previous || 先前的 ;; prior || 之前的 ;;
- phrases: the following day || 第二天 ;; following on from || 继…之后 ;; in the following || 在下文 ;; following up || 跟进，追踪 ;;
- collocations: following year || 下一年 ;; following example || 下面的例子 ;; large following || 大量追随者 ;; following instructions || 遵守指示 ;; following trend || 追随潮流 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Following + 名词短语, 主句 || 用来引出作为前提或背景的事件，主句说明后续情况 ;; The following + be动词 + 名词短语 || 用来引出下文要列举的内容，比如条目、例子等 ;; It is following that + 从句 || 用来强调某件事是基于前文的情况才发生的 ;;
- spokenExpressions: The following, please. || 请读/看下文。 ;; Following that, what happened? || 那之后发生了什么？ ;; Just following the rules. || 我只是按规矩办事而已。 ;;
- idioms: follow one's nose || 凭直觉行事，笔直走 ;; follow suit || 照着做，效仿 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 接下来的；下述的 ;; 接着的，随后的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在时间、顺序或位置上紧接在前面的事物之后的 ;; 用于指代接下来要提到、列举的内容 ;;
- definitionEn: Coming or happening immediately after something else in time, order, or position ;; Used to refer to the thing or person that is going to be mentioned next ;;
- example: The following chapter will discuss the impact of climate change on agriculture. || 接下来的章节将会讨论气候变化对农业的影响。
- example: Please read the following instructions carefully before you start the exam. || 开始考试前请仔细阅读下述说明。
- example: He suffered from a fever for three following days after he got caught in the rain. || 他淋雨后接下来的三天都在发烧。

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 追随者，拥护者 ;; 下述，下列内容 ;;
- definitionZh: 指支持某个公众人物、团体或理念的一群人 ;; 指接下来要列出或提到的内容 ;;
- definitionEn: A group of people who support and admire a particular person, organization, or idea ;; The things or people that are going to be mentioned next ;;
- example: The young singer has gained a huge following on social media over the past year. || 这位年轻歌手过去一年在社交媒体上收获了大量追随者。
- example: The following are the winners of this year's literary award. || 下列是本年度文学奖的获奖者。
- example: The startup has a loyal following of customers who love its eco-friendly products. || 这家初创公司拥有一群喜爱其环保产品的忠实客户群体。

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在…之后，紧随 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示在某个事件、行动发生之后紧接着出现另一件事 ;;
- definitionEn: Happening or done after a particular event or action ;;
- example: Following the heavy storm, many roads in the area were blocked by fallen trees. || 暴雨过后，该地区的许多道路都被倒下的树木堵住了。
- example: The restaurant will be closed for three days following the owner's retirement. || 店主退休后，这家餐厅将停业三天。
- example: Following the teacher's advice, she decided to apply for the postgraduate program. || 听从老师的建议后，她决定申请研究生项目。

## word: post
- uk: /pəʊst/
- us: /poʊst/
- synonyms: mail || 邮件，邮寄 ;; pole || 杆，柱 ;; publish || 发布，发表 ;; position || 职位，岗位 ;; send || 寄送，发送 ;;
- antonyms: delete || 删除 ;; recall || 撤回 ;;
- phrases: post office || 邮局 ;; post card || 明信片 ;; post code || 邮政编码 ;; post war || 战后 ;; post graduate || 研究生 ;;
- collocations: post a letter || 寄信 ;; post a notice || 张贴通知 ;; apply for a post || 申请职位 ;; hold a post || 担任职务 ;; post online || 在线发布 ;;
- sentencePatterns: post sth to sb || 表示“把某物邮寄给某人” ;; post sth on sth || 表示“把某物发布/张贴在某处” ;; be appointed to the post of || 表示“被任命担任某个职位” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Keep me posted! || 随时跟我通报情况！ ;; Did you get my post? || 你收到我发的帖子/邮件了吗？ ;; I'll post it first thing tomorrow. || 我明天一早就把这个寄出去。 ;;
- slang: post up || 待在某个地方停留 ;;
- idioms: post haste || 火速，尽快 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 邮政，邮寄 ;; 邮件，包裹 ;; 帖子，发布的内容 ;; 职位，岗位 ;; 柱，杆，桩 ;;
- definitionZh: 国家传递信件、包裹等的公共服务系统，或指邮寄的行为 ;; 经邮政系统传递的信件、包裹等物品 ;; 在互联网平台上公开发布的文字、图片、视频等内容 ;; 机构或公司中设置的正式工作岗位 ;; 直立的、用来支撑或标记位置的长条状硬物 ;;
- definitionEn: The public service system for delivering letters, parcels, etc., or the act of sending items via this system ;; Letters, parcels and other items sent through the postal system ;; Content such as text, pictures or videos publicly released on internet platforms ;; A formal job position in an organization or company ;; A long straight piece of wood, metal etc. that is fixed upright in the ground to support something or mark a place ;;
- example: I sent the document by post yesterday. || 我昨天把文件邮寄出去了。
- example: There's an interesting post about environmental protection on his social media homepage. || 他的社交媒体主页上有一篇关于环保的有趣帖子。
- example: She has applied for the post of marketing manager. || 她已经申请了市场经理的职位。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 邮寄，寄送 ;; 张贴，公布 ;; 发布（内容到互联网） ;; 派驻，使驻守 ;;
- definitionZh: 通过邮政系统把物品寄给特定对象 ;; 把通知、公告等贴在公众可见的位置 ;; 将文字、图片等内容上传到互联网平台公开发布 ;; 安排人员到特定地点执行工作任务 ;;
- definitionEn: To send something to a person or place via the postal system ;; To put a notice, announcement etc. in a public place where people can see it ;; To upload text, pictures or other content to an internet platform for public viewing ;; To send someone to a particular place to work for a period of time as part of their job ;;
- example: Remember to post this invitation card to Mr. Smith before Friday. || 记得周五之前把这张邀请函寄给史密斯先生。
- example: The school posted the exam results on the notice board this morning. || 学校今天早上把考试成绩张贴在了公告栏上。
- example: He often posts short videos about cooking on his personal account. || 他经常在自己的个人账号上发布关于烹饪的短视频。

## word: prior to
- uk: /ˈpraɪə(r) tuː/
- us: /ˈpraɪər tuː/
- synonyms: before || 在…之前 ;; ahead of || 早于，先于 ;; preceding || 在…之前的 ;; previous to || 先于，在…之前 ;; ante- || （前缀）在…之前 ;;
- antonyms: after || 在…之后 ;; following || 紧随…之后 ;; subsequent to || 继…之后 ;;
- phrases: prior to departure || 出发前 ;; prior to admission || 入院前，入学前 ;; prior to implementation || 实施前 ;; prior to the meeting || 会议开始前 ;; prior to delivery || 交货前，分娩前 ;;
- collocations: required prior to || 在…前需要 ;; completed prior to || 在…前完成 ;; submitted prior to || 在…前提交 ;; notified prior to || 在…前得到通知 ;; agreed prior to || 在…前商定 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is necessary to do sth prior to + n./doing || 表示“在做某件事之前有必要做另一事” ;; Prior to + n./doing, sb do sth || 表示“在某事件/动作发生之前，主语执行某动作” ;; No changes shall be made prior to + n./doing || 表示“在某事件发生之前不得做出变更”，多用于正式规定类语境 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Just let me know prior to coming, okay? || 来之前告诉我一声，好吗？ ;; You need to sign the form prior to getting the key. || 拿钥匙之前你得先签这个表。 ;; We have to finish the check prior to the guests arriving. || 客人到之前我们得完成检查。 ;;
- idioms: prior to someone's time || 在某人出生前，在某人来之前（指任职、居住等场景） ;;

### sense: prepositional phrase
- translationZh: 在……之前；先于……；早于…… ;;
- definitionZh: 表示时间、顺序上早于某一事件或动作，多用于正式语境； ;; 用于说明某动作或状态发生在另一指定事件的时间之前； ;;
- definitionEn: used to say that something happens or exists before a particular time or event, especially in formal contexts; ;; indicating that one action, event, or situation occurs earlier than another reference point; ;;
- example: All passengers are required to arrive at the airport two hours prior to the departure time. || 所有乘客需在航班起飞时间前两小时抵达机场。
- example: Prior to working in this company, she spent three years as a researcher in a university. || 在进入这家公司工作之前，她在一所大学做了三年研究员。
- example: The team conducted several rounds of tests prior to launching the new software to the public. || 在向公众推出新软件之前，团队进行了好几轮测试。

## word: subsequent to
- uk: /ˈsʌbsɪkwənt tuː/
- us: /ˈsʌbsɪkwənt tuː/
- synonyms: after || 在……之后 ;; following || 在……之后 ;; post || 在……之后 ;; succeeding || 继……之后 ;; prior to 的反义对应 不对，重新来：synonyms: after || 在……之后 ;; following || 紧随……之后 ;; post- || 在……之后 ;; succeeding || 继……之后 ;;
- antonyms: prior to || 在……之前 ;; before || 在……之前 ;; preceding || 在……之前 ;;
- phrases: subsequent to the event || 事件发生之后 ;; subsequent to the pandemic || 疫情之后 ;; subsequent to the meeting || 会议结束之后 ;; subsequent to the approval || 获得批准之后 ;;
- collocations: occur subsequent to || 发生在……之后 ;; be subsequent to || 晚于……；在……之后 ;; changes subsequent to || ……之后的变化 ;; developments subsequent to || ……之后的进展 ;;
- sentencePatterns: [Event A] takes place subsequent to [Event B] || 表示A事件发生在B事件之后 ;; Subsequent to [noun/doing sth], [main clause] || 用于句首，引出时间背景，后接主句 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Subsequent to what we discussed earlier, I've got a few updates. || 继我们之前讨论的内容之后，我有一些新进展要说明。 ;; We'll send you the details subsequent to your confirmation. || 你确认之后我们会把详情发给你。 ;;

### sense: prepositional phrase
- translationZh: 在……之后 ;; 继……之后 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示时间上晚于某一事件、动作或时间点，用于说明两件事的先后顺序 ;; 用于正式语境中，引出后续事件发生的时间参照 ;;
- definitionEn: happening or coming after something else, used to show the order of events in formal contexts ;; used to indicate that an event occurs at a time later than the reference event mentioned ;;
- example: Subsequent to the announcement, the company's share price rose by 10%. || 公告发布之后，该公司的股价上涨了10%。
- example: All the changes made subsequent to the initial draft must be marked in red. || 初稿之后做出的所有修改都必须用红色标注。
- example: He was arrested in the week subsequent to the robbery. || 抢劫案发生后的一周内他就被捕了。

## word: afternoon
- uk: /ˌɑːftəˈnuːn/
- us: /ˌæftərˈnuːn/
- synonyms: arvo || （澳非正式）下午 ;; p.m. || 下午，午后 ;; post meridiem || 下午，午后 ;; midday period || 午间时段 ;;
- antonyms: morning || 早晨，上午 ;; forenoon || 午前，上午 ;;
- phrases: in the afternoon || 在下午 ;; this afternoon || 今天下午 ;; tomorrow afternoon || 明天下午 ;; afternoon tea || 下午茶 ;; late afternoon || 傍晚，下午晚些时候 ;;
- collocations: sunny afternoon || 晴朗的下午 ;; lazy afternoon || 慵懒的下午 ;; afternoon nap || 午觉，下午小睡 ;; afternoon meeting || 下午的会议 ;; afternoon shift || 下午班，中班 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + 描述词 + afternoon. || 用于描述下午的天气或氛围 ;; We will + 具体活动 + on + 具体日期 + afternoon. || 用于说明某个特定下午的安排 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Good afternoon! || 下午好！ ;; Catch you this afternoon! || 今天下午见！ ;; Have a nice afternoon! || 祝你下午过得愉快！ ;;
- idioms: afternoon of life || 晚年，暮年 ;;

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 下午 ;; 午后 ;;
- definitionZh: 指从正午十二点到日落之前的这段时间 ;; 日常时段划分中位于上午之后、晚上之前的时间段 ;;
- definitionEn: the part of the day between noon and sunset ;; the time period after midday and before evening ;;
- example: I usually go for a walk in the afternoon after finishing my work. || 我通常在下午完成工作后去散步。
- example: We are going to attend a lecture on environmental protection this afternoon. || 我们今天下午要去参加一场关于环境保护的讲座。
- example: She brought homemade cookies when she came over for afternoon tea last weekend. || 上周末她过来喝下午茶的时候带了自制的曲奇饼干。



## word: arvo
- uk: /ˈɑːvəʊ/
- us: /ˈɑːrvoʊ/
- synonyms: afternoon || 下午 ;; p.m. || 午后 ;; post meridiem || 下午 ;;
- antonyms: morning || 上午 ;; forenoon || 午前 ;;
- phrases: this arvo || 今天下午 ;; tomorrow arvo || 明天下午 ;; saturday arvo || 周六下午 ;;
- collocations: sunny arvo || 晴朗的下午 ;; lazy arvo || 悠闲的下午 ;; work arvo || 工作日下午 ;;
- sentencePatterns: What are you doing this arvo? || 用于询问对方下午的安排 ;; We can meet up [time] arvo. || 用于约定下午的见面时间 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Catch you this arvo! || 下午见！ ;; Have a good arvo! || 下午过得愉快！ ;;
- slang: arvo || 下午（澳大利亚、新西兰口语对afternoon的缩略说法） ;;
- idioms:

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 下午 ;; 午后 ;;
- definitionZh: 澳大利亚和新西兰口语中对afternoon的非正式缩略表达，指中午12点到傍晚的时间段 ;; 非正式场合指代下午的时段，常用于日常轻松对话中 ;;
- definitionEn: An informal colloquial abbreviation of "afternoon" used in Australian and New Zealand English, referring to the period between noon and evening ;; A casual term for the time period after midday, used in relaxed daily conversations ;;
- example: I'm heading to the beach this arvo if the weather stays nice. || 如果天气一直好的话，我今天下午要去海滩。
- example: Let's grab a coffee together tomorrow arvo, yeah? || 我们明天下午一起去喝杯咖啡，好吗？
- example: We spent a lazy arvo watching old movies at my place last weekend. || 上周末我们在我家看老电影，度过了一个悠闲的下午。

## word: forenoon
- uk: /ˈfɔːnuːn/
- us: /ˈfɔːrnuːn/
- synonyms: morning || 早晨，上午 ;; ante meridiem || 午前 ;; a.m. || 上午 ;;
- antonyms: afternoon || 下午 ;; post meridiem || 午后 ;;
- phrases: forenoon session || 上午场次 ;; forenoon break || 午前休息 ;; forenoon shift || 早班 ;;

- sentencePatterns: sb spend + 时间段 + forenoon doing sth || 表示某人花费整个上午做某事 ;; The forenoon is + adj + for doing sth || 表示上午很适合做某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: See you in the forenoon! || 咱们上午见！ ;; I've got a packed forenoon tomorrow. || 我明天上午日程排满了。 ;;
### sense: noun

- definitionZh: 指从日出到中午之间的时间段，即正午之前的时段 ;; 日常语境中也可指上午工作、活动的时段 ;;
- definitionEn: the part of the day between sunrise and noon; the period of time before midday ;; the time period in the morning when people usually work or do activities ;;
- example: The negotiation is scheduled to kick off at nine o'clock in the forenoon. || 谈判定于上午九点开始。
- example: She spent the entire forenoon sorting out the historical documents in the archive. || 她整个上午都在档案室整理历史文件。
- example: Most shops in this small town only open after the forenoon on weekends. || 这个小镇的多数商店周末只有过了上午才开门。

## word: morning

- us: /ˈmɔːrnɪŋ/

- spokenExpressions: Good morning! || 早上好！ ;; Morning! || 早（非正式问候） ;; Have a nice morning! || 祝你上午过得愉快！ ;;

- definitionZh: 从日出到正午的这段时间 ;; 一天中日出之后的较早时段 ;;
- definitionEn: the part of the day between sunrise and noon ;; the early part of the day after waking up ;;
- example: I go jogging for half an hour every morning before work. || 我每天早上上班前都会慢跑半小时。
- example: The meeting is scheduled for 9 o'clock on Thursday morning. || 会议安排在周四上午九点。
- example: The fresh morning air makes me feel energetic all day. || 清晨的新鲜空气让我一整天都精力充沛。

### sense: exclamation
- translationZh: 早上好（非正式问候语） ;;
- definitionZh: 用于早上见面时的非正式问候，是good morning的简略说法 ;;
- definitionEn: an informal way of greeting someone when you meet them in the morning, short for "good morning" ;;
- example: Morning! Did you sleep well last night? || 早！你昨晚睡得好吗？
- example: Morning, everyone! Let's start today's lecture directly. || 大家早上好！我们直接开始今天的讲座吧。

## word: p.m.
- uk: /ˌpiː ˈem/
- us: /ˌpiː ˈem/
- synonyms: post meridiem || 下午，午后 ;; afternoon || 下午 ;; evening || 傍晚 ;;
- antonyms: a.m. || 上午，午前 ;; ante meridiem || 午前 ;;
- phrases: 3 p.m. || 下午三点 ;; 8 p.m. || 晚上八点 ;; p.m. shift || 下午班 ;; 11:59 p.m. || 夜里11点59分 ;;
- collocations: arrive at 5 p.m. || 下午五点到达 ;; close at 7 p.m. || 晚上七点关门 ;; start at 2 p.m. || 下午两点开始 ;; work until 10 p.m. || 工作到晚上十点 ;;
- sentencePatterns: 具体时间 + p.m. + 谓语 + 其他 || 用于说明下午/晚间某个时间发生的动作 ;; The event is scheduled for + 时间点 + p.m. || 用于说明活动的下午/晚间安排时间 ;;
- spokenExpressions: See you at 6 p.m. || 下午六点见 ;; It's already 11 p.m. || 现在都已经晚上十一点了 ;; The shop shuts at 9 p.m. today || 这家店今天晚上九点打烊 ;;

### sense: 缩写词
- translationZh: 下午 ;; 午后 ;;
- definitionZh: 指中午12点到午夜12点之间的时间段，是拉丁语post meridiem的缩写 ;; 用于标注12小时制中中午过后的时间 ;;
- definitionEn: abbreviation for post meridiem, used to refer to the time between 12 o'clock noon and 12 o'clock midnight ;; used when stating times in the 12-hour clock system to show that the time is in the afternoon or evening ;;
- example: The meeting will begin at 3 p.m. tomorrow. || 会议将于明天下午三点开始。
- example: The last train leaves at 11:45 p.m. on weekdays. || 工作日的末班车在晚上11点45分开出。
- example: I usually finish work at 6 p.m. and go home to cook. || 我通常下午六点下班，然后回家做饭。

## word: post meridiem
- uk: /ˌpəʊst məˈrɪdiəm/
- us: /ˌpoʊst məˈrɪdiəm/
- synonyms: P.M. || 下午 ;; afternoon || 午后 ;; p.m. || 下午时段 ;;
- antonyms: ante meridiem || 午前 ;; A.M. || 上午 ;;
- phrases: 2 o'clock post meridiem || 下午两点 ;; post meridiem hours || 下午时段 ;; post meridiem schedule || 下午日程 ;; 10 pm post meridiem || 晚上10点 ;;
- collocations: arrive post meridiem || 下午抵达 ;; post meridiem meeting || 下午会议 ;; post meridiem flight || 下午航班 ;; post meridiem appointment || 下午预约 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The event starts at [具体时间] post meridiem. || 用于说明活动在下午某时间开始 ;; Please arrive before [具体时间] post meridiem. || 用于告知对方需要在下午某时间前抵达 ;; The store closes at [具体时间] post meridiem on weekdays. || 用于说明工作日店铺下午的关门时间 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That's 3 post meridiem, right? || 那是下午3点，对吧？ ;; Let's schedule it for 2 post meridiem. || 我们把它安排在下午2点吧。 ;; I'm free after 1 post meridiem. || 我下午1点之后有空。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 下午 ;; 午后 ;;
- definitionZh: 指从正午十二点到半夜十二点的时间段，常用于标注十二小时制的下午时间 ;; 源自拉丁语，意为“正午之后”，常缩写为P.M.或p.m. ;;
- definitionEn: The period of time between noon and midnight, used to indicate times in the 12-hour clock system that fall in the afternoon or evening ;; A Latin phrase meaning "after midday", often abbreviated as P.M. or p.m. ;;
- example: The concert will begin at 7 o'clock post meridiem. || 音乐会将于晚上7点开始。
- example: You should submit your report by 5 post meridiem this Friday. || 你需要在本周五下午5点前提交报告。
- example: The post meridiem shift starts at 1 p.m. and ends at 9 p.m. || 下午班从下午1点开始，到晚上9点结束。

- sentencePatterns: Do sth again || 表示“再做一次某事”的祈使/陈述结构 ;; ... again, ... || 置于句首，引出重复出现的情况或再次提及的内容 ;; Not...again! || 表示厌烦、抗拒再次发生某事的感叹结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Come again? || 你说什么？请再说一遍？ ;; There you go again. || 你又来这一套了。 ;; Never again! || 再也不会了！ ;;
- idioms: back again || 回到原地，恢复原状 ;; now and again || 偶尔，不时 ;;

- definitionEn: one more time; used to introduce an extra point or fact; back to a previous state or condition ;;
- example: Could you say that again please? I didn't catch it. || 你能再说一遍吗？我没听清。
- example: He was ill last week, but he's well again now. || 他上周生病了，不过现在已经痊愈了。
- example: Again, we need to consider the cost of this project before making a decision. || 再者，我们在做决定前需要考虑这个项目的成本。



## word: afresh
- uk: /əˈfreʃ/

- collocations: start afresh || 重新开始 ;; approach sth afresh || 用新方式处理某事 ;; look at sth afresh || 重新审视某事 ;; begin afresh after failure || 失败后从头再来 ;;
- sentencePatterns: decide to do sth afresh || 决定重新做某事的句型 ;; help sb start afresh || 帮助某人重新开始的句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Let's start afresh, shall we? || 我们重新开始，好吗？ ;; I think we need to look at this problem afresh. || 我觉得我们得重新审视这个问题。 ;; After the argument, we agreed to begin afresh. || 争吵过后，我们同意重归于好。 ;;
- idioms: start afresh with a clean slate || 改头换面重新开始 ;;

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 重新；再度；从头
- definitionZh: 指以新的方式重新开始做某事，没有之前的影响或遗留问题；指从最初的阶段重新进行某件事
- definitionEn: if you do something afresh, you do it again in a different way, without using what was done before; starting from the beginning of a process, with no previous results or arrangements influencing you
- example: When you move to a new city, you get the chance to start afresh and make new friends. || 当你搬到一座新城市时，你就有机会重新开始，结交新朋友。
- example: The teacher suggested we approach the project afresh, using a completely different research method. || 老师建议我们从头处理这个项目，采用一种完全不同的研究方法。
- example: After the company was acquired by a larger firm, all the old policies were discarded and the management team built the business afresh. || 这家公司被大公司收购后，所有旧政策都被废除，管理团队从头开始打造业务。

- example: I have never been to Japan. || 我从来没去过日本。
- example: You should never lie to your family. || 你绝对不应该对家人撒谎。
- example: Never has she seen such a beautiful sunset before. || 她以前从未见过这么美的日落。

## word: once

- sentencePatterns: Once + 从句, 主句 || 引导时间状语从句，意为“一旦…就…” ;; It once was + 名词/形容词 || 描述过去曾经存在的状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Once more, please. || 请再来一次。 ;; Once I start, I can't stop. || 我一旦开始就停不下来。 ;; Once is enough, thanks. || 一次就够了，谢谢。 ;;
- idioms: once in a blue moon || 千载难逢 ;; once bitten, twice shy || 一朝被蛇咬，十年怕井绳 ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 一次 ;; 曾经 ;; 一度 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示动作发生的次数为一次 ;; 表示过去某个时间存在某种情况，现在已经不存在 ;;
- definitionEn: on one occasion only ;; at some time in the past ;;
- example: I've been to Paris once. || 我去过巴黎一次。
- example: She once worked as a nurse. || 她曾经做过护士。
- example: The town was once a famous fishing port. || 这个小镇一度是著名的渔港。

### sense: 连词
- translationZh: 一旦 ;; 一…就 ;;
- definitionZh: 引导条件状语从句，表示某个动作或情况一旦发生，就会引发另一个结果 ;;
- definitionEn: as soon as, from the moment when ;;
- example: Once you finish your homework, you can watch TV. || 你一旦完成作业就可以看电视。
- example: Once the sun sets, the temperature drops quickly. || 太阳一落山，气温就会迅速下降。
- example: Once he makes a promise, he will never break it. || 他一旦许下承诺就绝不会食言。

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 一次 ;; 一回 ;;
- definitionZh: 指单次的事件或情况 ;;
- definitionEn: a single occasion or instance ;;
- example: One mistake is okay, but once is enough. || 一次失误没关系，但一次就够了。
- example: The once of meeting him left a deep impression on me. || 和他的那次会面给我留下了深刻的印象。

## word: once more

- definitionEn: one more time; again; used to indicate that an action or event happens or is done another time ;;
- example: Could you explain that rule once more? I still don't quite understand it. || 你能再解释一遍那条规则吗？我还是不太明白。

## word: against
- uk: /əˈɡenst/
- us: /əˈɡenst/
- synonyms: opposite to || 与…相反 ;; opposing || 反对 ;; contra || 与…相反 ;; counter to || 与…对立 ;;
- antonyms: for || 支持 ;; pro || 赞成 ;; in favour of || 赞同 ;;
- phrases: against the law || 违法 ;; against the clock || 争分夺秒 ;; against one's will || 违背意愿 ;; go against || 违反，不利于 ;;
- collocations: fight against || 与…斗争 ;; protest against || 抗议 ;; discriminate against || 歧视 ;; guard against || 防范 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is against + 名词 + to do sth || 表示做某事违反某规定/原则 ;; verb + against + 宾语 || 表示动作指向反对/对抗的对象 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That's against the rules! || 那是违反规则的！ ;; I'm dead against the idea. || 我强烈反对这个主意。 ;; We're racing against time here. || 我们现在在争分夺秒。 ;;
- idioms: against all odds || 尽管困难重重 ;; go against the grain || 违背本意，不合常理 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 反对 ;; 违反 ;; 紧靠 ;; 以…为背景 ;; 对…不利 ;;
- definitionZh: 不同意或不支持某事物、某人 ;; 与某项规则、法律等相冲突 ;; 紧挨着某个表面、物体 ;; 以某个事物作为背景衬托 ;; 对某人、某件事产生不利的影响 ;;
- definitionEn: Disagreeing with or not supporting something or someone ;; Conflicting with a rule, law, etc. ;; Pressing closely on or next to a surface or object ;; With something as a background or contrast ;; Having an unfavorable effect on someone or something ;;
- example: Many residents are against the plan to build a new factory near the residential area. || 许多居民反对在住宅区附近建造新工厂的计划。
- example: He leaned against the wall, waiting for his friend to show up. || 他靠在墙上，等着他的朋友出现。
- example: The red flags stand out brightly against the blue sky. || 红旗在蓝天的映衬下显得格外鲜艳。
- example: All the evidence is against him, so he is likely to lose the lawsuit. || 所有证据都对他不利，所以他很可能会输掉这场官司。



## word: contra
- uk: /ˈkɒntrə/
- us: /ˈkɑːntrə/
- synonyms: opposite || 相反的事物 ;; counter || 反对物 ;; reverse || 对立面 ;; objection || 反对意见 ;; dissent || 异议 ;;
- antonyms: pro || 赞成者 ;; supporter || 支持者 ;; advocate || 拥护者 ;;
- phrases: pro and contra || 正反双方 ;; contra entry || 对销分录 ;; contra account || 备抵账户 ;; contra flow || 反向车流 ;;
- collocations: contra argument || 相反论点 ;; contra position || 对立立场 ;; contra measure || 应对措施 ;; contra party || 对立一方 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be contra to sth || 表示与某事物相反/违背 ;; argue contra sth || 表示为反对某事物而辩论 ;;
- spokenExpressions: On the contra, I think it's a bad idea. || 恰恰相反，我觉得这是个坏主意。 ;; Are you pro or contra the proposal? || 你是支持还是反对这项提议？ ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 相反事物 ;; 反对意见 ;; 避孕用具（尤指避孕药） ;;
- definitionZh: 与某事物相对或相反的事物、观点；用于反对某一主张的论据或意见；口服避孕药等避孕器具的非正式说法 ;;
- definitionEn: a thing that is opposite or contrary to something else; an argument or opinion opposing a claim or idea; an informal term for contraceptive, especially the birth control pill ;;
- example: The pros of the new policy far outweigh the contras. || 这项新政策的利远大于弊。
- example: She went to the clinic to get a prescription for the contra. || 她去诊所开避孕药的处方。
- example: Before making the final decision, we need to carefully consider all the contras raised by the opponents. || 在做最终决定之前，我们需要仔细考虑反对者提出的所有反对意见。

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 反对 ;; 与…相反 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示反对某一立场、提议或规则，或者与某事物的方向、性质相反 ;;
- definitionEn: used to show opposition to a position, proposal or rule, or that something is contrary to the direction or nature of another thing ;;
- example: The decision was made contra the advice of most experts. || 这个决定是违背大多数专家的建议做出的。
- example: He voted contra the proposed bill in the parliament. || 他在议会中对拟议的法案投了反对票。
- example: These actions are contra the basic principles of human rights. || 这些行为违背了人权的基本原则。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 相反的 ;; 反对的 ;;
- definitionZh: 描述性质、立场与另一事物相对或持反对态度的 ;;
- definitionEn: describing something that is opposite in nature or position, or holding an opposing attitude ;;
- example: The contra view holds that the measure will do more harm than good. || 相反的观点认为这项措施弊大于利。
- example: We need to listen to the contra opinions to make a balanced judgment. || 我们需要听取反对意见来做出平衡的判断。
- example: The two parties took contra stances on the environmental protection issue. || 双方在环保问题上持相反立场。

## word: for
- uk: /fɔː(r)/
- us: /fɔːr/
- synonyms: to || 向，为了 ;; toward || 朝向，对于 ;; intended for || 旨在，用于 ;; in favor of || 支持，赞同 ;;
- antonyms: against || 反对，违反 ;; opposed to || 反对 ;;
- phrases: for example || 例如 ;; for sale || 待售 ;; for free || 免费 ;; for sure || 肯定，毫无疑问 ;; for the time being || 暂时，目前 ;;
- collocations: apply for || 申请 ;; wait for || 等待 ;; look for || 寻找 ;; pay for || 支付，为……付出代价 ;; care for || 照顾，关心 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + 形容词 + for sb. + to do sth. || 表示“对某人来说做某事是……的”，it作形式主语，真正主语是后面的不定式 ;; sth. is for + 用途/对象 || 表示某物的用途、适用对象或归属 ;; thank sb. for (doing) sth. || 表示“因（做了）某事感谢某人” ;;
- spokenExpressions: For goodness' sake! || 看在上帝的份上！（表示不耐烦、惊讶等情绪） ;; That's for you. || 这是给你的。 ;; For what it's worth. || 不管有用没用，仅供参考。 ;;
- idioms: for good || 永久地，一劳永逸地 ;; for a song || 非常便宜地 ;; for the birds || 荒唐可笑的，毫无价值的 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 为了，给 ;; 对于，关于 ;; 因为，由于 ;; 持续（一段时间） ;; 就……而言 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示对象、用途等，指为特定的人、事或目的 ;; 表示时间、距离，指持续的时长或范围 ;; 表示原因、理由，意为因为、由于 ;; 表示支持、赞同； ;; 表示对比，指就某类事物的通常情况来看 ;;
- definitionEn: used to show who is intended to receive or benefit from something, or what the purpose of something is ;; used to say how long an action or situation continues ;; used to state the reason why something happens or exists ;; used to say you support or agree with someone or something ;; used when making a judgment about someone or something, compared to what is usual ;;
- example: I bought a gift for my mother on Mother's Day. || 母亲节的时候我给妈妈买了一份礼物。
- example: We have been friends for more than ten years. || 我们已经做了十多年的朋友了。
- example: He got praised for his excellent performance in the project. || 他因为在项目中的出色表现受到了表扬。
- example: For a beginner, she plays the piano really well. || 就初学者而言，她钢琴弹得非常好。
- example: Are you for the new policy or against it? || 你是支持这项新政策还是反对？

### sense: conjunction
- translationZh: 因为，由于 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于较正式的书面语中，引出对前文内容的解释或理由，语气比because弱 ;;
- definitionEn: used to introduce the reason for something mentioned in the previous clause, more formal than 'because' ;;
- example: We left early, for the concert started at 7 o'clock. || 我们很早就出发了，因为音乐会7点开始。
- example: He must have caught a cold, for he was sneezing all morning. || 他肯定是感冒了，因为他一早上都在打喷嚏。
- example: The park was almost empty, for it was raining heavily. || 公园里几乎空无一人，因为当时雨下得很大。

## word: opposing
- uk: /əˈpəʊzɪŋ/
- us: /əˈpoʊzɪŋ/
- synonyms: conflicting || 冲突的，矛盾的 ;; contrary || 相反的，对立的 ;; opposite || 相反的，对面的 ;; rival || 竞争的，敌对的 ;; contradictory || 矛盾的，对立的 ;;
- antonyms: supporting || 支持的，拥护的 ;; allied || 同盟的，联合的 ;; agreeing || 一致的，同意的 ;;
- phrases: opposing views || 相反的观点 ;; opposing forces || 敌对势力 ;; opposing team || 对手队伍 ;; opposing side || 对立一方 ;;
- collocations: opposing argument || 对立论点 ;; opposing policy || 相反的政策 ;; opposing reaction || 抵触反应 ;; opposing faction || 反对派 ;;
- sentencePatterns: opposing + n. || 修饰名词，表示“对立的、相反的某事物” ;; be + opposing + to + sth. || 表示“反对某事物” ;;
- spokenExpressions: The opposing side really brought their A-game today. || 对方今天真的拿出了最佳状态。 ;; I can see where the opposing argument is coming from. || 我能理解对立论点的出发点。 ;; We're up against the opposing team next week. || 我们下周要和对手队比赛。 ;;
- idioms: on opposing ends of the spectrum || 处于完全对立的立场 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 反对的 ;; 对立的 ;; 相反的 ;;
- definitionZh: 持有相反意见或立场的；处于竞争、对抗关系的；性质、方向等完全相反的 ;;
- definitionEn: Holding different opinions or opposite standpoints; being in a competitive or confrontational relationship; completely different in nature, direction, etc. ;;
- example: The opposing parties failed to reach an agreement after three hours of negotiation. || 经过三个小时的谈判，对立各方未能达成一致。
- example: There are two opposing theories about how the ancient monument was built. || 关于这座古代纪念碑是如何建造的，存在两种截然相反的理论。
- example: The goalkeeper managed to block three shots from the opposing team in the first half. || 守门员在上半场成功挡住了对手队的三次射门。

### sense: verb (oppose的现在分词)
- translationZh: 反对 ;; 抵制 ;; 与…竞争 ;;
- definitionZh: 公开表示不同意某事物并试图阻止其发生；在竞争、对抗中与某人/某方对立 ;;
- definitionEn: Publicly express disagreement with something and try to prevent it from happening; compete or confront someone/something in a contest or conflict ;;
- example: A growing number of residents are opposing the plan to build a new chemical factory near the residential area. || 越来越多的居民反对在居民区附近建造新化工厂的计划。
- example: He spent his whole political career opposing unfair policies that discriminated against marginalized groups. || 他整个政治生涯都在抵制歧视边缘群体的不公平政策。
- example: The two athletes are opposing each other in the final of the national tennis championship. || 这两名运动员正在全国网球锦标赛的决赛中对阵。

## word: opposite to
- uk: /ˈɒpəzɪt tuː/
- us: /ˈɑːpəzɪt tuː/
- synonyms: contrary to || 与…相反 ;; opposed to || 与…对立 ;; reverse of || 与…反向 ;; conflicting with || 与…相冲突 ;; counter to || 与…相悖 ;;
- antonyms: consistent with || 与…一致 ;; identical to || 与…相同 ;; similar to || 与…相似 ;;
- phrases: be opposite to || 与…相反；在…对面 ;; run opposite to || 与…背道而驰 ;; hold views opposite to || 持与…相反的观点 ;; act opposite to one's words || 言行不一 ;;
- collocations: completely opposite to || 与…完全相反 ;; directly opposite to || 与…直接对立/正对面 ;; fundamentally opposite to || 与…根本对立 ;; opposite to expectations || 与预期相反 ;; opposite to the norm || 与常态相悖 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sth + be + opposite to + sth || 用于说明两个事物在性质、位置等方面的对立关系 ;; What is opposite to + sth? || 用于询问某事物的对立面或对面是什么 ;; Sth runs/ goes + opposite to + sth || 用于描述某事物的发展趋势、特性与另一事物相悖 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It's just opposite to what I thought! || 这和我想的正好相反！ ;; The store is opposite to the bus stop. || 商店就在公交站对面。 ;; That's completely opposite to what he said earlier. || 这和他之前说的完全不一样。 ;;
- idioms: diametrically opposite to || 与…截然相反 ;;

### sense: 介词短语
- translationZh: 与…相反；与…相对；在…对面 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示两者在性质、方向、位置、观点等方面完全对立或处于相对的位置 ;; 用于描述位置时指处于某个地点的正对面 ;;
- definitionEn: used to show that two things are completely different in nature, direction, opinion, etc. ;; used when describing location, meaning being directly across from a particular place ;;
- example: His political views are opposite to mine. || 他的政治观点和我的相反。
- example: The post office is opposite to the city library. || 邮局在市图书馆的对面。
- example: The result of the experiment was totally opposite to what we had predicted. || 实验结果和我们之前预测的完全相反。

## word: pro
- uk: /prəʊ/
- us: /proʊ/
- synonyms: professional || 专业人士 ;; expert || 专家 ;; specialist ||  specialist ;; adept || 能手 ;;
- antonyms: amateur || 业余爱好者 ;; novice || 新手 ;; beginner || 初学者 ;;
- phrases: pro and con || 正反双方 ;; pro bono || 无偿公益服务的 ;; pro rata || 按比例的 ;; pro tem || 临时的，暂时的 ;;
- collocations: pro athlete || 职业运动员 ;; pro tip || 专业建议，实用小技巧 ;; pro gamer || 职业玩家 ;; pro version || 专业版 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb is a pro at (doing) sth || 表示某人在某方面是行家 ;; It takes a pro to do sth || 表示做某事需要专业人士才能完成 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Total pro! || 太专业了！ ;; Pro move! || 这操作太厉害了！ ;;
- slang: pro crastinator || 拖延症患者（网络戏谑用法，由pro和procrastinator合成） ;;
- idioms: weigh the pros and cons || 权衡利弊 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 专业人士，职业选手 ;; 好处，优点 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在特定领域接受过专业训练、具备专业技能的从业者，尤指职业运动员等职业从业者 ;; 对某件事有利的因素、优势 ;;
- definitionEn: a person who has professional training and skills in a specific field, especially a professional athlete or other professional practitioner ;; an advantage or positive factor of something ;;
- example: As a pro in the marketing industry, he has helped dozens of brands achieve explosive growth. || 作为营销行业的专业人士，他已经帮助几十个品牌实现了爆发式增长。
- example: The biggest pro of living in the suburbs is that the environment is quieter and the housing price is much lower. || 住在郊区最大的优点是环境更安静，而且房价也低得多。
- example: Many young gamers dream of becoming esports pros and competing in international tournaments. || 很多年轻玩家都梦想成为电竞职业选手，去国际赛事中参赛。

### sense: 形容词
- translationZh: 职业的，专业的 ;; 支持的，赞成的 ;;
- definitionZh: 属于专业级别的、符合专业人士标准的，或与职业从事相关的 ;; 表示支持某一立场、观点的 ;;
- definitionEn: of a professional level, meeting the standards of a professional, or related to professional engagement ;; supporting a certain position or opinion ;;
- example: The team hired a pro coach to help them prepare for the national competition. || 这支队伍聘请了一位专业教练来帮他们备战全国比赛。
- example: He has always been pro environmental protection, so he never uses disposable plastic products. || 他一直都支持环保，所以从来不用一次性塑料制品。
- example: This pro editing software has far more functions than the free version for ordinary users. || 这款专业编辑软件的功能比面向普通用户的免费版要多得多。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 赞成地，支持地 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示站在支持、赞同某一方的立场上 ;;
- definitionEn: in a way that supports or agrees with a certain side ;;
- example: Most people attending the meeting voted pro the new reform plan. || 参会的大多数人都投票支持新的改革方案。
- example: Those who argue pro the policy emphasize its long-term benefits for low-income groups. || 那些支持这项政策的人强调了它对低收入群体的长期益处。

## word: age
- uk: /eɪdʒ/
- us: /eɪdʒ/
- synonyms: era || 时代，时期 ;; lifetime || 一生，寿命 ;; maturity || 成年，成熟 ;; epoch || 纪元，时期 ;;
- antonyms: youth || 青年，青春 ;; infancy || 婴儿期，初期 ;;
- phrases: old age || 老年 ;; age group || 年龄组 ;; come of age || 达到法定成年年龄 ;; age limit || 年龄限制 ;;
- collocations: chronological age || 实际年龄 ;; mental age || 心理年龄 ;; age discrimination || 年龄歧视 ;; average age || 平均年龄 ;;
- sentencePatterns: at the age of + 基数词 || 表示“在……岁时”，用于说明具体年龄节点 ;; It is + 形容词 + for sb of sb's age to do sth || 表示“对某人这个年龄的人来说做某事是……的”，用于评价特定年龄人群的行为 ;; age + 动词 (show/ catch up with/ take its toll on) || 表示“年龄显现/对某人产生影响/造成损害”，用于描述年龄带来的变化 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Look your age! || 你看起来和你年龄相符！（常用来调侃人打扮或行为不符合年龄） ;; Age is just a number. || 年龄只是个数字而已。（用来安慰在意年龄的人） ;; Act your age, not your shoe size. || 举止成熟点，别像个小孩。 ;;
- idioms: act one's age || 举止与年龄相称，别孩子气 ;; under age || 未成年，未到法定年龄 ;;
### sense: n. 名词
- translationZh: 年龄 ;; 时代，时期 ;; 寿命，使用年限 ;;
- definitionZh: 人或生物从出生到某一时刻的生存时长；历史上的某一特定发展阶段；物品能够正常使用的时长 ;;
- definitionEn: the length of time that a person has lived or a thing has existed; a distinct period of history; the period of time during which something is functional or valid ;;
- example: Her age is a secret she never tells anyone. || 她的年龄是她从不告诉任何人的秘密。
- example: We are living in the digital age, where technology changes every day. || 我们生活在数字时代，科技每天都在发生变化。
- example: The age of this old furniture is over 100 years. || 这件旧家具的使用年限已经超过100年了。
### sense: v. 动词
- translationZh: 变老，老化 ;; （使）显老，（使）显旧 ;; 成熟，变陈 ;;
- definitionZh: 随着时间推移出现衰老的特征；让某人/某物看起来更老或更旧；食物、酒等经过储存后品质变得更好 ;;
- definitionEn: to grow old or show signs of growing old; to make someone or something appear older; to develop in flavor or quality over a period of time, especially for food or alcohol ;;
- example: He has aged a lot since his wife passed away. || 自从他妻子去世后，他老了很多。
- example: The whiskey is aged in oak barrels for at least 10 years before bottling. || 这种威士忌在橡木桶中至少陈酿10年才装瓶。
- example: Sun exposure can age your skin much faster than normal. || 日晒会让你的皮肤比正常情况下老化得快得多。



## word: era
- uk: /ˈɪərə/
- us: /ˈɪrə/
- synonyms: epoch || 纪元，时代 ;; age || 时代，时期 ;; period || 时期，阶段 ;; time || 时代，时段 ;; epochal period || 划时代时期 ;;
- antonyms: instant || 瞬间，片刻 ;; moment || 片刻，瞬间 ;; fleeting moment || 转瞬即逝的时刻 ;;
- phrases: new era || 新时代 ;; Victorian era || 维多利亚时代 ;; digital era || 数字时代 ;; post-war era || 战后时代 ;; era of globalization || 全球化时代 ;;
- collocations: mark a new era || 标志着一个新时代 ;; usher in an era || 开启一个时代 ;; end an era || 结束一个时代 ;; define an era || 定义一个时代 ;; an era of innovation || 创新时代 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The era of + n. + has come/ended. || 表示某一领域的时代已经到来或结束 ;; We are entering/stepping into + adj. + era. || 表达正步入某个特征的时代 ;; sth. symbolizes the dawn of a new era. || 描述某事物象征新时代的开端 ;;
- spokenExpressions: That's a whole new era for us! || 那对我们来说是个全新的时代啊！;; Those styles are a relic of a bygone era. || 那些风格都是过去时代的老古董了。;; This invention will change the whole era, you'll see. || 这项发明会改变整个时代的，等着瞧吧。;;
- idioms: era of good feelings || 善意时代（美国历史上的一段政治和谐时期，现也泛指和平繁荣的时期）;;

### sense: 可数名词
- translationZh: 时代，时期 ;; 纪元 ;; 年代 ;;
- definitionZh: 历史上以重要事件、人物或特征为标志的较长的一段时期 ;; 地质年代的划分单位，小于宙大于纪 ;;
- definitionEn: a long and distinct period of history with a particular feature or characteristic ;; a major division of geological time, smaller than an eon and larger than a period ;;
- example: The invention of the Internet ushered in a new era of global communication. || 互联网的发明开启了全球通信的新时代。
- example: The Roman era lasted for more than a thousand years in Europe. || 罗马时代在欧洲延续了一千多年。
- example: Many dinosaur species went extinct at the end of the Mesozoic Era. || 许多恐龙物种在中生代末期灭绝了。
- example: We are now living in an era where artificial intelligence is rapidly changing every aspect of daily life. || 我们如今生活在一个人工智能正快速改变日常生活方方面面的时代。

## word: infancy
- uk: /ˈɪnfənsi/
- us: /ˈɪnfənsi/
- synonyms: babyhood || 婴儿期 ;; childhood || 幼年时期 ;; inception || 初期，开端 ;; outset || 起始，开端 ;;
- antonyms: adulthood || 成年期 ;; maturity || 成熟期 ;;
- phrases: in its infancy || 处于初期阶段 ;; early infancy || 婴儿早期 ;; infancy stage || 初始阶段 ;; infancy period || 婴儿期 ;;
- collocations: leave infancy || 脱离婴儿期；走出初创阶段 ;; the infancy of science || 科学的萌芽期 ;; infancy nutrition || 婴幼儿营养 ;; infancy development || 婴幼儿发育 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sth is still in its infancy || 某事物仍处于发展初期 ;; During infancy, sb/sth does sth || 在婴儿期/初创阶段，人/事物会做某事 ;; The infancy of sth saw sth happen || 在某事物的萌芽阶段发生了某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It’s still in its infancy, cut it some slack. || 它还在初创阶段，多给点宽容吧。 ;; Back in my infancy, my parents moved abroad. || 我还很小的时候，我爸妈就移居国外了。 ;; The tech is in its infancy, so don’t expect too much. || 这项技术还在初期阶段，别抱太高期望。 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 婴儿期，幼年 ;; 初期，初创阶段 ;;
- definitionZh: 人出生后的早期成长阶段，通常指从出生到会走路的时期；某事物发展的最初、尚未成熟的阶段 ;;
- definitionEn: the early stage of life when a person is a baby, usually from birth to the age of walking; the very beginning stage of the development of something, when it is not yet fully developed ;;
- example: Children's brains develop extremely rapidly during infancy. || 儿童的大脑在婴儿期发育得极其迅速。
- example: The renewable energy industry is still in its infancy in many developing countries. || 可再生能源产业在很多发展中国家仍处于初期阶段。
- example: The research into this rare disease is only in its infancy, so we have no effective treatment yet. || 针对这种罕见病的研究还处于萌芽阶段，所以我们目前还没有有效的治疗方法。

## word: lifetime
- uk: /ˈlaɪftaɪm/
- us: /ˈlaɪftaɪm/
- synonyms: lifespan || 寿命，生命周期 ;; lifetime span || 一生时长 ;; whole life || 一生，终身 ;; existence || 有生之年 ;;
- antonyms: moment || 瞬间，片刻 ;; instant || 刹那，顷刻 ;;
- phrases: lifetime achievement || 终身成就 ;; lifetime guarantee || 终身保修 ;; lifetime employment || 终身雇佣制 ;; of a lifetime || 千载难逢的 ;;
- collocations: a lifetime of experience || 毕生的经验 ;; spend a lifetime || 花费一生 ;; lifetime opportunity || 一生难得的机遇 ;; lifetime member || 终身会员 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It takes sb a lifetime to do sth || 表示某人花费一生时间做某事 ;; sth is the chance/opportunity of a lifetime || 表示某事物是千载难逢的机会 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Once in a lifetime! || 一辈子就这一次！ ;; A lifetime isn't long enough for that. || 一辈子都不够干这事的。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms: the chance/opportunity of a lifetime || 千载难逢的机遇 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 一生，终身 ;; 寿命，使用期 ;;
- definitionZh: 人从出生到死亡的整个时间段 ;; 事物存在或发挥作用的整个时长 ;;
- definitionEn: The entire period of time during which a person is alive ;; The period of time during which something exists, functions, or lasts ;;
- example: He dedicated his lifetime to the research of environmental protection. || 他把毕生精力都投入到了环境保护研究中。
- example: This high-quality watch comes with a lifetime warranty. || 这款高品质手表提供终身保修服务。
- example: Meeting the legendary artist in person was the opportunity of a lifetime. || 能亲自见到那位传奇艺术家是千载难逢的机会。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 终身的，一生的 ;;
- definitionZh: 持续或适用于某人整个一生的 ;;
- definitionEn: Lasting or valid for the entire duration of a person's life ;;
- example: She was honored with a lifetime membership of the literary association. || 她被授予该文学协会的终身会员资格。
- example: The famous director received a lifetime achievement award at the film festival. || 这位著名导演在电影节上获得了终身成就奖。

## word: maturity
- uk: /məˈtʃʊərəti/
- us: /məˈtʃʊrəti/
- synonyms: adulthood || 成年 ;; ripeness || 成熟 ;; readiness || 妥当 ;; sophistication || 老练 ;;
- antonyms: immaturity || 不成熟 ;; childhood || 童年 ;;
- phrases: emotional maturity || 情感成熟 ;; sexual maturity || 性成熟 ;; reach maturity || 达到成熟 ;; maturity date || 到期日 ;;
- collocations: show maturity || 展现成熟 ;; lack maturity || 缺乏成熟 ;; financial maturity || 财务成熟 ;; cognitive maturity || 认知成熟 ;;
- sentencePatterns: reach maturity at + 年龄 || 表示在某一年龄达到成熟 ;; show maturity in + 某方面 || 表示在某方面展现出成熟 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Maturity looks good on you. || 你成熟起来挺有魅力的。 ;; It takes time to gain maturity. || 成熟是需要时间的。 ;;
- idioms: come to maturity || 发展成熟；达成最终形态 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 成熟 ;; 到期 ;; 成熟期 ;;
- definitionZh: 人或动植物发育完全的状态；思想、行为等沉稳周全的特质；票据、贷款等到期的时间 ;; 事物发展到完善程度的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: the state of being fully grown or developed; the quality of behaving in a sensible and adult way; the time when a financial arrangement such as a bond becomes ready to be paid ;; the state of something that has developed to its most complete or advanced stage ;;
- example: Her maturity showed in how she handled the conflict calmly. || 她冷静处理冲突的方式体现了她的成熟。
- example: The bond's maturity is three years from the date of purchase. || 这只债券的到期日是购买日起三年后。
- example: Most trees reach full maturity after 10 to 20 years of growth. || 大多数树木经过10到20年的生长会达到完全成熟的状态。
