- definitionEn: The period of life between childhood and adulthood, typically ranging from puberty to around the age of 30. ;; The collective term for people who are in the youth age group. ;;
- example: She wrote a lot of poetry during her youth. || 她在青年时期写了很多诗歌。
- example: The youth of today are more environmentally conscious than previous generations. || 现在的年轻一代比前几代人更有环保意识。
- example: The local government has launched a new program to support youth entrepreneurship. || 当地政府推出了一项支持青年创业的新项目。

## word: ago
- uk: /əˈɡəʊ/
- us: /əˈɡoʊ/
- synonyms: earlier || 早些时候 ;; previously || 以前 ;; before || 之前 ;;
- antonyms: later || 后来 ;; hence || 此后 ;;
- phrases: long ago || 很久以前 ;; years ago || 多年前 ;; a while ago || 不久前 ;;
- collocations: a few minutes ago || 几分钟前 ;; two decades ago || 二十年前 ;; not long ago || 没多久以前 ;;
- sentencePatterns: [时间段] + ago + 一般过去时句子 || 表示多久之前发生的过去动作 ;; It was + [时间段] + ago + that + 一般过去时从句 || 强调多久之前发生的某事 ;;
- spokenExpressions: A while back ago? || 是不久之前的事儿对吧？ ;; That was ages ago! || 那都是老早以前的事了！ ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 以前 ;; 之前 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于表示从现在往回推算的某个时间之前 ;; 修饰表示时间段的词，说明动作发生在过去的某个时间点 ;;
- definitionEn: used to show how far back in the past something happened ;; used with a period of time to refer to a time before the present ;;
- example: I moved to this city three years ago. || 我三年前搬到了这座城市。
- example: She called you ten minutes ago, but you were out. || 她十分钟前给你打过电话，但你当时出去了。
- example: Long ago, there was a beautiful princess living in the castle. || 很久以前，城堡里住着一位美丽的公主。



## word: before
- uk: /bɪˈfɔː(r)/
- us: /bɪˈfɔːr/
- synonyms: prior to || 在…之前 ;; earlier than || 早于 ;; preceding || 在…前面 ;; ahead of || 领先于，在…之前 ;; previously || 先前 ;;
- antonyms: after || 在…之后 ;; following || 在…后面 ;; later than || 晚于 ;;
- phrases: before long || 不久，很快 ;; the day before yesterday || 前天 ;; before now || 此前，到现在为止 ;; before dawn || 黎明前 ;; long before || 很久以前 ;;
- collocations: appear before || 出现在…面前；出庭 ;; go before || 走在前面；被提交 ;; think before acting || 三思而后行 ;; meet before the meeting || 会前见面 ;; arrive before noon || 正午前到达 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It + be + 时间段 + before + 从句 || 表示“过了多久才…” ;; 主句（完成时）+ before + 从句（一般时） || 表示“在从句动作发生之前，主句动作已经完成” ;; Hardly/Scarcely + 过去完成时 + before + 一般过去时从句 || 表示“刚…就…” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Before I forget! || 趁我还没忘！ ;; Let me think before I answer. || 让我先想想再回答。 ;; I've never seen that before! || 我以前从没见过那个！ ;;
- idioms: before you know it || 转眼之间，很快 ;; cast pearls before swine || 对牛弹琴 ;; before one's time || 过早，在某人出生/涉足之前 ;;

### sense: preposition
- translationZh: 在…之前；先于；面对；由…考虑处理 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示时间、位置、顺序等在某个人、事物或动作的前面；在需要处理、决定某事物的相关人员面前 ;;
- definitionEn: earlier in time, position, or order than someone or something; in the presence of someone who will judge, consider, or deal with something ;;
- example: Please arrive 10 minutes before the meeting starts. || 请在会议开始前十分钟到达。
- example: He stood before the judge waiting for the sentence. || 他站在法官面前等待判决。
- example: Health comes before wealth in most people's priority lists. || 在大多数人的优先级清单里，健康排在财富前面。

### sense: conjunction
- translationZh: 在…以前；到…为止；免得；不然 ;;
- definitionZh: 连接两个分句，表示主句动作发生在从句动作之前；用于提醒避免某事发生，或表示否则会出现某种情况 ;;
- definitionEn: used to connect two clauses, showing that the action in the main clause happens earlier than the action in the subordinate clause; used to warn that something should be done to avoid a bad situation ;;
- example: Turn off the lights before you leave the office. || 你离开办公室之前把灯关掉。
- example: Lock the door before someone breaks in. || 把门锁好，免得有人闯进来。
- example: It will be several months before the project is completed. || 还要好几个月这个项目才能完工。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 以前；过去；已经 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示在过去的某个时间，或在提到的某个时间之前 ;;
- definitionEn: at an earlier time; in the past; previously ;;
- example: I have been to Paris once before. || 我以前去过一次巴黎。
- example: That happened long before, when I was still a child. || 那件事发生在很久以前，当时我还是个孩子。
- example: She never told me about that before. || 她之前从没跟我说过那件事。

## word: earlier
- uk: /ˈɜːliə(r)/
- us: /ˈɜːrliər/
- synonyms: previous || 先前的，以前的 ;; prior || 在前的，优先的 ;; antecedent || 先前的，先行的 ;; former || 从前的，前者的 ;; preceding || 在前的，前面的 ;;
- antonyms: later || 后来的，稍后的 ;; subsequent || 随后的，之后的 ;; following || 接下来的，下述的 ;;
- phrases: earlier this year || 今年年初 ;; earlier on || 在初期，早先 ;; earlier today || 今天早些时候 ;; no earlier than || 不早于 ;; earlier period || 早期，前期 ;;
- collocations: arrive earlier || 早到 ;; leave earlier || 提前离开 ;; earlier version || 早期版本 ;; earlier stage || 初期阶段 ;; earlier experience || 先前的经验 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It was earlier + 时间状语 + that + 从句 || 强调“在更早的某个时间发生了某事”的强调句型 ;; ... earlier than expected || 表达“比预期更早”的比较结构 ;; If you had done sth earlier, you would have done sth || 表示“如果早点做某事就会达成某结果”的虚拟语气句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Earlier I was thinking... || 我刚才还在想… ;; Let's meet an hour earlier, okay? || 我们提前一小时见面，好吗？ ;; I should have told you earlier. || 我本该早点告诉你的。 ;;
- slang:
- idioms: the earlier the better || 越早越好 ;;

### sense: 形容词（adj.）
- translationZh: 更早的 ;; 先前的，以前的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指时间上更早发生或存在的；属于过去某个更早时间的 ;; 指在序列、顺序中排在前面的 ;;
- definitionEn: happening or existing before the present time or before the time you are talking about ;; coming before something else in order or sequence ;;
- example: I remember an earlier conversation we had about this project. || 我记得我们之前就这个项目有过一次谈话。
- example: The earlier version of the app had a lot more bugs than the current one. || 这款应用的早期版本比现在的版本漏洞多得多。
- example: We avoided the rush hour by taking an earlier train. || 我们坐了更早一班火车，避开了高峰时段。

### sense: 副词（adv.）
- translationZh: 更早地 ;; 先前，之前 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在某个特定时间之前发生或完成；时间上先于另一事件 ;; 指在过去的某个时间点，之前 ;;
- definitionEn: before the time that was arranged or expected ;; at a time before the present time or before the time you are talking about ;;
- example: If you had woken up earlier, you wouldn't have missed the school bus. || 你要是早点醒，就不会错过校车了。
- example: I saw your sister earlier in the supermarket, she was buying some snacks. || 我之前在超市看到你姐姐了，她当时在买一些零食。
- example: The meeting has been rescheduled to start half an hour earlier than planned. || 会议改时间了，比计划的提前半小时开始。

## word: hence
- uk: /hens/
- us: /hens/
- synonyms: therefore || 因此 ;; thus || 所以 ;; consequently || 因而 ;; accordingly || 相应地 ;; so || 于是 ;;
- antonyms: because || 因为 ;; since || 既然 ;;
- phrases: henceforth || 从今以后 ;; henceforward || 自此以后 ;; years hence || 几年后 ;; decades hence || 几十年后 ;; a week hence || 一周后 ;;
- collocations: hence the result || 因此有了这个结果 ;; hence the reason || 这就是原因 ;; hence it follows that || 由此得出 ;; hence the importance || 因此重要性在于 ;; hence the need || 因此有必要 ;;
- sentencePatterns: 分句 + ，hence + 名词短语 || 用于说明前文所述情况带来的直接结果 ;; 完整句子 + ; hence + 完整句子 || 连接两个有因果关系的独立分句，用分号分隔 ;; It is + 形容词 + that... , hence + 结论性分句 || 先说明某个事实的属性，再引出推论 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Hence the name. || 所以才有了这个名字。 ;; Hence the problem. || 这就是问题所在。 ;; Hence my confusion. || 所以我才会困惑。 ;;
- idioms: hence with || 拿走，去掉 ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 因此，所以 ;; 由此，因而 ;; 从现在起，此后 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于引出前文陈述内容所导致的结果或推论 ;; 表示从当前时间开始计算的某个时间点之后 ;;
- definitionEn: used to introduce a result or inference that follows logically from what has just been stated ;; used to refer to a time that starts from now ;;
- example: The cost of raw materials has risen sharply, hence the increase in product prices. || 原材料成本大幅上涨，因此产品价格有所提升。
- example: This kind of insect is highly adaptable to cold environments, hence its ability to survive in polar regions. || 这种昆虫对寒冷环境有极强的适应力，因此能在极地地区存活。
- example: We plan to finalize the project three months hence, so we need to speed up the current progress. || 我们计划三个月后完成这个项目，因此现在需要加快进度。

## word: later
- uk: /ˈleɪtə(r)/
- us: /ˈleɪtər/
- synonyms: afterwards || 后来，之后 ;; subsequently || 随后，继而 ;; thereafter || 此后，之后 ;;
- antonyms: earlier || 更早，先前 ;; before || 之前，以前 ;;
- phrases: later on || 后来，稍后 ;; see you later || 再见，回头见 ;; no later than || 不迟于 ;; sooner or later || 迟早，早晚 ;;
- collocations: much later || 很久以后 ;; a little later || 稍晚一点 ;; later years || 晚年 ;; later stage || 后期 ;;
- sentencePatterns: ... later + 句子 || 表示一段时间之后发生某事，可放在句首或句尾 ;; It is later than you think. || 固定表达，意为“时间比你想的要晚/事情已经到了更严重的地步” ;;
- spokenExpressions: Catch you later! || 回头见！;; Talk to you later! || 之后再聊！;; Later! || 拜拜！走了！;;
- idioms: sooner or later || 迟早，终归 ;;

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 后来，以后 ;; 晚些时候，稍后 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在某个时间点或事件之后的时间；比预期或原定时间更晚 ;; 用于指将来的某个时间，或过去某个时间点之后的时段 ;;
- definitionEn: at a time in the future, or after the time you are talking about; after the time that sth is expected to happen or the usual time ;;
- example: I'll call you later when I get home. || 我到家之后会给你打电话。
- example: He arrived ten minutes later than everyone else. || 他比其他人晚到了十分钟。
- example: Later, she realized that she had made a mistake. || 后来她意识到自己犯了个错误。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 后来的，后期的 ;; 晚年的，较后的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在时间上更靠后的，属于某个时段末尾的；相比早期版本、阶段等更新的 ;;
- definitionEn: happening or existing at a time after an earlier one; near the end of a period of time, sb's life, etc. ;;
- example: The later chapters of the book are much more interesting. || 这本书的后面几章要有趣得多。
- example: His later works show a more mature painting style. || 他后期的作品展现出了更成熟的绘画风格。
- example: In later life, he moved to the countryside to live alone. || 晚年时他搬到乡下独自生活。

## word: previously
- uk: /ˈpriːviəsli/
- us: /ˈpriːviəsli/
- synonyms: formerly || 以前，从前 ;; earlier || 早些时候，先前 ;; before || 之前，以前 ;; beforehand || 事先，预先 ;; hitherto || 迄今，至今 ;;
- antonyms: later || 后来，随后 ;; subsequently || 随后，之后 ;; hereafter || 今后，此后 ;;
- phrases: previously mentioned || 之前提到的 ;; previously unknown || 此前未知的 ;; previously agreed || 事先约定的 ;; previously held || 之前持有的，先前担任的 ;; previously scheduled || 原定计划的 ;;
- collocations: previously arranged meeting || 预先安排的会议 ;; previously published data || 此前发布的数据 ;; previously occupied territory || 先前被占领的领土 ;; previously convicted offender || 有前科的罪犯 ;; previously unseen footage || 从未公开的影像片段 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It was previously believed that... || 人们此前认为……（用于表述过去的普遍看法，通常暗示该看法现在已被推翻） ;; The project, previously planned for Q2, will be launched in Q3. || 原定第二季度的项目将在第三季度启动（用于插入语说明事物的原有安排） ;; As previously announced, the new policy will take effect next month. || 正如此前宣布的那样，新政策将于下月生效（用于引出之前已经告知过的信息） ;;
- spokenExpressions: As I mentioned previously... || 正如我之前提到的…… ;; If you've previously signed up, you don't need to register again. || 如果你之前已经报过名，就不用再注册了 ;; I haven't met him previously, so I'm not sure what he looks like. || 我之前没见过他，所以不确定他长什么样 ;;
- idioms: as previously noted || 如前所述 ;;

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 先前，以前 ;; 事先，预先 ;;
- definitionZh: 指在某个时间、事件或行动之前发生或存在的；提前安排或知晓的 ;; 用于引出更早的时间点的情况，或说明某事物的原有状态 ;;
- definitionEn: at a time before the present time or before the event you are talking about ;; before something happens or is done, used to describe an earlier state or arrangement ;;
- example: The building was previously used as a warehouse. || 这栋建筑以前被用作仓库。
- example: She had previously worked in marketing before switching to education. || 她转行做教育之前曾在营销行业工作。
- example: The previously scheduled concert has been postponed due to bad weather. || 原定举办的音乐会因为恶劣天气推迟了。

## word: agreement
- uk: /əˈɡriːmənt/
- us: /əˈɡriːmənt/
- synonyms: contract || 合同 ;; accord || 协议 ;; pact || 契约 ;; consensus || 共识 ;; concord || 一致 ;;
- antonyms: disagreement || 分歧 ;; dispute || 争端 ;; conflict || 冲突 ;;
- phrases: trade agreement || 贸易协定 ;; mutual agreement || 共同协议 ;; verbal agreement || 口头协议 ;; binding agreement || 有约束力的协议 ;; prenuptial agreement || 婚前协议 ;;
- collocations: reach an agreement || 达成协议 ;; sign an agreement || 签署协议 ;; draft an agreement || 起草协议 ;; breach an agreement || 违反协议 ;; honor an agreement || 履行协议 ;;
- sentencePatterns: reach an agreement on sth || 表示就某事项达成共识的句型 ;; enter into an agreement with sb || 表示与某人签订协议的句型 ;; be in agreement with sth || 表示与某观点/事物一致的句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: We have an agreement! || 我们可是说好的！ ;; Are we in agreement on this? || 这件事我们达成一致了吧？ ;; Let's put this agreement in writing. || 咱们把这份约定落实成书面形式吧。 ;;
- idioms: a gentleman's agreement || 君子协定 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 协议；协定 ;; 一致；同意 ;;
- definitionZh: 两方或多方之间达成的具有约束力的约定，通常涉及权利和义务的划分 ;; 不同主体在意见、立场、意愿等方面的统一状态 ;;
- definitionEn: a formal arrangement between two or more parties that specifies obligations and rights, which is legally enforceable ;; a state in which people have the same opinion, intention or position about something ;;
- example: The two companies signed a three-year cooperation agreement last week. || 这两家公司上周签署了一份为期三年的合作协议。
- example: After hours of negotiation, the management and the union finally reached an agreement on salary increases. || 经过数小时谈判，管理层和工会最终就加薪问题达成了一致。
- example: I am in full agreement with your proposal to adjust the project schedule. || 我完全同意你提出的调整项目进度的建议。



## word: accord
- uk: /əˈkɔːd/
- us: /əˈkɔːrd/
- synonyms: agreement || 协议，同意 ;; conform || 符合，一致 ;; grant || 授予，给予 ;; reconcile || 调和，使一致 ;;
- antonyms: conflict || 冲突，抵触 ;; disagree || 不一致，不同意 ;; deny || 拒绝，不授予 ;;
- phrases: in accord with || 与…一致 ;; of one's own accord || 自愿地，主动地 ;; reach an accord || 达成协议 ;; accord with || 符合，与…相符 ;;
- collocations: accord priority to || 优先考虑 ;; accord full recognition to || 充分认可 ;; mutual accord || 双方协议 ;; peace accord || 和平协议 ;;
- sentencePatterns: accord sb sth || 双宾语结构，表示授予某人某物 ;; accord with sth || 不及物动词用法，表示与某事物一致 ;; It is accorded that... || 形式主语结构，表示普遍认为… ;;
- spokenExpressions: Of my own accord. || 我是自愿的。;; We're in accord on this. || 我们在这件事上意见一致。;; That accords with what I heard. || 这和我听到的一致。;;
- idioms: of one's own accord || 主动地，自愿地 ;;

### sense: 动词（v.）
- translationZh: （与…）一致，符合 ;; 授予，给予 ;;
- definitionZh: 与某种情况、观点或标准保持一致；正式授予某人权力、地位或待遇等 ;;
- definitionEn: To agree with or match something; To formally give someone a position, right, or special treatment ;;
- example: His version of the event accords with the witness's statement. || 他对事件的描述和证人的证词一致。
- example: The university accorded him an honorary degree for his academic contributions. || 这所大学因他的学术贡献授予他荣誉学位。
- example: These new policies do not accord with the government's earlier promises. || 这些新政策和政府之前的承诺不相符。

### sense: 名词（n.）
- translationZh: 协议，协定 ;; 一致，符合 ;;
- definitionZh: 两方或多方达成的正式协议；不同事物之间保持一致的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: A formal agreement between two or more groups or countries; A situation in which two people or things are in agreement ;;
- example: The two countries signed a peace accord to end the decade-long conflict. || 两国签署了和平协定，结束了长达十年的冲突。
- example: The results are in accord with previous research findings. || 这些结果和之前的研究发现一致。
- example: He left the job of his own accord, without anyone asking him to. || 他主动辞去了工作，没有人要求他这么做。

## word: contract
- uk: /ˈkɒntrækt/ (noun); /kənˈtrækt/ (verb)
- us: /ˈkɑːntrækt/ (noun); /kənˈtrækt/ (verb)
- synonyms: agreement || 协议，契约 ;; pact || 协定，公约 ;; covenant || 盟约，契约 ;; shrink || 收缩，缩小 ;; condense || 压缩，浓缩 ;;
- antonyms: expand || 扩张，膨胀 ;; extend || 延伸，扩大 ;; disagreement || 分歧，异议 ;;
- phrases: employment contract || 劳动合同 ;; sales contract || 销售合同 ;; contract law || 合同法 ;; contract out || 外包，订约承办 ;; breach of contract || 违约 ;;
- collocations: sign a contract || 签署合同 ;; terminate a contract || 终止合同 ;; binding contract || 具有约束力的合同 ;; contract a disease || 感染疾病 ;; contract muscles || 收缩肌肉 ;;
- sentencePatterns: contract with sb to do sth || 表示“与某人签订合同做某事”的结构 ;; contract sth from sb/sth || 表示“从某人/某物处感染（疾病）”的结构 ;; be contracted to sb || 表示“与某人签约受雇”的被动结构 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Get that in writing in the contract. || 把那点写到合同里，白纸黑字。 ;; We're under contract, so we can't back out now. || 我们签了合同，现在不能反悔了。 ;; The contract runs for another two years. || 这份合同还有两年有效期。 ;;
- idioms: a contract is a contract || 合同就是合同（指必须遵守约定） ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 合同，契约 ;; 婚约 ;; （语法中的）缩略形式 ;;
- definitionZh: 双方或多方共同签署的具有法律效力的协议 ;; 表示约定婚姻的正式文书 ;; 由两个或多个单词组合而成的缩短书写形式 ;;
- definitionEn: a legal agreement between two or more parties that is enforceable by law ;; a formal agreement of marriage ;; a shortened form of a word or group of words used in grammar ;;
- example: The company offered me a two-year employment contract. || 公司给了我一份为期两年的劳动合同。
- example: You need to read all the terms carefully before signing the contract. || 签署合同之前你需要仔细阅读所有条款。
- example: "Don't" is a common contract of "do not". || "Don't"是"do not"的常见缩略形式。

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 收缩，缩小 ;; 感染（疾病） ;; 签订合同，订约 ;;
- definitionZh: 物体的体积、尺寸变小，或肌肉收紧 ;; 患上某种传染性疾病 ;; 与他人达成正式的契约约定 ;;
- definitionEn: to become smaller in size, or to make a muscle tighter ;; to catch or develop an infectious disease ;; to make a formal legal agreement with someone ;;
- example: Metal contracts when it gets cold. || 金属遇冷会收缩。
- example: He contracted a rare tropical disease during his trip to the rainforest. || 他在雨林旅行期间感染了一种罕见的热带疾病。
- example: The city has contracted with a local construction firm to build the new bridge. || 该市已经和当地一家建筑公司签订了建造新桥的合同。

## word: disagreement
- uk: /ˌdɪsəˈɡriːmənt/
- us: /ˌdɪsəˈɡriːmənt/
- synonyms: conflict || 冲突，争执 ;; dispute || 争论，争端 ;; dissent || 异议，意见不合 ;; argument || 争论，争吵 ;; discord || 不和，分歧 ;;
- antonyms: agreement || 同意，一致 ;; consensus || 共识，一致意见 ;; accord || 一致，和谐 ;;
- phrases: disagreement over sth || 关于某事的分歧 ;; disagreement between A and B || 甲乙双方的分歧 ;; area of disagreement || 分歧领域 ;; bitter disagreement || 严重分歧 ;; resolve a disagreement || 解决分歧 ;;
- collocations: cause disagreement || 引发分歧 ;; express disagreement || 表达异议 ;; have a disagreement || 产生分歧 ;; settle a disagreement || 平息分歧 ;; sharp disagreement || 尖锐分歧 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There is disagreement among sb about/over sth || 表示“某群体在某事上存在分歧” ;; A disagreement arises between A and B over sth || 表示“甲乙双方因某事产生分歧” ;; Sth led to serious disagreement between the two sides || 表示“某事导致双方出现严重分歧” ;;
- spokenExpressions: We have a little disagreement. || 我们有点小分歧。 ;; There's no disagreement there. || 这一点上大家没意见。 ;; Let's sort out this disagreement, shall we? || 我们把这个分歧解决了，好吗？ ;;
- idioms: have a disagreement of opinions || 意见不合 ;; agree to disagree || 保留各自意见，接受分歧存在 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 意见分歧 ;; 争执 ;; 不一致 ;;
- definitionZh: 人们在观点、看法、利益等方面存在的不同或矛盾；因意见不合产生的争论或冲突；事物之间不匹配、不一致的情况 ;;
- definitionEn: a difference of opinions, views, or interests between people; an argument or conflict caused by such a difference; a situation in which things do not match or correspond with each other ;;
- example: The couple had a minor disagreement about where to spend their holiday. || 这对夫妇在去哪里度假的问题上有个小分歧。
- example: There is widespread disagreement among experts over the effectiveness of the new policy. || 专家们对这项新政策的有效性存在普遍分歧。
- example: The disagreement between the management and the workers led to a three-day strike. || 管理层和工人之间的争执引发了一场为期三天的罢工。
- example: The survey found a sharp disagreement between the views of young people and older generations on this social issue. || 调查发现年轻人和老一辈在这个社会问题上的观点存在严重分歧。

## word: dispute
- uk: /dɪˈspjuːt/
- us: /dɪˈspjuːt/
- synonyms: argument || 争论，争吵 ;; conflict || 冲突，争执 ;; disagreement || 分歧，意见不合 ;; debate || 辩论，讨论 ;; quarrel || 口角，吵架 ;;
- antonyms: agreement || 同意，一致 ;; harmony || 和谐，融洽 ;; consensus || 共识，一致意见 ;;
- phrases: border dispute || 边界争端 ;; labor dispute || 劳资纠纷 ;; dispute resolution || 争议解决 ;; under dispute || 存在争议的 ;; legal dispute || 法律纠纷 ;;
- collocations: resolve a dispute || 解决争端 ;; spark a dispute || 引发争议 ;; settle a dispute || 平息纷争 ;; bitter dispute || 激烈的争执 ;; long-running dispute || 长期的争端 ;;
- sentencePatterns: dispute over sth || 表示“就某事产生争议” ;; It is disputed that... || 表示“……是存在争议的” ;; dispute with sb about/over sth || 表示“与某人就某事争论” ;;
- spokenExpressions: No dispute there. || 这一点没什么可争的。 ;; That's beyond dispute. || 这是无可争辩的。 ;; Let's not dispute over trivial things. || 咱们别为鸡毛蒜皮的事争了。 ;;
- idioms: past dispute || 无可争辩，毋庸置疑 ;;

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 争论，争吵 ;; 争端，纠纷 ;; 异议，质疑 ;;
- definitionZh: 两方或多方之间因意见不合产生的激烈争论；对某事的合法性、真实性等存在的不同意见 ;;
- definitionEn: a serious argument or disagreement between two or more groups or people; doubt about the truth or validity of something ;;
- example: The two countries have been involved in a territorial dispute for decades. || 这两个国家几十年来一直陷入领土争端。
- example: The exact cause of the accident is still in dispute. || 事故的确切原因仍然存在争议。
- example: The workers' strike was caused by a pay dispute with the management. || 工人罢工是由和管理层的薪资纠纷引发的。

### sense: 动词
- translationZh: 争论，辩论 ;; 对……提出质疑，否认 ;; 争夺（地盘、头衔等） ;;
- definitionZh: 就某事和他人争论；公开对某事的真实性、正确性等表示怀疑；争相获取某一事物的所有权 ;;
- definitionEn: to argue about something with someone; to say that something is not true, correct, or legal; to fight for control of something ;;
- example: No one disputed that the new policy would bring more benefits to low-income families. || 没有人质疑新政策会给低收入家庭带来更多福利这一说法。
- example: The two teams are disputing the championship title in the final match. || 两支队伍正在决赛中争夺冠军头衔。
- example: She disputed with her neighbor for hours over the noise from the construction work. || 她因为施工噪音和邻居争论了好几个小时。

## word: pact
- uk: /pækt/
- us: /pækt/
- synonyms: agreement || 协议，协定 ;; treaty || 条约，协约 ;; covenant || 盟约，契约 ;; accord || 协约，协议 ;; compact || 契约，合约 ;;
- antonyms: disagreement || 分歧，异议 ;; breach || 违约，违反 ;; repudiation || 废除，拒绝履行 ;;
- phrases: peace pact || 和平协定 ;; trade pact || 贸易协定 ;; non-aggression pact || 互不侵犯条约 ;; mutual defense pact || 共同防御协定 ;;
- collocations: sign a pact || 签署协定 ;; ratify a pact || 批准协定 ;; violate a pact || 违反协定 ;; negotiate a pact || 磋商协定 ;;
- sentencePatterns: The two countries signed a pact to do sth. || 两国签署协定以做某事，用于说明协定的签署目的 ;; Under the terms of the pact, sb./sth. will do sth. || 根据协定条款，某方将做某事，用于说明协定的具体内容 ;;
- spokenExpressions: We have a pact, right? || 我们说好的，对吧？ ;; Let's make a pact. || 我们定个约定吧。 ;; The pact's off if you break your promise. || 你要是食言，咱们的约定就作废了。 ;;
- idioms: a gentleman's pact || 君子协定 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 协定，条约 ;; 约定，契约 ;;
- definitionZh: 指两个或多个国家、组织或个人之间正式签订的、具有约束力的协议 ;; 也可指非正式的私人约定、承诺 ;;
- definitionEn: a formal written agreement between two or more countries, groups, or people that is legally binding ;; an informal promise or agreement made between people ;;
- example: The two nations signed a non-aggression pact to avoid military conflict. || 这两个国家签署了互不侵犯条约，以避免军事冲突。
- example: The children made a pact to never tell anyone about their secret hideout. || 孩子们约定永远不告诉任何人他们的秘密藏身之处。
- example: The trade pact between the two blocs is expected to boost cross-border commerce by 30 percent. || 这两个集团之间的贸易协定预计将推动跨境贸易增长30%。

## word: air
- uk: /eə(r)/
- us: /er/
- synonyms: atmosphere || 大气，大气层 ;; breeze || 微风 ;; appearance || 外貌，神态 ;;
- antonyms: land || 陆地 ;; water || 水 ;;
- phrases: air conditioning || 空调系统 ;; air force || 空军 ;; by air || 乘飞机 ;; air pollution || 空气污染 ;; fresh air || 新鲜空气 ;;
- collocations: clean air || 洁净的空气 ;; cold air || 冷空气 ;; air travel || 航空旅行 ;; air ticket || 机票 ;; put on airs || 摆架子 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + adj + to breathe the air + 地点状语 || 表示在某地呼吸空气的感受 ;; The air + 系动词 + adj + 时间状语 || 描述某段时间的空气状态 ;; sb + send sth by air + 目的状语 || 说明某人通过航空邮寄某物的目的 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Clear the air! || 把话说开，消除误会！ ;; Take air! || 出去透透气！ ;; Walk on air! || 高兴得飘飘然！ ;;
- idioms: up in the air || 悬而未决，尚未确定 ;; build castles in the air || 做白日梦，空想 ;;

### sense: n. (名词)
- translationZh: 空气 ;; 天空，空中 ;; 神态，气质 ;;
- definitionZh: 地球周围的混合气体，是人类、动植物生存所必需的物质 ;; 地球表面以上的空间，大气层所处的区域 ;; 人或事物呈现出来的整体印象、神态或氛围 ;;
- definitionEn: the mixture of gases that surrounds the earth and that people, animals and plants breathe ;; the space above the earth's surface where planes fly ;; the particular feeling or impression that is given by sb/sth ;;
- example: We need to open the window to let some fresh air in. || 我们需要打开窗户让新鲜空气进来。
- example: There were several birds flying high in the air. || 有几只鸟在空中高高飞翔。
- example: She has an air of confidence that makes her very popular in the team. || 她身上有一种自信的气质，这让她在团队里很受欢迎。

### sense: v. (动词)
- translationZh: 晾晒，通风 ;; 公开发表（观点、不满） ;; 播出（电视或广播节目） ;;
- definitionZh: 把衣物、被褥等放在通风处，或置于阳光下除去潮气和异味 ;; 公开表达自己的意见、抱怨等想法 ;; 电视或广播电台播放某个节目 ;;
- definitionEn: to let air enter a room, building, etc. to make it smell fresh and cool, or to put clothes in a place where the air can dry them completely ;; to express your opinions or complaints publicly ;; to broadcast a programme on television or radio ;;
- example: You should air your quilt on sunny days to get rid of the dampness. || 晴天的时候你应该晒晒被子去去潮气。
- example: The meeting gave everyone a chance to air their opinions about the new policy. || 这次会议给了每个人发表对新政策看法的机会。
- example: This documentary will be aired on national television next week. || 这部纪录片将于下周在国家电视台播出。

- definitionEn: the way that a person or thing looks to other people ;; an occasion when someone appears in public or in a particular place ;; the act of starting to exist or becoming noticeable ;;
- example: She was very proud of her neat appearance when attending the interview. || 她参加面试时为自己整洁的外表感到十分自豪。

- example: The singer's last public appearance was at the charity gala last December. || 这位歌手最后一次公开露面是在去年12月的慈善晚会上。

## word: atmosphere
- uk: /ˈætməsfɪə(r)/
- us: /ˈætməsfɪr/
- synonyms: ambience || 氛围，环境 ;; air || 空气，气氛 ;; mood || 情绪，氛围 ;; vibe || 感应，气氛 ;; climate || 气候，风气 ;;
- antonyms: void || 虚空，空白 ;; vacuum || 真空，空白 ;;
- phrases: earth's atmosphere || 地球大气层 ;; working atmosphere || 工作氛围 ;; festive atmosphere || 节日氛围 ;; atmospheric pollution || 大气污染 ;; tense atmosphere || 紧张气氛 ;;
- collocations: create an atmosphere || 营造氛围 ;; ruin the atmosphere || 破坏气氛 ;; warm atmosphere || 温暖的氛围 ;; relaxed atmosphere || 轻松的氛围 ;; upper atmosphere || 高层大气 ;;
- sentencePatterns: There is a + adj. + atmosphere + in/at + place || 表示某处有某种氛围 ;; The atmosphere of + place/event + makes sb + feel + adj. || 表示某地/某活动的氛围让某人产生某种感受 ;; + pollute/protect + the atmosphere || 表示污染/保护大气的动作 ;;
- spokenExpressions: The atmosphere here is so nice! || 这里的氛围太棒了！ ;; Let's light some candles to set the atmosphere. || 我们点些蜡烛来烘托氛围吧。 ;; That awkward atmosphere almost killed me. || 那尴尬的氛围快让我窒息了。 ;;
- idioms: heavy atmosphere || 压抑的氛围 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 大气层，大气 ;; 氛围，气氛 ;; 空气 ;;
- definitionZh: 环绕地球或其他天体的气体层 ;; 特定场所、群体或事件中人们感受到的整体情绪和环境基调 ;; 某个地方的空气，尤指其特质给人的感受 ;;
- definitionEn: the layer of gases that surrounds the earth or another planet ;; the general feeling or mood that exists in a particular place, among a group of people, or at an event ;; the air in a particular place, especially when it has a particular quality ;;
- example: The spacecraft re-entered the earth's atmosphere at a very high speed. || 宇宙飞船以极高的速度重返地球大气层。
- example: The warm and welcoming atmosphere of the small café makes it my favorite spot to study. || 这家小咖啡馆温暖宜人的氛围让它成了我最爱的学习地点。
- example: There was a very tense atmosphere at the meeting when the topic of layoffs was brought up. || 当裁员的话题被提出来时，会议现场的气氛十分紧张。

## word: breeze
- uk: /briːz/
- us: /briːz/
- synonyms: gust || 一阵风 ;; zephyr || 和风，微风 ;; waft || 一阵微风 ;; walkover || 轻易取得的胜利 ;; cinch || 容易做的事 ;;
- antonyms: gale || 大风，狂风 ;; storm || 暴风雨 ;;
- phrases: cool breeze || 凉风 ;; sea breeze || 海风 ;; light breeze || 轻风 ;; gentle breeze || 微风 ;; breeze through || 轻松通过 ;;
- collocations: a breeze blows || 微风吹拂 ;; a warm breeze || 暖风 ;; a spring breeze || 春风 ;; breeze past sb || 轻快地从某人身边走过 ;; breeze through the exam || 轻松通过考试 ;;
- sentencePatterns: It is + adj. + breeze that blows + prep. phrase || 用于描述某处吹着某种特征的微风 ;; Sth. is a breeze for sb. || 用于表示某事对某人来说轻而易举 ;;
- spokenExpressions: It's a breeze! || 这太简单了！ ;; Breeze off! || 走开，别烦我！ ;; Just breeze in whenever you want. || 你想什么时候来就随便来。 ;;
- slang: shoot the breeze || 闲聊，扯淡 ;;
- idioms: in a breeze || 毫不费力地 ;;

### sense: n.
- translationZh: 微风，和风 ;; 轻而易举的事 ;;
- definitionZh: 轻柔的风 ;; 容易完成、不费力气的事情 ;;
- definitionEn: a gentle wind ;; something that is very easy to do ;;
- example: A soft breeze rustled the leaves on the oak tree. || 一阵柔和的微风吹得橡树的叶子沙沙作响。
- example: The final exam was a breeze for all the students who had reviewed carefully. || 对于所有认真复习过的学生来说，期末考试简直轻而易举。
- example: We sat on the balcony enjoying the cool evening breeze after dinner. || 晚饭后我们坐在阳台上享受傍晚的凉风。

### sense: v.
- translationZh: 轻盈而自信地走 ;; 轻松完成 ;;
- definitionZh: 以轻松、不在意且自信的方式移动 ;; 毫不费力地完成某件事 ;;
- definitionEn: to move somewhere in a casual and confident way ;; to complete something very easily and without much effort ;;
- example: She just breezed into the room without even knocking on the door. || 她甚至都没敲门就轻快地走进了房间。
- example: He breezed through the interview and got the job offer the same day. || 他轻松通过了面试，当天就拿到了录用通知。
- example: The athlete breezed past all his competitors and won the 100-meter race. || 这名运动员轻松超过所有对手，赢得了百米赛跑的冠军。

## word: land
- uk: /lænd/
- us: /lænd/

- antonyms: sea || 海洋 ;; air || 天空 ;; water || 水域 ;;

- spokenExpressions: back on dry land! || 终于回到陆地上了！ ;; how did you land that gig? || 你怎么拿到那个好机会的？ ;; you'll land yourself in hot water if you keep doing that. || 你再这么做会惹上麻烦的。 ;;
- idioms: see how the land lies || 摸清情况，审时度势 ;; live off the land || 靠山吃山，靠水吃水，就地取食 ;;

### sense: n. 名词

- definitionZh: 相对于海洋、水域的地球表面固态部分 ;; 可供耕种、建造或拥有所有权的地表区域 ;; 一个国家管辖范围内的地域 ;;
- definitionEn: the solid part of the earth's surface that is not covered by water ;; an area of ground that is used for a particular purpose such as farming or building ;; the territory and boundaries of a particular country ;;
- example: After two weeks at sea, we were glad to set foot on land again. || 在海上航行了两周后，我们很高兴再次踏上陆地。
- example: The local government plans to sell this piece of land to a real estate developer. || 当地政府打算把这块地卖给一家房地产开发商。
- example: He devoted his whole life to protecting the land of his motherland. || 他毕生都在为保卫祖国的领土而奋斗。

### sense: v. 动词
- translationZh: 降落；着陆 ;; 获得（工作、机会等） ;; 使陷入（困境） ;;
- definitionZh: 飞机、航天器等降落到地面或其他物体表面 ;; 成功得到一份理想的工作、合同或难得的机会 ;; 让某人处于某种不愉快或麻烦的处境中 ;;
- definitionEn: (of an aircraft, spacecraft, etc.) to come down to the ground or another surface after a flight ;; to succeed in getting a job, contract, or opportunity that other people also want ;; to cause someone to be in a difficult or unpleasant situation ;;
- example: The flight will land at Beijing Capital International Airport in half an hour. || 这趟航班将在半小时后降落在北京首都国际机场。
- example: She managed to land a well-paid job at a top international company right after graduation. || 她刚毕业就成功在一家顶尖国际公司找到了一份高薪工作。
- example: Your careless words will land you in a lot of trouble if you don't apologize immediately. || 你要是不马上道歉，你那些无心的话会给你招来很多麻烦。

## word: water
- uk: /ˈwɔːtə(r)/
- us: /ˈwɔːtər/

- antonyms: land || 陆地 ;; fire || 火 ;;

- sentencePatterns: It is + adj. + to drink water || 描述喝水的属性，it作形式主语 ;; sb + spend + 时间 + watering sth || 描述某人花费时间给某物浇水 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Hold your water! || 沉住气！别着急！ ;; pour cold water on sth || 给某事泼冷水 ;; in deep water || 陷入困境 ;;
- idioms: blood is thicker than water || 血浓于水 ;; water under the bridge || 已成往事，无法挽回的过去 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 水 ;; 雨水 ;; 海域 ;;
- definitionZh: 无色无味的透明液体，是生命之源，存在于河流、湖泊、海洋中 ;; 大片的水域，如海洋、湖泊等 ;;
- definitionEn: a clear, colourless, odourless liquid that forms the seas, lakes, rivers, and rain and is the basis of the fluids of living organisms ;; an area of sea, lake, or river, especially when considered as belonging to a particular country ;;
- example: Remember to drink plenty of water every day. || 记得每天喝足量的水。
- example: The ship sailed into international waters last night. || 这艘船昨晚驶入了国际海域。
- example: The heavy water flooded many villages in the area. || 暴雨引发的洪水淹没了该地区的许多村庄。

### sense: verb

- definitionZh: 给植物、土地等浇灌水 ;; 看到或想到食物时唾液分泌增多 ;; 眼睛因为情绪、刺激等充满泪水 ;;
- definitionEn: pour water over plants, land, etc. to help them grow ;; produce saliva in the mouth, especially when seeing or thinking about food ;; become filled with tears, usually because of emotion or irritation ;;
- example: I water the vegetables in the garden every morning. || 我每天早上给菜园里的蔬菜浇水。
- example: The smell of freshly baked bread makes my mouth water. || 新鲜出炉的面包的香味让我流口水。
- example: Her eyes watered when she heard the sad news. || 听到这个悲伤的消息时，她的眼里充满了泪水。

## word: airstrip
- uk: /ˈeəstrɪp/
- us: /ˈerstrɪp/

- antonyms: helipad || 直升机停机坪 ;; seaplane base || 水上飞机基地 ;;
- phrases: emergency airstrip || 应急简易跑道 ;; unpaved airstrip || 未铺砌简易跑道 ;; remote airstrip || 偏远简易机场 ;; military airstrip || 军用简易跑道 ;;
- collocations: build an airstrip || 修建简易跑道 ;; land on an airstrip || 在简易跑道上降落 ;; extend an airstrip || 延长简易跑道 ;; operate an airstrip || 运营简易机场 ;;
- sentencePatterns: [Subject] + [verb] + airstrip + [prepositional phrase] || 用于描述主体对简易跑道执行的动作及相关场景 ;; There + be + [adjective] + airstrip + [location adverbial] || 用于说明某处存在某种类型的简易跑道 ;;
- spokenExpressions: The airstrip's too short for large planes. || 这条简易跑道太短了，大型飞机降不了。 ;; We'll touch down at the remote airstrip in 20 minutes. || 我们20分钟后会在那个偏远的简易跑道着陆。 ;; The storm damaged the local airstrip. || 暴风雨损坏了当地的简易跑道。 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 简易跑道 ;; 简易机场 ;;
- definitionZh: 通常较为短小、设施简单的飞机起降跑道，多建在偏远地区或作为应急起降使用 ;; 供小型飞机临时或固定起降的小型场地，配套设施较为简陋 ;;
- definitionEn: A short, simple runway for aircraft to take off and land on, often built in remote areas or for emergency use. ;; A small area with basic facilities for small aircraft to operate from, usually with limited supporting infrastructure. ;;
- example: The aid team built a temporary airstrip in the mountainous region to deliver medical supplies. || 救援队伍在山区修建了一条临时简易跑道，用来运送医疗物资。
- example: The small cargo plane managed to land safely on the narrow dirt airstrip despite the strong wind. || 尽管风力很大，这架小型货运飞机还是成功在狭窄的土质简易跑道上安全着陆。
- example: The remote village only has access to outside world via the small airstrip that was completed three years ago. || 这个偏远村庄只能通过三年前建成的小型简易机场和外界取得联系。

## word: alive

- sentencePatterns: be + alive + to + noun || 表示对某事物有所察觉/敏感 ;; be + alive + with + noun || 表示某处充满某事物、挤满某群体 ;; keep + sb/sth + alive || 表示让某人存活、使某事物留存 ;;

- idioms: alive and kicking || 活蹦乱跳的，健在的 ;; bring sth alive || 使某物变得生动有趣 ;;

- definitionEn: still living and not dead ;; full of energy, enthusiasm, or excitement ;; aware of and able to understand something ;; full of people or things that are moving and active ;;
- example: We don't know if he's alive or dead after the mountain accident. || 山难发生后我们不知道他是死是活。
- example: The party really came alive when the live band started playing. || 现场乐队开始演奏后，派对一下子就热闹起来了。
- example: As a journalist, you need to be alive to the latest social trends. || 作为记者，你需要对最新的社会趋势保持敏感。
- example: The downtown street is alive with tourists every weekend. || 每个周末市中心的街道上都挤满了游客，热闹非凡。



## word: animate
- uk: /ˈænɪmeɪt/
- us: /ˈænɪmeɪt/
- synonyms: enliven || 使活跃，使有生气 ;; vivify || 使生动，赋予生命 ;; energize || 使充满活力，激励 ;; liven || 使快活，使热闹 ;;
- antonyms: deaden || 使麻木，使失去活力 ;; dull || 使迟钝，使黯淡 ;; suppress || 抑制，压抑 ;;
- phrases: animate object || 有生命物体 ;; animate cartoon || 动画卡通 ;; animate nature || 生物界 ;; animate drawing || 动画绘制 ;;
- collocations: animate a crowd || 鼓动人群 ;; animate a story || 让故事生动 ;; animate a character || 赋予角色生命 ;; animate a discussion || 活跃讨论气氛 ;;
- sentencePatterns: animate sth || 及物动词用法，后接被赋予活力/生命的对象 ;; be animated by sth || 被动结构，表"被某事物驱动/激励" ;;
- spokenExpressions: Animate it up a bit! || 让它更有活力点！ ;; That really animated the room. || 那一下子就让整个场子热起来了。 ;;
- idioms: animate the dead || 起死回生，做看似不可能的事 ;;

### sense: verb
- translationZh: 使有生气，使活跃 ;; 把……制作成动画 ;; 赋予……生命 ;; 激励，鼓动 ;;
- definitionZh: 给某事物注入活力、趣味或生命力，使其更生动；将静态内容制作成动态动画形式；驱动、鼓励他人采取行动 ;; 赋予非生命事物拟人的生命特征 ;;
- definitionEn: To give life, action, or energy to something to make it more lively or interesting; to create a film, cartoon, etc. by making drawings, models, etc. seem to move; to encourage or drive someone to do something. ;; To endow inanimate things with life-like characteristics.
- example: The smile on her face animated the whole room. || 她脸上的笑容让整个房间都充满了生气。
- example: The studio spent two years animating the main characters of the fantasy film. || 这家工作室花了两年时间为这部奇幻电影的主角制作动画效果。
- example: The inspiring speech animated the volunteers to take immediate action for the community project. || 这场鼓舞人心的演讲激励志愿者们立刻为社区项目采取行动。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 有生命的 ;; 有活力的，生气勃勃的 ;;
- definitionZh: 具有生命特征的，区别于无生命物体；形容人或氛围充满活力、积极鲜活的状态 ;;
- definitionEn: Living, having the characteristics of life; full of energy and vitality, active and lively.
- example: Children are usually more interested in animate creatures like puppies and kittens than in static toys. || 比起静态玩具，孩子们通常对小狗小猫这类有生命的生物更感兴趣。
- example: The animate conversation at the dinner party lasted until midnight. || 晚宴上轻松活跃的交谈一直持续到了午夜。
- example: In this mythology tale, even inanimate stones can become animate and talk under the magic spell. || 在这个神话故事里，哪怕是无生命的石头在咒语作用下也能变得有生命还能说话。

## word: breathing
- uk: /ˈbriːðɪŋ/
- us: /ˈbriːðɪŋ/
- synonyms: respiration || 呼吸 ;; inhalation || 吸气 ;; exhalation || 呼气 ;; ventilation || 通气，呼吸 ;;
- antonyms: breathlessness || 呼吸困难，气促 ;; apnea || 呼吸暂停 ;;
- phrases: deep breathing || 深呼吸 ;; mouth breathing || 口呼吸 ;; breathing exercise || 呼吸练习 ;; breathing rate || 呼吸频率 ;;
- collocations: slow breathing || 缓慢呼吸 ;; shallow breathing || 浅呼吸 ;; labored breathing || 费力呼吸 ;; regular breathing || 规律呼吸 ;;
- sentencePatterns: Sb's breathing becomes + adj || 描述某人的呼吸状态变化 ;; Doing sth helps improve + one's breathing || 描述某行为对呼吸的改善作用 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Take a minute to steady your breathing. || 花点时间平稳你的呼吸。 ;; Your breathing's a bit ragged, slow down. || 你呼吸有点乱，慢一点。 ;; Just focus on your breathing, everything will be okay. || 专心调整呼吸，一切都会好的。 ;;
- idioms: breathing room || 喘息空间，活动余地 ;; a breathing space || 短暂的休整机会 ;;

### sense: noun
- translationZh: 呼吸；呼吸作用；呼吸气息 ;;
- definitionZh: 生物体吸入和呼出空气的生理过程；呼吸时进出的气息；植物或细胞的气体交换过程 ;;
- definitionEn: The physiological process of taking air into the lungs and expelling it from the body; the air that is inhaled and exhaled during respiration; the gas exchange process of plants or cells. ;;
- example: Her breathing became slow and regular as she fell asleep. || 她睡着后呼吸变得缓慢而规律。
- example: The doctor checked the patient's breathing and pulse immediately. || 医生立刻检查了病人的呼吸和脉搏。
- example: You can feel the cold air on your face with each breathing in winter. || 冬天每次呼吸时你都能感受到脸上的冷空气。

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 呼吸的；活的，有生命的 ;;
- definitionZh: 与呼吸相关的；还活着的、有呼吸的 ;;
- definitionEn: Relating to the process of respiration; alive and having the ability to breathe. ;;
- example: The breathing apparatus can help workers stay safe in toxic environments. || 呼吸装置可以帮助工人在有毒环境中保障安全。
- example: He's the breathing embodiment of the traditional craftsman spirit. || 他是传统工匠精神的鲜活化身。
- example: The breathing mask is essential for people with severe allergies during pollen season. || 花粉季时呼吸面罩对严重过敏的人来说必不可少。

## word: dead
- uk: /ded/
- us: /ded/
- synonyms: deceased || 已故的 ;; lifeless || 无生命的 ;; extinct || 灭绝的 ;; inert || 惰性的、无活力的 ;; stagnant || 停滞的 ;;
- antonyms: alive || 活着的 ;; living || 活的 ;; lively || 活泼的 ;;
- phrases: dead end || 死胡同、绝境 ;; dead time || 停滞期、无效时间 ;; dead heat || 势均力敌的比赛、并列第一 ;; dead silence || 死寂 ;; dead weight || 重负、静载荷 ;;
- collocations: dead body || 尸体 ;; dead tired || 累极了的 ;; dead stop || 完全停止 ;; dead language || 死语言（不再有人日常使用的语言） ;; dead loss || 完全无用的人/物、净损失 ;;
- sentencePatterns: be + dead + from/of + 原因 || 表示死于某种原因 ;; be + dead + to + 名词 || 表示对某事物无动于衷、不受某事物影响 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Over my dead body! || 休想！除非我死了！ ;; You look dead beat. || 你看起来累垮了。 ;; Drop dead! || 去死吧！（愤怒的呵斥） ;;
- slang: dead ringer || 长得一模一样的人 ;; dead cash || 闲置资金、不动用的现金 ;;
- idioms: dead to the world || 睡得极熟、不省人事 ;; beat a dead horse || 白费口舌、做无用功 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 死的，去世的 ;; 无生命的，停滞的 ;; 完全的，绝对的 ;; 无活力的，沉闷的 ;;
- definitionZh: 已经停止生命活动的；不再活着的 ;; 缺乏活力、运动或生命力的；没有生机的 ;; 用于强调程度，完全的、彻底的 ;; 没有任何声响、动静或反应的 ;;
- definitionEn: No longer alive; having ceased to live. ;; Lacking vitality, movement, or active properties; not operating or functioning. ;; Used for emphasis, meaning complete or absolute. ;; Without any sound, movement, or reaction. ;;
- example: Her grandmother has been dead for ten years. || 她的祖母已经去世十年了。
- example: The town center is completely dead after 9 p.m. || 晚上9点之后市中心就完全没了生气。
- example: There was dead silence in the room when he announced the bad news. || 他宣布这个坏消息的时候，房间里一片死寂。

### sense: adverb
- translationZh: 完全地，绝对地 ;; 直接地，正好地 ;;
- definitionZh: 用于强调程度，完全、彻底 ;; 表示位置准确，正好、正对 ;;
- definitionEn: Used to emphasize that something is completely the case. ;; Exactly or directly in a particular position. ;;
- example: I'm dead certain that he was the one who stole the wallet. || 我百分百确定就是他偷了钱包。
- example: The arrow landed dead in the center of the target. || 箭正好射中了靶心。
- example: You're dead right about this project needing more funding. || 关于这个项目需要更多资金这件事，你说得完全正确。

## word: lifeless
- uk: /ˈlaɪfləs/
- us: /ˈlaɪfləs/
- synonyms: inanimate || 无生命的 ;; dull || 沉闷的 ;; sluggish || 呆滞的 ;; lifelessness || 无生气（名词形式，近义状态） ;; dead || 死的 ;;
- antonyms: alive || 活着的 ;; vibrant || 充满活力的 ;; lively || 活泼的 ;;
- phrases: lifeless body || 尸体 ;; lifeless performance || 沉闷的表演 ;; lifeless landscape || 荒凉的景观 ;; lifeless hair || 无光泽的头发 ;;
- collocations: completely lifeless || 完全没有生气的 ;; look lifeless || 看起来死气沉沉的 ;; feel lifeless || 感觉毫无活力 ;; lifeless planet || 无生命的星球 ;;
- sentencePatterns: sb/sth seems lifeless || 某人/某物看起来毫无生气，描述直观感受 ;; It is lifeless to do sth || 做某事很乏味，表述行为的枯燥感 ;; The + n. + remains lifeless || 某事物仍然没有生机，描述持续的无生气状态 ;;
- spokenExpressions: This place feels so lifeless! || 这地方太死气沉沉了！ ;; The meeting was totally lifeless. || 这场会议完全没意思。 ;; My phone's lifeless, can I borrow yours? || 我手机没电了，能借你的用下吗？ ;;
- idioms: a lifeless duck || 彻底失败的项目/没价值的事物 ;;

### sense: adjective
- translationZh: 无生命的 ;; 死气沉沉的，无活力的 ;; 无趣味的，枯燥的 ;; （物体）无光泽的，死板的 ;;
- definitionZh: 没有生命体征的，不属于活物的 ;; 缺乏活力、热情或趣味的，沉闷乏味的 ;; 外观上缺乏生气或光泽的 ;;
- definitionEn: not having or showing any signs of life ;; lacking energy, interest, or excitement ;; not bright or interesting in appearance ;;
- example: The astronomers believe that the distant planet is completely lifeless. || 天文学家认为那颗遥远的星球完全没有生命存在。
- example: His lifeless speech made half the audience fall asleep. || 他枯燥的演讲让一半听众都睡着了。
- example: After working 12 hours straight, she felt completely lifeless when she got home. || 连续工作12个小时后，她回到家时感觉一点力气都没有了。
- example: The old castle looked cold and lifeless in the winter rain. || 那座古老的城堡在冬雨中看起来冰冷又毫无生气。

## word: living
- uk: /ˈlɪvɪŋ/
- us: /ˈlɪvɪŋ/
- synonyms: alive || 活着的 ;; dwelling || 住处 ;; livelihood || 生计 ;; existing || 现存的 ;; residence || 居所 ;;
- antonyms: dead || 死的 ;; extinct || 灭绝的 ;; deceased || 已故的 ;;
- phrases: living room || 客厅 ;; standard of living || 生活水平 ;; living cost || 生活成本 ;; living creature || 生物 ;; living condition || 居住条件 ;;
- collocations: make a living || 谋生 ;; living environment || 居住环境 ;; daily living || 日常生活 ;; living space || 生存空间 ;; living wage || 最低生活工资 ;;
- sentencePatterns: make a living by doing sth || 表示通过做某事谋生的句型 ;; It is + adj. + for living creatures to do sth || 表示生物做某事具有某种属性的形式主语句型 ;;
- spokenExpressions: Earn a living, huh? || 混口饭吃呗，是吧？ ;; What do you do for a living? || 你是做什么工作的？ ;; Living the dream! || 过得太如意了！ ;;
- idioms: the living daylights out of sb || 把某人吓得魂飞魄散 ;;

### sense: 形容词
- translationZh: 活着的；活的 ;; 现存的；在使用的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指有生命的、尚未死亡的 ;; 指当前仍然存在、仍在使用或运行的 ;;
- definitionEn: still alive and not dead ;; currently existing or in use ;;
- example: The living are more important to us than the dead. || 对我们来说，活着的人比逝去的人更重要。
- example: This is the oldest living custom in the local area. || 这是当地现存最古老的习俗。
- example: No living person has ever seen that rare wild animal. || 没有哪个活着的人见过那种珍稀的野生动物。

### sense: 名词
- translationZh: 生计；收入 ;; 生活方式 ;;
- definitionZh: 用来维持生活的收入或谋生的手段 ;; 指人们日常的生活状态和方式 ;;
- definitionEn: the money that you earn to pay for food, housing, etc. ;; the way in which you live your daily life ;;
- example: He makes a living by selling handmade crafts on the street. || 他靠在街上售卖手工制品谋生。
- example: Many young people are struggling to improve their quality of living in big cities. || 很多年轻人都在大城市里努力提升自己的生活质量。
- example: The rise in prices has had a huge impact on the living of low-income families. || 物价上涨对低收入家庭的生计造成了巨大影响。

## word: all
- uk: /ɔːl/
- us: /ɔːl/
- synonyms: entire || 全部的，整个的 ;; whole || 完整的，全部的 ;; total || 总的，全部的 ;; every || 每个的，所有的 ;; complete || 完全的，全部的 ;;
- antonyms: partial || 部分的，不完全的 ;; some || 一些，部分 ;; none || 没有一个，毫无 ;;
- phrases: all over || 到处，遍及 ;; all right || 好的，没问题 ;; all in all || 总而言之，总的来说 ;; all the time || 一直，始终 ;; all of a sudden || 突然，忽然 ;;
- collocations: all day || 一整天 ;; all people || 所有人 ;; all the way || 一路上，自始至终 ;; all the best || 一切顺利，万事如意 ;; all kinds of || 各种各样的 ;;
- sentencePatterns: All of + 名词/代词 + 谓语 || 表示“所有的……都……”，指代特定范围内的全部对象 ;; Not all + 名词 + 谓语 || 表示部分否定，意为“并非所有的……都……” ;; All + 从句 + be + 表语 || 表示“……的全部就是……”，强调内容的唯一性 ;;
- spokenExpressions: All right? || 你还好吗？/没问题吧？ ;; That's all. || 就这些，说完了。 ;; All the best! || 祝一切顺利！ ;;
- idioms: all ears || 洗耳恭听 ;; all eyes || 目不转睛，全神贯注地看 ;; all in || 筋疲力尽的 ;;

### sense: 形容词
- translationZh: 全部的，所有的 ;; 整个的，全部的 ;;
- definitionZh: 指涵盖某一范围内的每一个个体，没有遗漏 ;; 指完整的、未被分割的整体 ;;
- definitionEn: including every person or thing in a particular group, with no exceptions ;; referring to a whole or complete amount, period, or thing, not divided ;;
- example: All students need to hand in their homework before Friday. || 所有学生都需要在周五之前上交作业。
- example: We spent all day cleaning the house. || 我们花了一整天打扫房子。
- example: All the bread has gone stale. || 所有的面包都不新鲜了。

### sense: 代词
- translationZh: 所有，全部 ;; 一切，所有事物 ;;
- definitionZh: 指代某一范围内的全部人、事物或数量 ;; 指代所有的情况、事物等整体概念 ;;
- definitionEn: the whole number or amount of people or things in a group ;; everything that is involved in a particular situation ;;
- example: All of us are going to the picnic this weekend. || 我们所有人这周末都要去野餐。
- example: All I want is a cup of hot tea. || 我想要的一切就是一杯热茶。
- example: She gave all she had to help the poor children. || 她倾尽所有来帮助那些贫困儿童。

### sense: 副词
- translationZh: 完全地，全部地 ;; （表示程度）很，非常 ;;
- definitionZh: 表示完全、彻底的程度，没有剩余 ;; 用于强调状态或程度之深 ;;
- definitionEn: completely or entirely, with no part left ;; used to emphasize how strong a feeling or quality is ;;
- example: The cake was all eaten by the kids. || 蛋糕完全被孩子们吃光了。
- example: I'm all confused about the new rules. || 我完全搞不懂这些新规则。
- example: She was all excited when she received the admission letter. || 她收到录取通知书的时候非常兴奋。
